п»ҝ// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\config\DatabaseConfig.java ==========
package com.auction.config;

import com.zaxxer.hikari.HikariConfig;
import com.zaxxer.hikari.HikariDataSource;
import io.zonky.test.db.postgres.embedded.EmbeddedPostgres;
import java.io.File;
import java.sql.Connection;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.sql.Statement;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.Jdbi;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * KhГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo vГғВ  quГЎВәВЈn lГғВҪ kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi database (Singleton, thread-safe).
 *
 * <p>Logic chГЎВ»ВҚn database:
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>NГЎВәВҝu biГЎВәВҝn mГғВҙi trГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng {@code DB_URL} Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc set ГўвҖ вҖҷ kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi PostgreSQL ngoГғВ i.
 *   <li>NГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng cГғВі {@code DB_URL} ГўвҖ вҖҷ tГЎВ»Вұ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng khГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng Embedded PostgreSQL bГғВӘn trong JVM.
 * </ul>
 *
 * <p>NhГЎВ»Вқ Г„вҖҳГғВі ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ chГЎВәВЎy {@code java -jar auction.jar} mГғВ  khГғВҙng cГЎВәВ§n cГғВ i PostgreSQL.
 */
public class DatabaseConfig {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(DatabaseConfig.class);

  // Singleton instances
  private static volatile Jdbi jdbi;
  private static HikariDataSource dataSource;

  // GiГЎВ»ВҜ tham chiГЎВәВҝu Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ Г„вҖҳГғВіng khi shutdown
  private static EmbeddedPostgres embeddedPostgres;

  // TГғВӘn database dГғВ№ng cho embedded mode
  private static final String EMBEDDED_DB_NAME = "auction_db";

  // ThГҶВ° mГЎВ»ВҘc lГҶВ°u data PostgreSQL cГЎВ»вҖҳ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖ№nh ГўвӮ¬вҖқ data Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc giГЎВ»ВҜ lГЎВәВЎi giГЎВ»ВҜa cГғВЎc lГЎВәВ§n chГЎВәВЎy
  private static final File EMBEDDED_DATA_DIR = new File("data/postgres");

  /**
   * KhГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo hoГЎВәВ·c trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ Jdbi instance duy nhГЎВәВҘt (thread-safe, double-checked locking).
   *
   * @return Jdbi instance Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc cГЎВәВҘu hГғВ¬nh
   */
  public static Jdbi create() {
    if (jdbi == null) {
      synchronized (DatabaseConfig.class) {
        if (jdbi == null) {
          String dbUrl = System.getenv("DB_URL");

          if (dbUrl != null && !dbUrl.isBlank()) {
            // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ TrГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng hГЎВ»ВЈp 1: DГғВ№ng PostgreSQL ngoГғВ i ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
            initExternalPostgres(dbUrl);
          } else {
            // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ TrГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng hГЎВ»ВЈp 2: TГЎВ»Вұ khГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng Embedded PostgreSQL ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
            initEmbeddedPostgres();
          }
        }
      }
    }
    return jdbi;
  }

  /** KГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi tГЎВ»вҖәi PostgreSQL ngoГғВ i qua biГЎВәВҝn mГғВҙi trГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng DB_URL, DB_USER, DB_PASSWORD. */
  private static void initExternalPostgres(String dbUrl) {
    String dbUser = getEnvOrDefault("DB_USER", "postgres");
    String dbPass = getEnvOrDefault("DB_PASSWORD", "auction_pass");

    LOGGER.info("Г°ЕёвҖқвҖ” KГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi PostgreSQL ngoГғВ i: {}", dbUrl);

    HikariConfig config = buildHikariConfig(dbUrl, dbUser, dbPass);

    try {
      dataSource = new HikariDataSource(config);
      jdbi = Jdbi.create(dataSource);
      LOGGER.info("ГўЕ“вҖҰ KГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi PostgreSQL ngoГғВ i thГғВ nh cГғВҙng");
    } catch (Exception e) {
      LOGGER.error("ГўВқЕ’ KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi PostgreSQL ngoГғВ i: {}", e.getMessage());
      throw new RuntimeException("Could not connect to external database", e);
    }
  }

  /**
   * KhГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng Embedded PostgreSQL bГғВӘn trong JVM. LГЎВәВ§n Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§u chГЎВәВЎy sГЎВәВҪ tГЎВәВЈi binary PostgreSQL phГғВ№ hГЎВ»ВЈp vГЎВ»вҖәi
   * OS (~15MB, tГЎВ»Вұ cache lГЎВәВЎi). CГғВЎc lГЎВәВ§n sau khГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng ngay lГЎВәВӯp tГЎВ»В©c.
   *
   * <p>Data Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc lГҶВ°u cГЎВ»вҖҳ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖ№nh tГЎВәВЎi {@code data/postgres/} trong thГҶВ° mГЎВ»ВҘc chГЎВәВЎy ГЎВ»В©ng dГЎВ»ВҘng, Г„вҖҳГЎВәВЈm bГЎВәВЈo khГғВҙng
   * bГЎВ»вҖ№ reset giГЎВ»ВҜa cГғВЎc lГЎВәВ§n chГЎВәВЎy.
   */
  private static void initEmbeddedPostgres() {
    LOGGER.info("Г°ЕёЕЎвӮ¬ KhГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy DB_URL ГўвӮ¬вҖқ khГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng Embedded PostgreSQL...");
    LOGGER.info("   (LГЎВәВ§n Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§u chГЎВәВЎy cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ mГЎВәВҘt 10-30 giГғВўy Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ tГЎВәВЈi PostgreSQL binary)");
    LOGGER.info("   Data directory: {}", EMBEDDED_DATA_DIR.getAbsolutePath());

    try {
      // TГЎВәВЎo thГҶВ° mГЎВ»ВҘc nГЎВәВҝu chГҶВ°a tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi
      if (!EMBEDDED_DATA_DIR.exists()) {
        EMBEDDED_DATA_DIR.mkdirs();
        LOGGER.info("Г°ЕёвҖңВҒ Г„ВҗГғВЈ tГЎВәВЎo data directory: {}", EMBEDDED_DATA_DIR.getAbsolutePath());
      }

      // XГғВіa postmaster.pid nГЎВәВҝu cГғВІn sГғВіt tГЎВ»В« lГЎВәВ§n chГЎВәВЎy trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc bГЎВ»вҖ№ crash
      File pidFile = new File(EMBEDDED_DATA_DIR, "postmaster.pid");
      if (pidFile.exists()) {
        pidFile.delete();
        LOGGER.warn("ГўЕЎВ ГҜВёВҸ  Г„ВҗГғВЈ xГғВіa postmaster.pid cГғВІn sГғВіt tГЎВ»В« lГЎВәВ§n chГЎВәВЎy trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc");
      }

      embeddedPostgres = EmbeddedPostgres.builder().setDataDirectory(EMBEDDED_DATA_DIR).start();

      int port = embeddedPostgres.getPort();

      // Embedded PostgreSQL mГЎВәВ·c Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖ№nh: user=postgres, password=""
      String dbUser = "postgres";
      String dbPass = "";

      LOGGER.info("ГўЕ“вҖҰ Embedded PostgreSQL Г„вҖҳГғВЈ khГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng tГЎВәВЎi port {}", port);

      // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ TГЎВәВЎo database auction_db nГЎВәВҝu chГҶВ°a tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
      // PhГЎВәВЈi connect vГғВ o DB mГЎВәВ·c Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖ№nh "postgres" trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc, khГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ connect thГЎВәВіng vГғВ o auction_db
      try (Connection conn = embeddedPostgres.getPostgresDatabase().getConnection();
          Statement stmt = conn.createStatement()) {
        ResultSet rs =
            stmt.executeQuery(
                "SELECT 1 FROM pg_database WHERE datname = '" + EMBEDDED_DB_NAME + "'");
        if (!rs.next()) {
          stmt.execute("CREATE DATABASE " + EMBEDDED_DB_NAME);
          LOGGER.info("ГўЕ“вҖҰ Г„ВҗГғВЈ tГЎВәВЎo database '{}'", EMBEDDED_DB_NAME);
        } else {
          LOGGER.info("ГўвҖһВ№ГҜВёВҸ  Database '{}' Г„вҖҳГғВЈ tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi, bГЎВ»ВҸ qua bГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc tГЎВәВЎo", EMBEDDED_DB_NAME);
        }
      }

      String dbUrl = String.format("jdbc:postgresql://localhost:%d/%s", port, EMBEDDED_DB_NAME);
      HikariConfig config = buildHikariConfig(dbUrl, dbUser, dbPass);

      dataSource = new HikariDataSource(config);
      jdbi = Jdbi.create(dataSource);

      LOGGER.info("ГўЕ“вҖҰ KГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi Embedded PostgreSQL thГғВ nh cГғВҙng");

    } catch (Exception e) {
      LOGGER.error("ГўВқЕ’ KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ khГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng Embedded PostgreSQL: {}", e.getMessage());
      throw new RuntimeException("Could not start embedded database", e);
    }
  }

  /** TГЎВәВЎo HikariConfig vГЎВ»вҖәi cГғВЎc thГғВҙng sГЎВ»вҖҳ chung. */
  private static HikariConfig buildHikariConfig(String url, String user, String pass) {
    HikariConfig config = new HikariConfig();
    config.setJdbcUrl(url);
    config.setUsername(user);
    config.setPassword(pass);
    config.setMaximumPoolSize(10);
    config.setMinimumIdle(5);
    config.setConnectionTimeout(30000);
    config.setPoolName("Auction-Jdbi-Pool");
    config.addDataSourceProperty("currentSchema", "public");
    return config;
  }

  /** Г„ВҗГғВіng toГғВ n bГЎВ»в„ў connection pool vГғВ  embedded PostgreSQL (nГЎВәВҝu cГғВі). GГЎВ»ВҚi khi server tГЎВәВҜt. */
  public static void shutDown() {
    if (dataSource != null && !dataSource.isClosed()) {
      dataSource.close();
      jdbi = null;
      dataSource = null;
      LOGGER.info("Г°ЕёвҖқЕ’ Database connection pool Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГғВіng.");
    }

    if (embeddedPostgres != null) {
      try {
        embeddedPostgres.close();
        embeddedPostgres = null;
        LOGGER.info("Г°ЕёвҖқЕ’ Embedded PostgreSQL Г„вҖҳГғВЈ tГЎВәВҜt.");
      } catch (Exception e) {
        LOGGER.warn("LГЎВ»вҖ”i khi tГЎВәВҜt Embedded PostgreSQL: {}", e.getMessage());
      }
    }
  }

  private static String getEnvOrDefault(String key, String defaultValue) {
    String value = System.getenv(key);
    return (value != null && !value.isEmpty()) ? value : defaultValue;
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\config\JwtUtil.java ==========
package com.auction.config;

import com.auth0.jwt.JWT;
import com.auth0.jwt.algorithms.Algorithm;
import com.auth0.jwt.interfaces.DecodedJWT;
import com.auth0.jwt.interfaces.JWTVerifier;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.time.temporal.ChronoUnit;

public class JwtUtil {

  private static final String SECRET_KEY;

  static {
    String envSecret = System.getenv("JWT_SECRET");
    SECRET_KEY = (envSecret != null && !envSecret.isBlank()) ? envSecret : "auction-secret-key-dev";
  }

  private static final Algorithm ALGORITHM =
      Algorithm.HMAC256(
          SECRET_KEY); // Г„ВҗГғВўy lГғВ  thuГЎВәВӯt toГғВЎn mГғВЈ hГғВіa Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖҳi xГЎВ»В©ng. NghГ„В©a lГғВ  hГЎВ»вҖЎ thГЎВ»вҖҳng dГғВ№ng chung 1 cГғВЎi
  // SECRET_KEY vГЎВ»В«a Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ khГғВіa (tГЎВәВЎo token) vГЎВ»В«a Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ mГЎВ»Её khГғВіa (xГғВЎc minh token).

  private static final JWTVerifier VERIFIER =
      JWT.require(ALGORITHM)
          .build(); // Г„ВҗГғВўy lГғВ  cГғВЎi "MГғВЎy quГғВ©t thГЎВәВ»". ThГЎВәВ§y Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ nГғВі lГғВ  static final (biГЎВәВҝn tГ„В©nh hГЎВәВұng sГЎВ»вҖҳ) Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’

  // mГғВЎy tГғВӯnh chГЎВ»вҖ° khГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo nГғВі Г„вҖҳГғВәng 1 lГЎВәВ§n duy nhГЎВәВҘt khi chГЎВәВЎy server, giГғВәp tiГЎВәВҝt kiГЎВ»вҖЎm
  // bГЎВ»в„ў nhГЎВ»вҖә vГғВ  tГ„Ж’ng tГЎВ»вҖҳc Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ў xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ khi cГғВі hГғВ ng nghГғВ¬n ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng cГғВ№ng truy cГЎВәВӯp.

  public static String createToken(Long userId, String username, String role) {
    return JWT.create()
        .withClaim("userId", userId)
        .withClaim("username", username)
        .withClaim("role", role)
        .withExpiresAt(Instant.now().plus(24, ChronoUnit.HOURS))
        .sign(ALGORITHM);
  }

  public static DecodedJWT verifyToken(String token) {
    // HГғВ m nГғВ y sГЎВәВҪ tГЎВ»Вұ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng quГ„Ж’ng lГЎВ»вҖ”i cГЎВ»В§a thГҶВ° viГЎВ»вҖЎn JWT nГЎВәВҝu token hГЎВәВҝt hГЎВәВЎn hoГЎВәВ·c sai chГЎВ»ВҜ kГғВҪ
    return VERIFIER.verify(token);
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\controller\AuctionController.java ==========
package com.auction.controller;

import com.auction.dto.AuctionResponse;
import com.auction.dto.CreateAuctionRequest;
import com.auction.exception.UnauthorizedException;
import com.auction.model.Auction;
import com.auction.service.AuctionService;
import io.javalin.Javalin;
import io.javalin.http.Context;
import java.util.List;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * Controller xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ toГғВ n bГЎВ»в„ў thao tГғВЎc CRUD cho tГғВ i nguyГғВӘn Auction (phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ).
 *
 * <p>Danh sГғВЎch endpoints vГғВ  quyГЎВ»ВҒn truy cГЎВәВӯp:
 *
 * <pre>
 *   GET    /api/auctions           ГўвҖ вҖҷ MГЎВ»ВҚi user Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp (filter ?status=RUNNING)
 *   GET    /api/auctions/:id       ГўвҖ вҖҷ MГЎВ»ВҚi user Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp (trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ AuctionResponse Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§y Г„вҖҳГЎВ»В§)
 *   POST   /api/auctions           ГўвҖ вҖҷ ChГЎВ»вҖ° SELLER
 *   PUT    /api/auctions/:id       ГўвҖ вҖҷ ChГЎВ»вҖ° SELLER sГЎВ»Её hГЎВ»ВҜu phiГғВӘn, chГЎВ»вҖ° khi status=OPEN
 *   DELETE /api/auctions/:id       ГўвҖ вҖҷ SELLER sГЎВ»Её hГЎВ»ВҜu phiГғВӘn hoГЎВәВ·c ADMIN
 * </pre>
 *
 * <p>TГғВӯch hГЎВ»ВЈp State Pattern:
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>{@code PUT} (sГЎВ»Вӯa phiГғВӘn) ГўвҖ вҖҷ service gГЎВ»ВҚi {@code state.edit()} ГўвҖ вҖҷ {@code OpenState} cho phГғВ©p,
 *       {@code RunningState}/{@code FinishedState} nГғВ©m {@code AuctionClosedException}.
 *   <li>{@code POST} bid (trong {@link BidController}) ГўвҖ вҖҷ service gГЎВ»ВҚi {@code state.placeBid()} ГўвҖ вҖҷ chГЎВ»вҖ°
 *       {@code RunningState} cho phГғВ©p.
 * </ul>
 *
 * <p>KhГғВЎc biГЎВ»вҖЎt vГЎВ»вҖәi {@link ItemController}: endpoint {@code GET /api/auctions/:id} trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ {@link
 * AuctionResponse} (enriched object) thay vГғВ¬ {@link com.auction.model.Auction} raw, bao gГЎВ»вҖңm thГғВӘm:
 * {@code itemName}, {@code leadingBidderUsername}, {@code remainingTimeMs}.
 *
 * @see com.auction.service.AuctionService
 * @see com.auction.pattern.state.AuctionState
 * @see BidController
 */
public class AuctionController {

  /** Logger ghi lГЎВәВЎi cГғВЎc thao tГғВЎc CRUD trГғВӘn phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ */
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(AuctionController.class);

  /** HГғВ m khГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo private ГўвӮ¬вҖқ lГЎВ»вҖәp nГғВ y chГЎВ»вҖ° dГғВ№ng static methods, khГғВҙng cГЎВәВ§n instance. */
  private AuctionController() {}

  /**
   * Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ route cГЎВ»В§a AuctionController vГғВ o Javalin instance.
   *
   * @param app Javalin instance Г„вҖҳang chГЎВәВЎy
   * @param auctionService service xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ logic nghiГЎВ»вҖЎp vГЎВ»ВҘ cho phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   */
  public static void register(Javalin app, AuctionService auctionService) {
    app.get("/api/auctions", ctx -> handleGetAll(ctx, auctionService));
    app.get("/api/auctions/{id}", ctx -> handleGetById(ctx, auctionService));
    app.post("/api/auctions", ctx -> handleCreate(ctx, auctionService));
    app.put("/api/auctions/{id}", ctx -> handleUpdate(ctx, auctionService));
    app.delete("/api/auctions/{id}", ctx -> handleDelete(ctx, auctionService));

    LOGGER.info(
        "Г„ВҗГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ AuctionController: GET/POST /api/auctions, "
            + "GET/PUT/DELETE /api/auctions/:id");
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy danh sГғВЎch tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ, cГғВі hГЎВ»вҖ” trГЎВ»ВЈ lГЎВ»ВҚc theo trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi.
   *
   * <p>Query parameter tГғВ№y chГЎВ»ВҚn:
   *
   * <ul>
   *   <li>{@code ?status=RUNNING} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ chГЎВ»вҖ° lГЎВәВҘy phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳang diГЎВ»вҖҰn ra.
   *   <li>{@code ?status=OPEN} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ chГЎВ»вҖ° lГЎВәВҘy phiГғВӘn sГЎВәВҜp mГЎВ»Её.
   *   <li>{@code ?status=FINISHED} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ chГЎВ»вҖ° lГЎВәВҘy phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГғВЈ kГЎВәВҝt thГғВәc.
   *   <li>KhГғВҙng cГғВі parameter ГўвҖ вҖҷ trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ TГЎВәВӨT CГЎВәВў phiГғВӘn (trГЎВ»В« CANCELED vГғВ  PAID nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng phГЎВәВЈi ADMIN).
   * </ul>
   *
   * <p>VГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ response (mГЎВәВЈng {@link AuctionResponse}):
   *
   * <pre>
   *   [
   *     {
   *       "id": 1,
   *       "itemName": "iPhone 15 Pro",
   *       "currentPrice": 15000000,
   *       "status": "RUNNING",
   *       "remainingTimeMs": 1800000,
   *       "leadingBidderUsername": "alice"
   *     }
   *   ]
   * </pre>
   *
   * @param ctx Javalin context chГЎВ»В©a HTTP request/response
   * @param auctionService service truy vГЎВәВҘn danh sГғВЎch phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   */
  private static void handleGetAll(Context ctx, AuctionService auctionService) {
    // LГЎВәВҘy query param lГЎВ»ВҚc trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi (cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ null nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng truyГЎВ»ВҒn)
    String statusFilter = ctx.queryParam("status");

    List<AuctionResponse> auctions = auctionService.getAll(statusFilter);
    ctx.status(200).json(auctions);
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy chi tiГЎВәВҝt mГЎВ»в„ўt phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ theo ID ГўвӮ¬вҖқ trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ {@link AuctionResponse} Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§y Г„вҖҳГЎВ»В§.
   *
   * <p>KhГғВЎc vГЎВ»вҖәi {@code GET /api/auctions} (trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ list), endpoint nГғВ y trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc
   * "enriched" (lГғВ m giГғВ u thГғВӘm thГғВҙng tin) bao gГЎВ»вҖңm:
   *
   * <ul>
   *   <li>{@code itemName} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ tГғВӘn sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m (join tГЎВ»В« bГЎВәВЈng items).
   *   <li>{@code leadingBidderUsername} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ username cГЎВ»В§a ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi Г„вҖҳang dГЎВәВ«n Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§u.
   *   <li>{@code remainingTimeMs} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ thГЎВ»Вқi gian cГғВІn lГЎВәВЎi (milliseconds).
   * </ul>
   *
   * <p>Client dГғВ№ng endpoint nГғВ y khi mГЎВ»Её mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh {@code auction-detail.fxml}.
   *
   * @param ctx Javalin context chГЎВ»В©a HTTP request/response
   * @param auctionService service tГғВ¬m kiГЎВәВҝm vГғВ  enrich dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   */
  private static void handleGetById(Context ctx, AuctionService auctionService) {
    Long auctionId = Long.parseLong(ctx.pathParam("id"));
    AuctionResponse auction = auctionService.getById(auctionId);
    ctx.status(200).json(auction);
  }

  /**
   * TГЎВәВЎo phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ mГЎВ»вҖәi ГўвӮ¬вҖқ CHГЎВ»ЛҶ SELLER Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc phГғВ©p thГЎВ»Вұc hiГЎВ»вҖЎn.
   *
   * <p>LuГЎВ»вҖңng xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ:
   *
   * <ol>
   *   <li>KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra {@code role == "SELLER"} tГЎВ»В« JWT context.
   *   <li>Parse {@link CreateAuctionRequest} tГЎВ»В« body (chГЎВ»В©a itemId, startingPrice, startTime,
   *       endTime).
   *   <li>GГЎВ»ВҚi {@code AuctionService.create()} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra item thuГЎВ»в„ўc seller, validate startTime <
   *       endTime, tГЎВәВЎo Auction vГЎВ»вҖәi status = "OPEN".
   * </ol>
   *
   * <p>PhiГғВӘn mГЎВ»вҖәi tГЎВәВЎo luГғВҙn cГғВі status = {@code OPEN}. {@link com.auction.service.AuctionScheduler} sГЎВәВҪ
   * tГЎВ»Вұ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng chuyГЎВ»Ж’n sang {@code RUNNING} khi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn {@code startTime}.
   *
   * <p>VГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ request body:
   *
   * <pre>
   *   {
   *     "itemId": 3,
   *     "startingPrice": 5000000,
   *     "startTime": "2025-06-01T10:00:00",
   *     "endTime": "2025-06-01T12:00:00"
   *   }
   * </pre>
   *
   * @param ctx Javalin context chГЎВ»В©a HTTP request/response
   * @param auctionService service tГЎВәВЎo phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ mГЎВ»вҖәi
   * @throws UnauthorizedException nГЎВәВҝu user khГғВҙng cГғВі role SELLER
   */
  private static void handleCreate(Context ctx, AuctionService auctionService) {
    // KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra quyГЎВ»ВҒn: chГЎВ»вҖ° SELLER mГЎВ»вҖәi Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc mГЎВ»Её phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
    requireRole(ctx, "SELLER");

    Long sellerId = ctx.attribute("userId");

    // Parse JSON body
    CreateAuctionRequest request = ctx.bodyAsClass(CreateAuctionRequest.class);

    // Service kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra item thuГЎВ»в„ўc sellerId vГғВ  tГЎВәВЎo phiГғВӘn mГЎВ»вҖәi vГЎВ»вҖәi status=OPEN
    Auction created = auctionService.create(request, sellerId);

    LOGGER.info(
        "TГЎВәВЎo phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ mГЎВ»вҖәi: sellerId={}, itemId={}, startingPrice={}",
        sellerId,
        request.getItemId(),
        request.getStartingPrice());

    ctx.status(201).json(created);
  }

  /**
   * CГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt thГғВҙng tin phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ ГўвӮ¬вҖқ CHГЎВ»ЛҶ SELLER sГЎВ»Её hГЎВ»ВҜu phiГғВӘn vГғВ  KHI PHIГғЕ N CГғвҖҷN ГЎВ»Еҫ TRГЎВәВ NG THГғВҒI OPEN.
   *
   * <p>State Pattern Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc ГғВЎp dГЎВ»ВҘng tГЎВәВЎi Г„вҖҳГғВўy:
   *
   * <ul>
   *   <li>NГЎВәВҝu phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳang ГЎВ»Её {@code OpenState} ГўвҖ вҖҷ {@code state.edit()} thГғВ nh cГғВҙng ГўвҖ вҖҷ cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt DB.
   *   <li>NГЎВәВҝu phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳang ГЎВ»Её {@code RunningState} ГўвҖ вҖҷ {@code state.edit()} nГғВ©m {@code
   *       AuctionClosedException("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ sГЎВ»Вӯa khi phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳang diГЎВ»вҖҰn ra")}.
   *   <li>NГЎВәВҝu phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳang ГЎВ»Её {@code FinishedState}/{@code PaidState}/{@code CanceledState} ГўвҖ вҖҷ tГҶВ°ГҶВЎng
   *       tГЎВ»Вұ, nГғВ©m exception.
   * </ul>
   *
   * <p>NhГЎВ»ВҜng trГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt khi OPEN: {@code startingPrice}, {@code startTime}, {@code
   * endTime}. KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi {@code itemId} sau khi tГЎВәВЎo phiГғВӘn.
   *
   * @param ctx Javalin context chГЎВ»В©a HTTP request/response
   * @param auctionService service cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt phiГғВӘn sau khi qua State pattern validation
   * @throws UnauthorizedException nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng phГЎВәВЈi SELLER hoГЎВәВ·c khГғВҙng sГЎВ»Её hГЎВ»ВҜu phiГғВӘn
   */
  private static void handleUpdate(Context ctx, AuctionService auctionService) {
    requireRole(ctx, "SELLER");

    Long auctionId = Long.parseLong(ctx.pathParam("id"));
    Long userId = ctx.attribute("userId");

    // Parse body ГўвӮ¬вҖқ chГЎВ»В©a cГғВЎc trГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng muГЎВ»вҖҳn cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt
    CreateAuctionRequest request = ctx.bodyAsClass(CreateAuctionRequest.class);

    // Service: kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra ownership + State pattern (chГЎВ»вҖ° OPEN mГЎВ»вҖәi cho sГЎВ»Вӯa)
    AuctionResponse updated = auctionService.update(auctionId, request, userId);

    LOGGER.info("CГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ: auctionId={}, sellerId={}", auctionId, userId);

    ctx.status(200).json(updated);
  }

  /**
   * HГЎВ»В§y phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ ГўвӮ¬вҖқ SELLER sГЎВ»Её hГЎВ»ВҜu phiГғВӘn hoГЎВәВ·c ADMIN.
   *
   * <p>Logic phГғВўn quyГЎВ»ВҒn:
   *
   * <ul>
   *   <li>Role {@code ADMIN} ГўвҖ вҖҷ cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ hГЎВ»В§y bГЎВәВҘt kГЎВ»Ві phiГғВӘn nГғВ o ГЎВ»Её mГЎВ»ВҚi trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi.
   *   <li>Role {@code SELLER} ГўвҖ вҖҷ chГЎВ»вҖ° hГЎВ»В§y Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc phiГғВӘn cГЎВ»В§a chГғВӯnh mГғВ¬nh khi status lГғВ  {@code OPEN} hoГЎВәВ·c
   *       {@code RUNNING} (cho phГғВ©p hГЎВ»В§y trong trГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng hГЎВ»ВЈp bГЎВәВҘt khГЎВәВЈ khГғВЎng).
   *   <li>Role {@code BIDDER} ГўвҖ вҖҷ khГғВҙng Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc phГғВ©p ГўвҖ вҖҷ {@code UnauthorizedException}.
   * </ul>
   *
   * <p>HГЎВ»вҖЎ thГЎВ»вҖҳng khГғВҙng xГғВіa cГЎВ»В©ng (hard delete) mГғВ  chuyГЎВ»Ж’n status sang {@code CANCELED} Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ Г„вҖҳГЎВәВЈm bГЎВәВЈo toГғВ n
   * vГЎВәВ№n lГЎВ»вҖ№ch sГЎВ»Вӯ bid.
   *
   * @param ctx Javalin context chГЎВ»В©a HTTP request/response
   * @param auctionService service xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ hГЎВ»В§y phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @throws UnauthorizedException nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng cГғВі quyГЎВ»ВҒn hГЎВ»В§y
   */
  private static void handleDelete(Context ctx, AuctionService auctionService) {
    String role = ctx.attribute("role");
    Long userId = ctx.attribute("userId");
    Long auctionId = Long.parseLong(ctx.pathParam("id"));

    // ChГЎВ»вҖ° SELLER hoГЎВәВ·c ADMIN mГЎВ»вҖәi Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc hГЎВ»В§y phiГғВӘn
    if (!"SELLER".equals(role) && !"ADMIN".equals(role)) {
      throw new UnauthorizedException(
          "ChГЎВ»вҖ° ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi bГғВЎn hoГЎВәВ·c quГЎВәВЈn trГЎВ»вҖ№ viГғВӘn mГЎВ»вҖәi cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ hГЎВ»В§y phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ");
    }

    // Service xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ: kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra ownership (vГЎВ»вҖәi SELLER), chuyГЎВ»Ж’n status ГўвҖ вҖҷ CANCELED
    auctionService.delete(auctionId, userId, role);

    LOGGER.info(
        "HГЎВ»В§y phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ: auctionId={}, thГЎВ»Вұc hiГЎВ»вҖЎn bГЎВ»Еёi userId={}, role={}",
        auctionId,
        userId,
        role);

    // 204 No Content ГўвӮ¬вҖқ thГғВ nh cГғВҙng, khГғВҙng cГғВі body
    ctx.status(204);
  }

  /**
   * KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra role cГЎВ»В§a user hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi cГғВі khГЎВ»вҖәp vГЎВ»вҖәi role yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u khГғВҙng.
   *
   * <p>PhГҶВ°ГҶВЎng thГЎВ»В©c helper dГғВ№ng nГЎВ»в„ўi bГЎВ»в„ў Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ trГғВЎnh lГЎВәВ·p code kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra role. Attribute {@code "role"} Г„вҖҳГғВЈ
   * Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc {@code JwtMiddleware} set vГғВ o context trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc Г„вҖҳГғВі.
   *
   * @param ctx Javalin context chГЎВ»В©a role cГЎВ»В§a user sau khi middleware xГғВЎc thГЎВ»Вұc
   * @param requiredRole role yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u (vГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ: "SELLER", "ADMIN")
   * @throws UnauthorizedException nГЎВәВҝu role khГғВҙng khГЎВ»вҖәp
   */
  private static void requireRole(Context ctx, String requiredRole) {
    String role = ctx.attribute("role");
    if (!requiredRole.equals(role)) {
      throw new UnauthorizedException(
          "ChГЎВ»вҖ° " + requiredRole + " mГЎВ»вҖәi cГғВі quyГЎВ»ВҒn thГЎВ»Вұc hiГЎВ»вҖЎn thao tГғВЎc nГғВ y");
    }
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\controller\AuctionWebSocketHandler.java ==========
package com.auction.controller;

import com.auction.config.JwtUtil;
import com.auction.dto.BidUpdateMessage;
import com.auction.pattern.observer.AuctionEventManager;
import com.auction.pattern.observer.WebSocketObserver;
import com.auth0.jwt.exceptions.JWTVerificationException;
import com.auth0.jwt.interfaces.DecodedJWT;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.JavaTimeModule;
import io.javalin.websocket.WsCloseContext;
import io.javalin.websocket.WsConnectContext;
import io.javalin.websocket.WsContext;
import io.javalin.websocket.WsErrorContext;
import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
import java.util.concurrent.CopyOnWriteArraySet;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * WebSocket handler ГўвӮ¬вҖқ quГЎВәВЈn lГғВҪ kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi realtime giГЎВ»ВҜa server vГғВ  client.
 *
 * <p><b>Vai trГғВІ trong hГЎВ»вҖЎ thГЎВ»вҖҳng:</b> AuctionWebSocketHandler lГғВ  cГЎВәВ§u nГЎВ»вҖҳi giГЎВ»ВҜa Observer pattern
 * (AuctionEventManager) vГғВ  transport layer (WebSocket). Khi client kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi:
 *
 * <ol>
 *   <li>XГғВЎc thГЎВ»Вұc JWT token tГЎВ»В« query parameter.
 *   <li>LГҶВ°u WebSocket session vГғВ o map theo auctionId.
 *   <li>TГЎВәВЎo {@link WebSocketObserver} vГғВ  subscribe vГғВ o {@link AuctionEventManager}.
 * </ol>
 *
 * <p>Khi cГғВі sГЎВ»Вұ kiГЎВ»вҖЎn (bid mГЎВ»вҖәi, gia hГЎВәВЎn, kГЎВәВҝt thГғВәc):
 *
 * <pre>
 *   BidService ГўвҖ вҖҷ EventManager.notify() ГўвҖ вҖҷ WebSocketObserver.onBidUpdate()
 *     ГўвҖ вҖҷ AuctionWebSocketHandler.broadcast() ГўвҖ вҖҷ gГЎВ»Вӯi JSON Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ client
 * </pre>
 *
 * <p><b>LiГғВӘn kГЎВәВҝt vГЎВ»вҖәi cГғВЎc file khГғВЎc:</b>
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>{@link AuctionEventManager} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ subscribe/unsubscribe observer khi client connect/disconnect
 *   <li>{@link WebSocketObserver} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ observer nhГЎВәВӯn events vГғВ  gГЎВ»ВҚi broadcast()
 *   <li>{@link com.auction.App} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ WebSocket route /ws/auction/{id}
 * </ul>
 */
public class AuctionWebSocketHandler {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(AuctionWebSocketHandler.class);

  /**
   * Map auctionId ГўвҖ вҖҷ set WebSocket sessions Г„вҖҳang kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi. ConcurrentHashMap + CopyOnWriteArraySet Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’
   * thread-safe.
   */
  private final Map<Long, Set<WsContext>> connections = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();

  /**
   * Map userId ГўвҖ вҖҷ set WebSocket sessions cГЎВ»В§a kГғВӘnh riГғВӘng user ({@code /ws/user/{id}}). DГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ push
   * thГғВҙng bГғВЎo biГЎВәВҝn Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng sГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ° khi Admin duyГЎВ»вҖЎt/tГЎВ»В« chГЎВ»вҖҳi nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn.
   */
  private final Map<Long, Set<WsContext>> userConnections = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();

  /** Map session ГўвҖ вҖҷ WebSocketObserver tГҶВ°ГҶВЎng ГЎВ»В©ng. DГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ unsubscribe khi client disconnect. */
  private final Map<WsContext, WebSocketObserver> observers = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();

  private final AuctionEventManager eventManager;
  private final ObjectMapper objectMapper;

  public AuctionWebSocketHandler(AuctionEventManager eventManager) {
    this.eventManager = eventManager;
    this.objectMapper = new ObjectMapper();
    this.objectMapper.registerModule(new JavaTimeModule());
  }

  /**
   * XГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ client kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi WebSocket
   *
   * <p>LuГЎВ»вҖңng:
   *
   * <ol>
   *   <li>LГЎВәВҘy auctionId tГЎВ»В« URL path ({@code /ws/auction/{id}}).
   *   <li>Verify JWT tГЎВ»В« query param {@code token}.
   *   <li>LГҶВ°u session vГғВ o connections map.
   *   <li>TГЎВәВЎo WebSocketObserver vГғВ  subscribe vГғВ o EventManager.
   * </ol>
   */
  public void onConnect(WsConnectContext ctx) {
    try {
      Long auctionId = Long.parseLong(ctx.pathParam("id"));
      String token = ctx.queryParam("token");

      if (token == null || token.isEmpty()) {
        LOGGER.warn("WebSocket tГЎВ»В« chГЎВ»вҖҳi: thiГЎВәВҝu token");
        ctx.session.close(4001, "Missing token");
        return;
      }

      DecodedJWT decoded = JwtUtil.verifyToken(token);
      String username = decoded.getSubject();

      // LГҶВ°u connection
      connections.computeIfAbsent(auctionId, k -> new CopyOnWriteArraySet<>()).add(ctx);

      // TГЎВәВЎo observer vГғВ  subscribe vГғВ o EventManager
      WebSocketObserver observer = new WebSocketObserver(this, auctionId);
      observers.put(ctx, observer);
      eventManager.subscribe(auctionId, observer);

      LOGGER.info("WebSocket kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi: user={}, phiГғВӘn=#{}", username, auctionId);

    } catch (JWTVerificationException e) {
      LOGGER.warn("WebSocket tГЎВ»В« chГЎВ»вҖҳi: token khГғВҙng hГЎВ»ВЈp lГЎВ»вҖЎ");
      ctx.session.close(4001, "Invalid token");
    } catch (Exception e) {
      LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi WebSocket: {}", e.getMessage());
      ctx.session.close(4000, "Connection error");
    }
  }

  /** XГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ client ngГЎВәВҜt kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi ГўвӮ¬вҖқ dГЎВ»ВҚn dГЎВәВ№p connection vГғВ  unsubscribe observer. */
  public void onClose(WsCloseContext ctx) {
    removeConnection(ctx);
    LOGGER.debug("WebSocket ngГЎВәВҜt kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi: status={}, reason={}", ctx.status(), ctx.reason());
  }

  /** XГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ lГЎВ»вҖ”i WebSocket ГўвӮ¬вҖқ dГЎВ»ВҚn dГЎВәВ№p connection vГғВ  unsubscribe observer. */
  public void onError(WsErrorContext ctx) {
    removeConnection(ctx);
    if (ctx.error() != null) {
      LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i WebSocket: {}", ctx.error().getMessage());
    }
  }

  /**
   * GГЎВ»Вӯi BidUpdateMessage JSON Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ client Г„вҖҳang xem phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ.
   *
   * <p>Serialize message 1 lГЎВәВ§n, gГЎВ»Вӯi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ connections cГЎВ»В§a phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГғВі. TГЎВ»Вұ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng dГЎВ»ВҚn dГЎВәВ№p cГғВЎc
   * session Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГғВіng.
   *
   * @param auctionId ID phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @param message message cГЎВәВ§n gГЎВ»Вӯi (BID_UPDATE, TIME_EXTENDED, AUCTION_ENDED)
   */
  public void broadcast(Long auctionId, BidUpdateMessage message) {
    Set<WsContext> auctionConnections = connections.get(auctionId);
    if (auctionConnections == null || auctionConnections.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }

    try {
      String json = objectMapper.writeValueAsString(message);

      for (WsContext wsCtx : auctionConnections) {
        try {
          if (wsCtx.session.isOpen()) {
            wsCtx.send(json);
          } else {
            auctionConnections.remove(wsCtx);
          }
        } catch (Exception e) {
          LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i gГЎВ»Вӯi WebSocket message: {}", e.getMessage());
          auctionConnections.remove(wsCtx);
        }
      }

      LOGGER.debug(
          "Broadcast {} Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn {} client cho phiГғВӘn #{}",
          message.getType(),
          auctionConnections.size(),
          auctionId);

    } catch (Exception e) {
      LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i serialize WebSocket message: {}", e.getMessage());
    }
  }

  // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ KГғВӘnh WebSocket riГғВӘng cho user (/ws/user/{id}) ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬

  /**
   * XГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ client kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi kГғВӘnh user ГўвӮ¬вҖқ xГғВЎc thГЎВ»Вұc JWT vГғВ  lГҶВ°u session theo userId. Route: {@code
   * /ws/user/{id}}
   */
  public void onUserConnect(WsConnectContext ctx) {
    try {
      Long userId = Long.parseLong(ctx.pathParam("id"));
      String token = ctx.queryParam("token");

      if (token == null || token.isEmpty()) {
        ctx.session.close(4001, "Missing token");
        return;
      }

      DecodedJWT decoded = JwtUtil.verifyToken(token);
      String username = decoded.getSubject();

      userConnections.computeIfAbsent(userId, k -> new CopyOnWriteArraySet<>()).add(ctx);
      LOGGER.info("User WebSocket kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi: user={}, userId=#{}", username, userId);

    } catch (JWTVerificationException e) {
      ctx.session.close(4001, "Invalid token");
    } catch (Exception e) {
      LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi User WebSocket: {}", e.getMessage());
      ctx.session.close(4000, "Connection error");
    }
  }

  /** XГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ ngГЎВәВҜt kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi kГғВӘnh user. */
  public void onUserClose(WsCloseContext ctx) {
    userConnections.values().forEach(set -> set.remove(ctx));
    LOGGER.debug("User WebSocket ngГЎВәВҜt kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi: status={}", ctx.status());
  }

  /** XГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ lГЎВ»вҖ”i kГғВӘnh user. */
  public void onUserError(WsErrorContext ctx) {
    userConnections.values().forEach(set -> set.remove(ctx));
    if (ctx.error() != null) {
      LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i User WebSocket: {}", ctx.error().getMessage());
    }
  }

  /**
   * Push thГғВҙng bГғВЎo biГЎВәВҝn Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng sГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ° Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn user cГЎВ»ВҘ thГЎВ»Ж’ qua kГғВӘnh {@code /ws/user/{id}}.
   *
   * @param userId ID user cГЎВәВ§n notify
   * @param newBalance sГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ° mГЎВ»вҖәi (null nГЎВәВҝu bГЎВ»вҖ№ tГЎВ»В« chГЎВ»вҖҳi)
   * @param approved true = duyГЎВ»вҖЎt (cГЎВ»в„ўng tiГЎВ»ВҒn), false = tГЎВ»В« chГЎВ»вҖҳi
   */
  public void notifyBalanceUpdate(Long userId, BigDecimal newBalance, boolean approved) {
    Set<WsContext> sessions = userConnections.get(userId);
    if (sessions == null || sessions.isEmpty()) {
      LOGGER.warn("notifyBalanceUpdate: userId={} khГғВҙng cГғВі WS session, bГЎВ»ВҸ qua.", userId);
      return;
    }
    try {
      BidUpdateMessage msg = BidUpdateMessage.balanceUpdated(userId, newBalance, approved);
      String json = objectMapper.writeValueAsString(msg);
      for (WsContext wsCtx : sessions) {
        try {
          if (wsCtx.session.isOpen()) {
            wsCtx.send(json);
          } else {
            sessions.remove(wsCtx);
          }
        } catch (Exception e) {
          LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i gГЎВ»Вӯi User WebSocket message: {}", e.getMessage());
          sessions.remove(wsCtx);
        }
      }
      LOGGER.info(
          "Г„ВҗГғВЈ notify BALANCE_UPDATED ГўвҖ вҖҷ userId={}, approved={}, newBalance={}",
          userId,
          approved,
          newBalance);
    } catch (Exception e) {
      LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i serialize BALANCE_UPDATED message: {}", e.getMessage());
    }
  }

  /** XГғВіa connection vГғВ  unsubscribe observer khГЎВ»ВҸi EventManager. */
  private void removeConnection(WsContext ctx) {
    connections.values().forEach(set -> set.remove(ctx));

    WebSocketObserver observer = observers.remove(ctx);
    if (observer != null) {
      eventManager.unsubscribe(observer.getAuctionId(), observer);
    }
  }

  /** LГЎВәВҘy sГЎВ»вҖҳ lГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈng kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi Г„вҖҳang active cho mГЎВ»в„ўt phiГғВӘn ГўвӮ¬вҖқ dГғВ№ng cho health check. */
  public int getConnectionCount(Long auctionId) {
    Set<WsContext> set = connections.get(auctionId);
    return set != null ? set.size() : 0;
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\controller\AuthController.java ==========
package com.auction.controller;

import com.auction.config.JwtUtil;
import com.auction.dto.ForgotPasswordRequest;
import com.auction.dto.LoginRequest;
import com.auction.dto.RegisterRequest;
import com.auction.model.User;
import com.auction.service.PasswordResetService;
import com.auction.service.UserService;
import io.javalin.Javalin;
import io.javalin.http.Context;
import java.util.Map;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * Controller xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ cГғВЎc endpoint xГғВЎc thГЎВ»Вұc ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng: Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ, Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp, quГғВӘn mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u.
 *
 * <p>CГғВЎc endpoint khГғВҙng yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u JWT token (khai bГғВЎo public trong {@code JwtMiddleware}):
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>{@code POST /api/auth/register} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ TГЎВәВЎo tГғВ i khoГЎВәВЈn mГЎВ»вҖәi, trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ JWT token.
 *   <li>{@code POST /api/auth/login} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp, trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ JWT token.
 *   <li>{@code POST /api/auth/forgot-password} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ GГЎВ»Вӯi yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t lГЎВәВЎi mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u cho Admin duyГЎВ»вҖЎt.
 * </ul>
 *
 * @see com.auction.service.UserService
 * @see com.auction.config.JwtUtil
 */
public class AuthController {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(AuthController.class);

  private AuthController() {}

  /**
   * Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ route Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ vГғВ  Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp vГғВ o Javalin instance.
   *
   * @param app Javalin instance
   * @param userService service xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ, Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp
   */
  public static void register(Javalin app, UserService userService) {
    app.post("/api/auth/register", ctx -> handleRegister(ctx, userService));
    app.post("/api/auth/login", ctx -> handleLogin(ctx, userService));
    LOGGER.info("Г„ВҗГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ AuthController: POST /api/auth/register, POST /api/auth/login");
  }

  /**
   * Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ route quГғВӘn mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u ГўвӮ¬вҖқ user gГЎВ»Вӯi yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u, Admin duyГЎВ»вҖЎt.
   *
   * <ul>
   *   <li>{@code POST /api/auth/forgot-password} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ TГЎВәВЎo yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u PENDING, Admin sГЎВәВҪ xГғВ©t duyГЎВ»вҖЎt.
   * </ul>
   *
   * @param app Javalin instance
   * @param resetService service quГЎВәВЈn lГғВҪ yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t lГЎВәВЎi mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u
   */
  public static void registerPasswordReset(Javalin app, PasswordResetService resetService) {
    app.post("/api/auth/forgot-password", ctx -> handleForgotPassword(ctx, resetService));
    LOGGER.info("Г„ВҗГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ: POST /api/auth/forgot-password");
  }

  private static void handleRegister(Context ctx, UserService userService) {
    RegisterRequest request = ctx.bodyAsClass(RegisterRequest.class);
    User newUser = userService.register(request);
    String token = JwtUtil.createToken(newUser.getId(), newUser.getUsername(), newUser.getRole());

    LOGGER.info(
        "Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ thГғВ nh cГғВҙng: username={}, role={}", newUser.getUsername(), newUser.getRole());

    ctx.status(201)
        .json(
            Map.of(
                "token", token,
                "role", newUser.getRole(),
                "username", newUser.getUsername(),
                "userId", newUser.getId()));
  }

  private static void handleLogin(Context ctx, UserService userService) {
    LoginRequest request = ctx.bodyAsClass(LoginRequest.class);
    String token = userService.login(request);

    String role = userService.getRoleByUsername(request.getUsername());
    String username = request.getUsername();
    long userId = JwtUtil.verifyToken(token).getClaim("userId").asLong();

    LOGGER.info("Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp thГғВ nh cГғВҙng: username={}", username);

    ctx.status(200)
        .json(
            Map.of(
                "token", token,
                "role", role,
                "username", username,
                "userId", userId));
  }

  /**
   * XГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u quГғВӘn mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u ГўвӮ¬вҖқ tГЎВәВЎo bГЎВәВЈn ghi PENDING cho Admin xГғВ©t duyГЎВ»вҖЎt.
   *
   * <p>Request body: {@code {"email": "user@example.com"}}
   *
   * @param ctx Javalin context
   * @param service PasswordResetService
   */
  private static void handleForgotPassword(Context ctx, PasswordResetService service) {
    ForgotPasswordRequest req = ctx.bodyAsClass(ForgotPasswordRequest.class);
    if (req.getEmail() == null || req.getEmail().trim().isEmpty()) {
      ctx.status(400).json(Map.of("message", "Email khГғВҙng Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ trГЎВ»вҖҳng."));
      return;
    }
    service.requestReset(req.getEmail().trim());
    ctx.status(200)
        .json(
            Map.of(
                "message",
                "YГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГЎВ»Вӯi. Admin sГЎВәВҪ xГғВ©t duyГЎВ»вҖЎt vГғВ  mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u sГЎВәВҪ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t lГЎВәВЎi vГЎВ»ВҒ"
                    + " 123456."));
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\controller\BidController.java ==========
package com.auction.controller;

import com.auction.dto.BidRequest;
import com.auction.exception.UnauthorizedException;
import com.auction.model.BidTransaction;
import com.auction.service.BidService;
import io.javalin.Javalin;
import java.util.List;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * Controller xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ cГғВЎc endpoint Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t giГғВЎ vГғВ  lГЎВ»вҖ№ch sГЎВ»Вӯ bid
 *
 * <p>Danh sГғВЎch endpoints:
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>{@code POST /api/auctions/{id}/bid} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ Г„ВҗГЎВәВ·t giГғВЎ, chГЎВ»вҖ° BIDDER
 *   <li>{@code GET /api/auctions/{id}/bids} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ LГЎВәВҘy lГЎВ»вҖ№ch sГЎВ»Вӯ bid cГЎВ»В§a phiГғВӘn (Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ vГЎВәВҪ chart)
 * </ul>
 *
 * <p>Controller nГғВ y delegate toГғВ n bГЎВ»в„ў business logic sang {@link BidService}: validate giГғВЎ,
 * anti-sniping, auto-bid chain, vГғВ  WebSocket broadcast.
 */
public class BidController {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(BidController.class);

  private final BidService bidService;

  public BidController(BidService bidService) {
    this.bidService = bidService;
  }

  public void register(Javalin app) {
    // POST /api/auctions/{id}/bid ГўвӮ¬вҖқ Г„ВҗГЎВәВ·t giГғВЎ
    // YГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u: role = BIDDER (SELLER khГғВҙng Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc tГЎВ»Вұ bid phiГғВӘn cГЎВ»В§a chГғВӯnh mГғВ¬nh nhГҶВ°ng vГЎВәВ«n Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc bid
    // phiГғВӘn cГЎВ»В§a ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi khГғВЎc)
    // Body: {"amount": 500000}
    // Response 201: BidTransaction JSON
    app.post(
        "/api/auctions/{id}/bid",
        ctx -> {
          String role = ctx.attribute("role");

          if (!"BIDDER".equals(role) && !"SELLER".equals(role)) {
            throw new UnauthorizedException("ChГЎВ»вҖ° BIDDER hoГЎВәВ·c SELLER mГЎВ»вҖәi Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc tham gia Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t giГғВЎ");
          }

          Long auctionId = Long.parseLong(ctx.pathParam("id"));
          Long bidderId = ctx.attribute("userId");
          BidRequest request = ctx.bodyAsClass(BidRequest.class);

          // GГЎВ»ВҚi BidService vГЎВ»вҖәi signature mГЎВ»вҖәi
          BidTransaction bid = bidService.placeBid(auctionId, bidderId, request.getAmount(), false);

          LOGGER.info("Bid Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t thГғВ nh cГғВҙng qua API: auction={}, bidder={}", auctionId, bidderId);
          ctx.status(201).json(bid);
        });

    // GET /api/auctions/{id}/bids ГўвӮ¬вҖқ LГЎВ»вҖ№ch sГЎВ»Вӯ bid
    // DГғВ№ng cho Bid History Chart (trГЎВ»ВҘc X = thГЎВ»Вқi gian, trГЎВ»ВҘc Y = giГғВЎ)
    // Response: List<BidTransaction> sГЎВәВҜp xГЎВәВҝp theo createdAt ASC
    app.get(
        "/api/auctions/{id}/bids",
        ctx -> {
          Long auctionId = Long.parseLong(ctx.pathParam("id"));
          List<BidTransaction> bids = bidService.getBidHistory(auctionId);
          ctx.json(bids);
        });
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\controller\ItemController.java ==========
package com.auction.controller;

import com.auction.dto.CreateItemRequest;
import com.auction.exception.UnauthorizedException;
import com.auction.model.Item;
import com.auction.service.ItemService;
import io.javalin.Javalin;
import io.javalin.http.Context;
import java.util.List;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * Controller xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ toГғВ n bГЎВ»в„ў thao tГғВЎc CRUD cho tГғВ i nguyГғВӘn Item (sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ)
 *
 * <p>Danh sГғВЎch endpoints vГғВ  quyГЎВ»ВҒn truy cГЎВәВӯp:
 *
 * <pre>
 *   GET    /api/items          ГўвҖ вҖҷ MГЎВ»ВҚi user Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp (cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ filter theo sellerId)
 *   GET    /api/items/:id      ГўвҖ вҖҷ MГЎВ»ВҚi user Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp
 *   POST   /api/items          ГўвҖ вҖҷ ChГЎВ»вҖ° SELLER
 *   PUT    /api/items/:id      ГўвҖ вҖҷ ChГЎВ»вҖ° SELLER sГЎВ»Её hГЎВ»ВҜu item Г„вҖҳГғВі
 *   DELETE /api/items/:id      ГўвҖ вҖҷ SELLER sГЎВ»Её hГЎВ»ВҜu item hoГЎВәВ·c ADMIN
 * </pre>
 *
 * <p>CГҶВЎ chГЎВәВҝ kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra quyГЎВ»ВҒn:
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>JWT Middleware (cГЎВәВҘu hГғВ¬nh trong {@link com.auction.App}) Г„вҖҳГғВЈ xГғВЎc thГЎВ»Вұc token vГғВ  set cГғВЎc
 *       attribute vГғВ o context: {@code userId}, {@code username}, {@code role}
 *   <li>Controller Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҚc {@code ctx.attribute("role")} Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra role
 *   <li>Controller Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҚc {@code ctx.attribute("userId")} Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra ownership
 * </ul>
 *
 * <p>Factory Method pattern Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc ГғВЎp dГЎВ»ВҘng trong {@link ItemService#create}: nhГЎВәВӯn {@code category} tГЎВ»В«
 * request ("ELECTRONICS"/"ART"/"VEHICLE"), tГЎВәВЎo Г„вҖҳГғВәng subclass tГҶВ°ГҶВЎng ГЎВ»В©ng
 *
 * @see com.auction.service.ItemService
 * @see com.auction.pattern.factory.ItemFactory
 */
public class ItemController {

  /** Logger ghi lГЎВәВЎi cГғВЎc thao tГғВЎc CRUD trГғВӘn item. */
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ItemController.class);

  /** HГғВ m khГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo private ГўвӮ¬вҖқ lГЎВ»вҖәp nГғВ y chГЎВ»вҖ° dГғВ№ng static methods, khГғВҙng cГЎВәВ§n instance. */
  private ItemController() {}

  /**
   * Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ route cГЎВ»В§a ItemController vГғВ o Javalin instance.
   *
   * @param app Javalin instance Г„вҖҳang chГЎВәВЎy
   * @param itemService service xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ logic nghiГЎВ»вҖЎp vГЎВ»ВҘ cho Item
   */
  public static void register(Javalin app, ItemService itemService) {
    app.get("/api/items", ctx -> handleGetAll(ctx, itemService));
    app.get("/api/items/{id}", ctx -> handleGetById(ctx, itemService));
    app.post("/api/items", ctx -> handleCreate(ctx, itemService));
    app.put("/api/items/{id}", ctx -> handleUpdate(ctx, itemService));
    app.delete("/api/items/{id}", ctx -> handleDelete(ctx, itemService));

    LOGGER.info(
        "Г„ВҗГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ ItemController: GET/POST /api/items, " + "GET/PUT/DELETE /api/items/:id");
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy danh sГғВЎch tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m, cГғВі hГЎВ»вҖ” trГЎВ»ВЈ lГЎВ»ВҚc theo {@code sellerId}.
   *
   * <p>Query parameter tГғВ№y chГЎВ»ВҚn:
   *
   * <ul>
   *   <li>{@code ?sellerId=5} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ chГЎВ»вҖ° trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ item cГЎВ»В§a seller cГғВі id=5.
   *   <li>KhГғВҙng cГғВі parameter ГўвҖ вҖҷ trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ item trong hГЎВ»вҖЎ thГЎВ»вҖҳng.
   * </ul>
   *
   * <p>VГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ response:
   *
   * <pre>
   *   [
   *     {"id": 1, "name": "iPhone 15", "category": "ELECTRONICS",
   *      "sellerId": 3, "brand": "Apple"},
   *     {"id": 2, "name": "Tranh SГҶВЎn DГЎВәВ§u", "category": "ART",
   *      "sellerId": 5, "artist": "NguyГЎВ»вҖҰn VГ„Ж’n A"}
   *   ]
   * </pre>
   *
   * @param ctx Javalin context chГЎВ»В©a HTTP request/response
   * @param itemService service truy vГЎВәВҘn danh sГғВЎch item
   */
  private static void handleGetAll(Context ctx, ItemService itemService) {
    // KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra query param sellerId (nГЎВәВҝu cГғВі) Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ lГЎВ»ВҚc theo ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi bГғВЎn
    String sellerIdParam = ctx.queryParam("sellerId");

    List<Item> items;
    if (sellerIdParam != null) {
      Long sellerId = Long.parseLong(sellerIdParam);
      items = itemService.getBySellerId(sellerId);
    } else {
      items = itemService.getAll();
    }

    ctx.status(200).json(items);
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy chi tiГЎВәВҝt mГЎВ»в„ўt sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m theo ID.
   *
   * <p>NГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy item vГЎВ»вҖәi ID Г„вҖҳГғВЈ cho, service sГЎВәВҪ nГғВ©m {@code NotFoundException} vГғВ  exception
   * handler trong {@code App.java} sГЎВәВҪ trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ HTTP 404.
   *
   * @param ctx Javalin context chГЎВ»В©a HTTP request/response
   * @param itemService service tГғВ¬m kiГЎВәВҝm item theo ID
   */
  private static void handleGetById(Context ctx, ItemService itemService) {
    Long itemId = Long.parseLong(ctx.pathParam("id"));
    Item item = itemService.getById(itemId);
    ctx.status(200).json(item);
  }

  /**
   * TГЎВәВЎo sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m mГЎВ»вҖәi ГўвӮ¬вҖқ CHГЎВ»ЛҶ SELLER Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc phГғВ©p thГЎВ»Вұc hiГЎВ»вҖЎn.
   *
   * <p>Factory Method pattern Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc ГғВЎp dГЎВ»ВҘng ГЎВ»Её Г„вҖҳГғВўy: {@code ItemService.create()} nhГЎВәВӯn {@code
   * category} tГЎВ»В« request vГғВ  gГЎВ»ВҚi {@code ItemFactory.create()} Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ tГЎВәВЎo Г„вҖҳГғВәng subclass ({@code
   * Electronics}, {@code Art}, hoГЎВәВ·c {@code Vehicle}).
   *
   * <p>LuГЎВ»вҖңng xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ:
   *
   * <ol>
   *   <li>KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra {@code role == "SELLER"} tГЎВ»В« JWT context ГўвӮ¬вҖқ nГғВ©m {@code UnauthorizedException} nГЎВәВҝu
   *       khГғВҙng phГЎВәВЈi SELLER.
   *   <li>LГЎВәВҘy {@code userId} tГЎВ»В« JWT context Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ gГғВЎn lГғВ m {@code sellerId}.
   *   <li>Parse {@link CreateItemRequest} tГЎВ»В« body.
   *   <li>GГЎВ»ВҚi {@code ItemService.create()} ГўвҖ вҖҷ Factory tГЎВәВЎo Г„вҖҳГғВәng subclass ГўвҖ вҖҷ lГҶВ°u DB.
   * </ol>
   *
   * <p>VГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ request body:
   *
   * <pre>
   *   {
   *     "name": "iPhone 15 Pro",
   *     "description": "MГғВЎy mГЎВ»вҖәi 100%, chГҶВ°a kГғВӯch hoГЎВәВЎt",
   *     "category": "ELECTRONICS",
   *     "categoryDetail": "Apple"
   *   }
   * </pre>
   *
   * @param ctx Javalin context chГЎВ»В©a HTTP request/response
   * @param itemService service tГЎВәВЎo item qua Factory pattern
   * @throws UnauthorizedException nГЎВәВҝu user khГғВҙng cГғВі role SELLER
   */
  private static void handleCreate(Context ctx, ItemService itemService) {
    // KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra quyГЎВ»ВҒn: chГЎВ»вҖ° SELLER mГЎВ»вҖәi Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc tГЎВәВЎo sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m
    requireRole(ctx, "SELLER");

    // LГЎВәВҘy sellerId tГЎВ»В« JWT token (Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc middleware parse vГғВ  set vГғВ o context)
    Long sellerId = ctx.attribute("userId");

    // Parse JSON body thГғВ nh DTO
    CreateItemRequest request = ctx.bodyAsClass(CreateItemRequest.class);

    // GГЎВ»ВҚi service: dГғВ№ng Factory Method Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ tГЎВәВЎo Г„вҖҳГғВәng subclass Item
    Item createdItem = itemService.create(request, sellerId);

    LOGGER.info(
        "TГЎВәВЎo item mГЎВ»вҖәi: sellerId={}, category={}, name={}",
        sellerId,
        request.getCategory(),
        request.getName());

    ctx.status(201).json(createdItem);
  }

  /**
   * CГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt thГғВҙng tin sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m ГўвӮ¬вҖқ CHГЎВ»ЛҶ SELLER sГЎВ»Её hГЎВ»ВҜu item mГЎВ»вҖәi Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc phГғВ©p.
   *
   * <p>KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra ownership: {@code item.sellerId == userId tГЎВ»В« JWT}. NГЎВәВҝu mГЎВ»в„ўt seller cГЎВ»вҖҳ sГЎВ»Вӯa item cГЎВ»В§a
   * seller khГғВЎc ГўвҖ вҖҷ {@code UnauthorizedException}.
   *
   * <p>LГҶВ°u ГғВҪ: Item Г„вҖҳang Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc dГғВ№ng trong phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ RUNNING sГЎВәВҪ KHГғвҖқNG thГЎВ»Ж’ sГЎВ»Вӯa (logic nГғВ y Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc xГЎВ»Вӯ
   * lГғВҪ ГЎВ»Её tГЎВәВ§ng Service, khГғВҙng phГЎВәВЈi Controller).
   *
   * @param ctx Javalin context chГЎВ»В©a HTTP request/response
   * @param itemService service cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt item sau khi kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra ownership
   * @throws UnauthorizedException nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng phГЎВәВЈi SELLER hoГЎВәВ·c khГғВҙng sГЎВ»Её hГЎВ»ВҜu item
   */
  private static void handleUpdate(Context ctx, ItemService itemService) {
    // KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra role cГҶВЎ bГЎВәВЈn
    requireRole(ctx, "SELLER");

    Long itemId = Long.parseLong(ctx.pathParam("id"));
    Long userId = ctx.attribute("userId");

    // Parse body ГўвӮ¬вҖқ chГЎВ»В©a cГғВЎc trГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng cГЎВәВ§n cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt
    CreateItemRequest request = ctx.bodyAsClass(CreateItemRequest.class);

    // Service sГЎВәВҪ kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra item.sellerId == userId trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc khi update
    Item updatedItem = itemService.update(itemId, request, userId);

    LOGGER.info("CГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt item: itemId={}, sellerId={}", itemId, userId);

    ctx.status(200).json(updatedItem);
  }

  /**
   * XГғВіa sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m ГўвӮ¬вҖқ SELLER sГЎВ»Её hГЎВ»ВҜu item hoГЎВәВ·c ADMIN Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc phГғВ©p.
   *
   * <p>Logic phГғВўn quyГЎВ»ВҒn:
   *
   * <ul>
   *   <li>Role {@code ADMIN} ГўвҖ вҖҷ cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ xГғВіa bГЎВәВҘt kГЎВ»Ві item nГғВ o.
   *   <li>Role {@code SELLER} ГўвҖ вҖҷ chГЎВ»вҖ° xГғВіa Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc item cГЎВ»В§a mГғВ¬nh.
   *   <li>Role {@code BIDDER} ГўвҖ вҖҷ khГғВҙng Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc phГғВ©p ГўвҖ вҖҷ {@code UnauthorizedException}.
   * </ul>
   *
   * <p>NГЎВәВҝu item Г„вҖҳang liГғВӘn kГЎВәВҝt vГЎВ»вҖәi phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ RUNNING, service sГЎВәВҪ nГғВ©m lГЎВ»вҖ”i Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ trГғВЎnh mГЎВәВҘt tГғВӯnh toГғВ n
   * vГЎВәВ№n dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu.
   *
   * @param ctx Javalin context chГЎВ»В©a HTTP request/response
   * @param itemService service xГғВіa item sau khi kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra quyГЎВ»ВҒn vГғВ  tГғВӯnh toГғВ n vГЎВәВ№n dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu
   * @throws UnauthorizedException nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng cГғВі quyГЎВ»ВҒn xГғВіa
   */
  private static void handleDelete(Context ctx, ItemService itemService) {
    String role = ctx.attribute("role");
    Long userId = ctx.attribute("userId");
    Long itemId = Long.parseLong(ctx.pathParam("id"));

    // ChГЎВ»вҖ° SELLER hoГЎВәВ·c ADMIN mГЎВ»вҖәi Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc xГғВіa
    if (!"SELLER".equals(role) && !"ADMIN".equals(role)) {
      throw new UnauthorizedException("ChГЎВ»вҖ° ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi bГғВЎn hoГЎВәВ·c quГЎВәВЈn trГЎВ»вҖ№ viГғВӘn mГЎВ»вҖәi cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ xГғВіa sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m");
    }

    // Service xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ logic phГғВўn quyГЎВ»ВҒn chi tiГЎВәВҝt (ADMIN bypass ownership check, SELLER thГғВ¬ khГғВҙng)
    itemService.delete(itemId, userId, role);

    LOGGER.info("XГғВіa item: itemId={}, thГЎВ»Вұc hiГЎВ»вҖЎn bГЎВ»Еёi userId={}, role={}", itemId, userId, role);

    // 204 No Content ГўвӮ¬вҖқ xГғВіa thГғВ nh cГғВҙng, khГғВҙng cГғВі body trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ
    ctx.status(204);
  }

  /**
   * KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra role cГЎВ»В§a user hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi cГғВі khГЎВ»вҖәp vГЎВ»вҖәi role yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u khГғВҙng.
   *
   * <p>PhГҶВ°ГҶВЎng thГЎВ»В©c helper dГғВ№ng nГЎВ»в„ўi bГЎВ»в„ў Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ trГғВЎnh lГЎВәВ·p code kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra role. Attribute {@code "role"} Г„вҖҳГғВЈ
   * Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc {@code JwtMiddleware} set vГғВ o context trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc Г„вҖҳГғВі.
   *
   * @param ctx Javalin context chГЎВ»В©a role cГЎВ»В§a user sau khi middleware xГғВЎc thГЎВ»Вұc
   * @param requiredRole role yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u (vГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ: "SELLER", "ADMIN")
   * @throws UnauthorizedException nГЎВәВҝu role khГғВҙng khГЎВ»вҖәp
   */
  private static void requireRole(Context ctx, String requiredRole) {
    String role = ctx.attribute("role");
    if (!requiredRole.equals(role)) {
      throw new UnauthorizedException(
          "ChГЎВ»вҖ° " + requiredRole + " mГЎВ»вҖәi cГғВі quyГЎВ»ВҒn thГЎВ»Вұc hiГЎВ»вҖЎn thao tГғВЎc nГғВ y");
    }
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\dao\AuctionDao.java ==========
package com.auction.dao;

import com.auction.model.Auction;
import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.sql.SQLException;
import java.time.LocalDateTime;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.Jdbi;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.mapper.RowMapper;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.statement.StatementContext;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * DAO (Data Access Object) cho bГЎВәВЈng auctions
 *
 * <p>Class nГғВ y chГЎВ»вҖ№u trГғВЎch nhiГЎВ»вҖЎm giao tiГЎВәВҝp vГЎВ»вҖәi bГЎВәВЈng auctions trong database. Г„ВҗГғВўy lГғВ  DAO quan trГЎВ»ВҚng
 * nhГЎВәВҘt vГғВ¬ nГғВі xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ cГғВЎc thao tГғВЎc Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ cГЎВ»вҖҳt lГғВөi, bao gГЎВ»вҖңm cГЎВәВЈ viГЎВ»вҖЎc khГғВіa row Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ trГғВЎnh race condition
 * (SELECT FOR UPDATE)
 *
 * <h3>Vai trГғВІ trong hГЎВ»вҖЎ thГЎВ»вҖҳng</h3>
 *
 * <p>AuctionDao nГЎВәВұm ГЎВ»Её tГЎВәВ§ng dГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәi cГғВ№ng, Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc AuctionService vГғВ  BidService gГЎВ»ВҚi. MГЎВ»ВҚi thao tГғВЎc Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҚc/ghi
 * trГғВӘn bГЎВәВЈng auctions Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҒu Г„вҖҳi qua DAO nГғВ y
 *
 * <h3>Concurrency - SELECT FOR UPDATE</h3>
 *
 * <p>Khi nhiГЎВ»ВҒu user bid cГғВ№ng lГғВәc, cГЎВәВ§n Г„вҖҳГЎВәВЈm bГЎВәВЈo khГғВҙng cГғВі lost update. GiГЎВәВЈi phГғВЎp: 2 tГЎВәВ§ng bГЎВәВЈo vГЎВ»вҖЎ
 *
 * <ol>
 *   <li><b>TГЎВәВ§ng application:</b> synchronized(auction) trong BidService
 *   <li><b>TГЎВәВ§ng database:</b> SELECT ... FOR UPDATE khГғВіa row khi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҚc
 * </ol>
 *
 * <p>LuГЎВ»вҖңng xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ bid an toГғВ n:
 *
 * <pre>
 * jdbi.inTransaction(handle -> {
 *     // 1. KhГғВіa row - cГғВЎc transaction khГғВЎc phГЎВәВЈi chГЎВ»Вқ
 *     Auction auction = auctionDao.findByIdForUpdate(handle, auctionId);
 *
 *     // 2. Validate vГғВ  update trong Java
 *     auction.setCurrentPrice(newPrice);
 *     auction.setLeadingBidderId(userId);
 *
 *     // 3. Update database - lock Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc giГЎВәВЈi phГғВіng khi commit
 *     auctionDao.updateInTransaction(handle, auction);
 *
 *     // 4. Commit transaction
 *     return auction;
 * });
 * </pre>
 *
 * <h3>State pattern liГғВӘn kГЎВәВҝt</h3>
 *
 * <p>TrГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi cГЎВ»В§a Auction (OPEN, RUNNING, FINISHED, PAID, CANCELED) Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc quГЎВәВЈn lГғВҪ bГЎВ»Еёi State
 * pattern trong service layer. DAO chГЎВ»вҖ° Г„вҖҳГҶВЎn thuГЎВәВ§n Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҚc/ghi trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi, khГғВҙng quyГЎВәВҝt Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖ№nh logic chuyГЎВ»Ж’n
 * trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi.
 *
 * <h3>LiГғВӘn kГЎВәВҝt vГЎВ»вҖәi cГғВЎc file khГғВЎc</h3>
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li><b>Auction.java</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ model class, chГЎВ»В©a dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
 *   <li><b>BidService.java</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ gГЎВ»ВҚi findByIdForUpdate() vГғВ  updateInTransaction()
 *   <li><b>AuctionService.java</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ CRUD thГғВҙng thГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng cho auction
 *   <li><b>AuctionScheduler.java</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi khi hГЎВәВҝt giГЎВ»Вқ
 *   <li><b>V1__initial_schema.sql</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖ№nh nghГ„В©a bГЎВәВЈng auctions
 * </ul>
 */
public class AuctionDao {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(AuctionDao.class);

  /**
   * Danh sГғВЎch cГЎВ»в„ўt SELECT dГғВ№ng chung, trГғВЎnh copy-paste. [FIX #10]
   *
   * <p>Bao gГЎВ»вҖңm cГЎВәВЈ updated_at [FIX #6] ГўвӮ¬вҖқ trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc Г„вҖҳГғВўy SELECT cГғВі updated_at nhГҶВ°ng Mapper khГғВҙng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҚc, gГғВўy
   * mГЎВәВҘt thГғВҙng tin cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt cuГЎВ»вҖҳi cГғВ№ng.
   */
  private static final String SELECT_COLUMNS =
      "id, item_id, starting_price, current_price, leading_bidder_id, "
          + "start_time, end_time, status, created_at, updated_at";

  private final Jdbi jdbi;

  public AuctionDao(Jdbi jdbi) {
    this.jdbi = jdbi;
  }

  /**
   * RowMapper chuyГЎВ»Ж’n ResultSet thГғВ nh Auction object.
   *
   * <p>[FIX #6] Mapper giГЎВ»Вқ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҚc cГЎВәВЈ cГЎВ»в„ўt updated_at vГғВ  set vГғВ o Auction object. TrГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc Г„вҖҳГғВўy cГЎВ»в„ўt nГғВ y Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc
   * SELECT nhГҶВ°ng bГЎВ»вҖ№ bГЎВ»ВҸ qua ГўвҖ вҖҷ mГЎВәВҘt dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu "cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt lГЎВәВ§n cuГЎВ»вҖҳi".
   *
   * <p><b>LГҶВҜU ГғВқ:</b> CГЎВәВ§n thГғВӘm field {@code updatedAt} (kiГЎВ»Ж’u LocalDateTime) vГғВ  setter {@code
   * setUpdatedAt()} vГғВ o model {@code Auction.java} nГЎВәВҝu chГҶВ°a cГғВі.
   *
   * <p>Map cГғВЎc cГЎВ»в„ўt trong bГЎВәВЈng auctions:
   *
   * <pre>
   * | id | item_id | starting_price | current_price | leading_bidder_id |
   * | start_time | end_time | status | created_at | updated_at |
   * </pre>
   */
  private static class AuctionMapper implements RowMapper<Auction> {
    @Override
    public Auction map(ResultSet rs, StatementContext ctx) throws SQLException {
      Auction auction =
          new Auction(
              rs.getLong("id"),
              rs.getLong("item_id"),
              rs.getBigDecimal("starting_price"),
              rs.getBigDecimal("current_price"),
              getLongOrNull(rs, "leading_bidder_id"),
              rs.getTimestamp("start_time").toLocalDateTime(),
              rs.getTimestamp("end_time").toLocalDateTime(),
              rs.getString("status"),
              rs.getTimestamp("created_at").toLocalDateTime());

      // [FIX #6] Г„ВҗГЎВ»ВҚc updated_at vГғВ  set vГғВ o Auction
      var updatedAtTs = rs.getTimestamp("updated_at");
      if (updatedAtTs != null) {
        auction.setUpdatedAt(updatedAtTs.toLocalDateTime());
      }

      return auction;
    }

    private Long getLongOrNull(ResultSet rs, String column) throws SQLException {
      long value = rs.getLong(column);
      return rs.wasNull() ? null : value;
    }
  }

  // ============================================================
  // CREATE (INSERT)
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * TГЎВәВЎo phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ mГЎВ»вҖәi.
   *
   * <p>Г„ВҗГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГЎВ»ВҚi khi Seller tГЎВәВЎo phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ mГЎВ»вҖәi (AuctionService.createAuction()).
   *
   * @param auction Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖҳi tГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈng Auction (chГҶВ°a cГғВі id, status = "OPEN")
   * @return Auction Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГғВЎn id tГЎВ»В« database
   */
  public Auction insert(Auction auction) {
    String sql =
        """
        INSERT INTO auctions (
            item_id, starting_price, current_price,
            leading_bidder_id, start_time, end_time,
            status, created_at, updated_at
        ) VALUES (
            :itemId, :startingPrice, :currentPrice,
            :leadingBidderId, :startTime, :endTime,
            :status, :createdAt, :updatedAt
        )
        RETURNING id
        """;

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> {
          long id =
              handle
                  .createQuery(sql)
                  .bind("itemId", auction.getItemId())
                  .bind("startingPrice", auction.getStartingPrice())
                  .bind("currentPrice", auction.getCurrentPrice())
                  .bind("leadingBidderId", auction.getLeadingBidderId())
                  .bind("startTime", auction.getStartTime())
                  .bind("endTime", auction.getEndTime())
                  .bind("status", auction.getStatus())
                  .bind("createdAt", auction.getCreatedAt())
                  .bind("updatedAt", auction.getCreatedAt()) // mГЎВ»вҖәi tГЎВәВЎo, updatedAt = createdAt
                  .mapTo(Long.class)
                  .one();

          auction.setId(id);
          LOGGER.debug("Inserted auction: id={}, itemId={}", id, auction.getItemId());
          return auction;
        });
  }

  // ============================================================
  // READ (SELECT)
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * TГғВ¬m phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ theo ID (SELECT thГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng, khГғВҙng khГғВіa).
   *
   * <p>DГғВ№ng cho cГғВЎc thao tГғВЎc Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҚc thГғВҙng thГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng nhГҶВ°:
   *
   * <ul>
   *   <li>GET /api/auctions/{id} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ xem chi tiГЎВәВҝt phiГғВӘn
   *   <li>KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra phiГғВӘn tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc khi xГғВіa
   * </ul>
   *
   * @param id ID cГЎВ»В§a phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @return Optional chГЎВ»В©a Auction nГЎВәВҝu tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy, Optional.empty() nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng
   */
  public Optional<Auction> findById(Long id) {
    String sql = "SELECT " + SELECT_COLUMNS + " FROM auctions WHERE id = :id";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("id", id).map(new AuctionMapper()).findOne());
  }

  /**
   * TГғВ¬m phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ vГЎВ»вҖәi khГғВіa row (SELECT FOR UPDATE).
   *
   * <p><b>QUAN TRГЎВ»Е’NG:</b> Method nГғВ y phГЎВәВЈi Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГЎВ»ВҚi TRONG TRANSACTION. Row bГЎВ»вҖ№ khГғВіa cho Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn khi
   * transaction COMMIT hoГЎВәВ·c ROLLBACK. CГғВЎc transaction khГғВЎc cГЎВ»вҖҳ gГЎВәВҜng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҚc row nГғВ y sГЎВәВҪ phГЎВәВЈi chГЎВ»Вқ.
   *
   * <p>Г„ВҗГғВўy lГғВ  tГЎВәВ§ng bГЎВәВЈo vГЎВ»вҖЎ thГЎВ»В© 2 cho concurrency (sau synchronized trong BidService).
   *
   * <p><b>VГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ sГЎВ»Вӯ dГЎВ»ВҘng trong transaction:</b>
   *
   * <pre>
   * jdbi.inTransaction(handle -> {
   *     Auction auction = auctionDao.findByIdForUpdate(handle, auctionId);
   *     // xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ bid...
   *     auctionDao.updateInTransaction(handle, auction);
   *     return auction;
   * });
   * </pre>
   *
   * @param handle Handle tГЎВ»В« JDBI transaction (Г„вҖҳГғВЈ mГЎВ»Её transaction)
   * @param id ID cГЎВ»В§a phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @return Auction vГЎВ»вҖәi row Г„вҖҳГғВЈ bГЎВ»вҖ№ khГғВіa (FOR UPDATE)
   * @throws org.jdbi.v3.core.statement.UnableToExecuteStatementException nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy
   */
  public Auction findByIdForUpdate(org.jdbi.v3.core.Handle handle, Long id) {
    String sql = "SELECT " + SELECT_COLUMNS + " FROM auctions WHERE id = :id FOR UPDATE";

    return handle
        .createQuery(sql)
        .bind("id", id)
        .map(new AuctionMapper())
        .one(); // throw exception nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ.
   *
   * <p>DГғВ№ng cho mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh danh sГғВЎch phiГғВӘn (auction-list.fxml).
   *
   * @return List chГЎВ»В©a tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ Auction (sГЎВәВҜp xГЎВәВҝp theo end_time gГЎВәВ§n nhГЎВәВҘt trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc)
   */
  public List<Auction> findAll() {
    String sql = "SELECT " + SELECT_COLUMNS + " FROM auctions ORDER BY end_time ASC";

    return jdbi.withHandle(handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).map(new AuctionMapper()).list());
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy cГғВЎc phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ theo trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi.
   *
   * <p>DГғВ№ng cho:
   *
   * <ul>
   *   <li>AuctionScheduler: tГғВ¬m cГғВЎc phiГғВӘn RUNNING sГЎВәВҜp hГЎВәВҝt giГЎВ»Вқ
   *   <li>Admin Panel: lГЎВ»ВҚc phiГғВӘn theo trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi
   *   <li>Seller: xem phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳang chГЎВәВЎy cГЎВ»В§a mГғВ¬nh
   * </ul>
   *
   * @param status trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi cГЎВәВ§n tГғВ¬m (OPEN, RUNNING, FINISHED, PAID, CANCELED)
   * @return List cГғВЎc Auction cГғВі status tГҶВ°ГҶВЎng ГЎВ»В©ng
   */
  public List<Auction> findByStatus(String status) {
    String sql =
        "SELECT " + SELECT_COLUMNS + " FROM auctions WHERE status = :status ORDER BY end_time ASC";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("status", status).map(new AuctionMapper()).list());
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy cГғВЎc phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt item (sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ nhiГЎВ»ВҒu lГЎВәВ§n).
   *
   * <p>Theo logic, mГЎВ»вҖ”i item chГЎВ»вҖ° nГғВӘn cГғВі 1 phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ, nhГҶВ°ng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ an toГғВ n vГЎВәВ«n hГЎВ»вҖ” trГЎВ»ВЈ lГЎВәВҘy danh sГғВЎch
   * (trong trГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng hГЎВ»ВЈp item Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc Г„вҖҳem Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ lГЎВәВЎi).
   *
   * @param itemId ID cГЎВ»В§a sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m
   * @return List cГғВЎc Auction cГЎВ»В§a item Г„вҖҳГғВі
   */
  public List<Auction> findByItemId(Long itemId) {
    String sql =
        "SELECT "
            + SELECT_COLUMNS
            + " FROM auctions WHERE item_id = :itemId ORDER BY created_at DESC";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("itemId", itemId).map(new AuctionMapper()).list());
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy cГғВЎc phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳang diГЎВ»вҖҰn ra (RUNNING) cho mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh chГғВӯnh.
   *
   * @return List cГғВЎc Auction cГғВі status = "RUNNING" vГғВ  chГҶВ°a hГЎВәВҝt giГЎВ»Вқ
   */
  public List<Auction> findActiveAuctions() {
    String sql =
        "SELECT "
            + SELECT_COLUMNS
            + " FROM auctions WHERE status = 'RUNNING' AND end_time > NOW()"
            + " ORDER BY end_time ASC";

    return jdbi.withHandle(handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).map(new AuctionMapper()).list());
  }

  // ============================================================
  // UPDATE
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * CГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ ГўвӮ¬вҖқ phiГғВӘn bГЎВәВЈn dГғВ№ng trong TRANSACTION.
   *
   * <p>[FIX #5] Г„ВҗГЎВ»вҖўi tГғВӘn tГЎВ»В« {@code update(Handle, Auction)} thГғВ nh {@code updateInTransaction(Handle,
   * Auction)} Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ phГғВўn biГЎВ»вҖЎt rГғВө hГғВ nh vi:
   *
   * <ul>
   *   <li>{@code updateInTransaction} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ <b>throw exception</b> nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy (fail-fast trong
   *       transaction, rollback toГғВ n bГЎВ»в„ў)
   *   <li>{@code update} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ <b>return false</b> nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy (caller tГЎВ»Вұ xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ)
   * </ul>
   *
   * <p>Method nГғВ y Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc dГғВ№ng trong transaction khi cГғВі findByIdForUpdate() trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc Г„вҖҳГғВі.
   *
   * @param handle Handle tГЎВ»В« transaction Г„вҖҳang mГЎВ»Её
   * @param auction Auction Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt (phГЎВәВЈi cГғВі id)
   * @throws IllegalStateException nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy auction ГўвҖ вҖҷ rollback transaction
   */
  public void updateInTransaction(org.jdbi.v3.core.Handle handle, Auction auction) {
    String sql =
        """
        UPDATE auctions
        SET current_price = :currentPrice,
            leading_bidder_id = :leadingBidderId,
            end_time = :endTime,
            status = :status,
            updated_at = :updatedAt
        WHERE id = :id
        """;

    int rowsAffected =
        handle
            .createUpdate(sql)
            .bind("currentPrice", auction.getCurrentPrice())
            .bind("leadingBidderId", auction.getLeadingBidderId())
            .bind("endTime", auction.getEndTime())
            .bind("status", auction.getStatus())
            .bind("updatedAt", LocalDateTime.now())
            .bind("id", auction.getId())
            .execute();

    if (rowsAffected == 0) {
      LOGGER.warn("Auction not found for update in transaction: id={}", auction.getId());
      throw new IllegalStateException("Auction not found: " + auction.getId());
    }
  }

  /**
   * CГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ ГўвӮ¬вҖқ phiГғВӘn bГЎВәВЈn NGOГғвӮ¬I transaction.
   *
   * <p>DГғВ№ng cho cГғВЎc thao tГғВЎc update Г„вҖҳГҶВЎn giГЎВәВЈn khГғВҙng cГЎВәВ§n transaction, vГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ: Admin sГЎВ»Вӯa trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi,
   * AuctionScheduler Г„вҖҳГғВіng phiГғВӘn.
   *
   * @param auction Auction Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt (phГЎВәВЈi cГғВі id)
   */
  public void update(Auction auction) {
    String sql =
        """
        UPDATE auctions
        SET current_price = :currentPrice,
            leading_bidder_id = :leadingBidderId,
            end_time = :endTime,
            status = :status,
            updated_at = :updatedAt
        WHERE id = :id
        """;

    int rowsAffected =
        jdbi.withHandle(
            handle ->
                handle
                    .createUpdate(sql)
                    .bind("currentPrice", auction.getCurrentPrice())
                    .bind("leadingBidderId", auction.getLeadingBidderId())
                    .bind("endTime", auction.getEndTime())
                    .bind("status", auction.getStatus())
                    .bind("updatedAt", LocalDateTime.now())
                    .bind("id", auction.getId())
                    .execute());

    if (rowsAffected > 0) {
      LOGGER.debug(
          "Updated auction: id={}, status={}, price={}",
          auction.getId(),
          auction.getStatus(),
          auction.getCurrentPrice());
    } else {
      LOGGER.warn("Auction not found for update: id={}", auction.getId());
    }
  }

  // ============================================================
  // DELETE
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * XГғВіa phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ.
   *
   * <p>ChГЎВ»вҖ° Admin hoГЎВәВ·c Seller cГЎВ»В§a item mГЎВ»вҖәi cГғВі quyГЎВ»ВҒn xГғВіa phiГғВӘn chГҶВ°a bГЎВәВҜt Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§u.
   *
   * @param id ID cГЎВ»В§a phiГғВӘn cГЎВәВ§n xГғВіa
   * @return true nГЎВәВҝu xГғВіa thГғВ nh cГғВҙng, false nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy
   */
  public void delete(Long id) {
    String sql = "DELETE FROM auctions WHERE id = :id";

    int rowsAffected = jdbi.withHandle(handle -> handle.createUpdate(sql).bind("id", id).execute());

    if (rowsAffected > 0) {
      LOGGER.info("Deleted auction: id={}", id);
    } else {
      LOGGER.warn("Auction not found for deletion: id={}", id);
    }
  }

  /**
   * XГғВіa cГЎВ»В©ng phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ cГғВ№ng toГғВ n bГЎВ»в„ў dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu liГғВӘn quan (bid_transactions, auto_bid_configs).
   * ThГЎВ»Вұc hiГЎВ»вҖЎn trong 1 transaction Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ Г„вҖҳГЎВәВЈm bГЎВәВЈo tГғВӯnh toГғВ n vГЎВәВ№n dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu.
   */
  public void hardDelete(Long id) {
    jdbi.useTransaction(
        handle -> {
          handle
              .createUpdate("DELETE FROM auto_bid_configs WHERE auction_id = :id")
              .bind("id", id)
              .execute();
          handle
              .createUpdate("DELETE FROM bid_transactions WHERE auction_id = :id")
              .bind("id", id)
              .execute();
          handle.createUpdate("DELETE FROM auctions WHERE id = :id").bind("id", id).execute();
        });
    LOGGER.info("Hard-deleted auction: id={}", id);
  }

  // ============================================================
  // HELPER METHODS
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * Г„ВҗГғВіng cГғВЎc phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ Г„вҖҳГғВЈ hГЎВәВҝt hГЎВәВЎn.
   *
   * <p>Г„ВҗГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГЎВ»ВҚi bГЎВ»Еёi AuctionScheduler mГЎВ»вҖ”i phГғВәt Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ chuyГЎВ»Ж’n cГғВЎc phiГғВӘn hГЎВәВҝt hГЎВәВЎn tГЎВ»В« trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi RUNNING
   * sang FINISHED.
   *
   * @return sГЎВ»вҖҳ lГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈng phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc Г„вҖҳГғВіng
   */
  public int closeExpiredAuctions() {
    String sql =
        """
        UPDATE auctions
        SET status = 'FINISHED', updated_at = NOW()
        WHERE status = 'RUNNING' AND end_time <= NOW()
        """;

    int rowsAffected = jdbi.withHandle(handle -> handle.createUpdate(sql).execute());

    if (rowsAffected > 0) {
      LOGGER.info("Closed {} expired auctions", rowsAffected);
    }

    return rowsAffected;
  }

  /**
   * ChuyГЎВ»Ж’n cГғВЎc phiГғВӘn tГЎВ»В« OPEN sang RUNNING khi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn giГЎВ»Вқ bГЎВәВҜt Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§u.
   *
   * <p>Г„ВҗГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГЎВ»ВҚi bГЎВ»Еёi AuctionScheduler mГЎВ»вҖ”i phГғВәt.
   *
   * @return sГЎВ»вҖҳ lГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈng phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc chuyГЎВ»Ж’n sang RUNNING
   */
  public int startScheduledAuctions() {
    String sql =
        """
        UPDATE auctions
        SET status = 'RUNNING', updated_at = NOW()
        WHERE status = 'OPEN' AND start_time <= NOW()
        """;

    int rowsAffected = jdbi.withHandle(handle -> handle.createUpdate(sql).execute());

    if (rowsAffected > 0) {
      LOGGER.info("Started {} scheduled auctions", rowsAffected);
    }

    return rowsAffected;
  }

  /**
   * KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ cГғВі tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi khГғВҙng.
   *
   * @param id ID cГЎВәВ§n kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra
   * @return true nГЎВәВҝu tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi, false nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng
   */
  public boolean existsById(Long id) {
    String sql = "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM auctions WHERE id = :id";

    long count =
        jdbi.withHandle(handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("id", id).mapTo(Long.class).one());

    return count > 0;
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy giГғВЎ hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi cГЎВ»В§a phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ.
   *
   * <p>DГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc khi bid mГғВ  khГғВҙng cГЎВәВ§n load toГғВ n bГЎВ»в„ў Auction.
   *
   * @param id ID cГЎВ»В§a phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @return Optional chГЎВ»В©a giГғВЎ hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi, Optional.empty() nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy
   */
  public Optional<BigDecimal> getCurrentPrice(Long id) {
    String sql = "SELECT current_price FROM auctions WHERE id = :id";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("id", id).mapTo(BigDecimal.class).findOne());
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\dao\AutoBidConfigDao.java ==========
package com.auction.dao;

import com.auction.model.AutoBidConfig;
import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.sql.SQLException;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.Jdbi;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.mapper.RowMapper;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.statement.StatementContext;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * DAO (Data Access Object) cho bГЎВәВЈng auto_bid_configs
 *
 * <p>Class nГғВ y chГЎВ»вҖ№u trГғВЎch nhiГЎВ»вҖЎm quГЎВәВЈn lГғВҪ cГЎВәВҘu hГғВ¬nh Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ tГЎВ»Вұ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng (auto-bid). Auto-bid cho phГғВ©p
 * ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc giГғВЎ tГЎВ»вҖҳi Г„вҖҳa vГғВ  bГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc giГғВЎ, hГЎВ»вҖЎ thГЎВ»вҖҳng sГЎВәВҪ tГЎВ»Вұ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng trГЎВәВЈ giГғВЎ thay hГЎВ»ВҚ khi cГғВі ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi
 * khГғВЎc bid
 *
 * <h3>Vai trГғВІ trong hГЎВ»вҖЎ thГЎВ»вҖҳng</h3>
 *
 * <p>AutoBidConfig lГғВ  mГЎВ»в„ўt phГЎВәВ§n quan trГЎВ»ВҚng cГЎВ»В§a chГЎВ»В©c nГ„Ж’ng nГғВўng cao auto-bidding. MГЎВ»вҖ”i khi cГғВі bid mГЎВ»вҖәi,
 * AutoBidStrategy sГЎВәВҪ:
 *
 * <ol>
 *   <li>LГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ auto-bid configs active cГЎВ»В§a phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГғВі
 *   <li>SГЎВәВҜp xГЎВәВҝp theo registered_at (ai Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc ГҶВ°u tiГғВӘn)
 *   <li>DuyГЎВ»вҖЎt tГЎВ»В«ng config, nГЎВәВҝu cГғВІn budget thГғВ¬ tГЎВ»Вұ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng bid
 *   <li>LГЎВәВ·p lГЎВәВЎi cho Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn khi khГғВҙng cГғВІn ai Г„вҖҳГЎВ»В§ budget
 * </ol>
 *
 * <h3>RГғВ ng buГЎВ»в„ўc UNIQUE</h3>
 *
 * <p>BГЎВәВЈng auto_bid_configs cГғВі constraint UNIQUE(auction_id, bidder_id). Г„ВҗiГЎВ»ВҒu nГғВ y Г„вҖҳГЎВәВЈm bГЎВәВЈo mГЎВ»вҖ”i user
 * chГЎВ»вҖ° cГғВі 1 auto-bid config active cho mГЎВ»вҖ”i phiГғВӘn. Khi user thay Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi maxBid, ta UPDATE thay vГғВ¬ INSERT
 * mГЎВ»вҖәi.
 *
 * <h3>TrГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi active</h3>
 *
 * <p>Auto-bid config cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ bГЎВ»вҖ№ vГғВҙ hiГЎВ»вҖЎu hГғВіa (active = false) trong cГғВЎc trГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng hГЎВ»ВЈp:
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>User chГЎВ»В§ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng tГЎВәВҜt auto-bid
 *   <li>Max bid Г„вҖҳГғВЈ bГЎВ»вҖ№ vГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈt quГғВЎ (hГЎВәВҝt budget)
 *   <li>User Г„вҖҳГғВЈ thГЎВәВҜng phiГғВӘn (khГғВҙng cГЎВәВ§n auto-bid nГЎВ»ВҜa)
 * </ul>
 *
 * <h3>LiГғВӘn kГЎВәВҝt vГЎВ»вҖәi cГғВЎc file khГғВЎc</h3>
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li><b>AutoBidConfig.java</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ model class, chГЎВ»В©a cГЎВәВҘu hГғВ¬nh auto-bid
 *   <li><b>BidService.java</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ gГЎВ»ВҚi DAO Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ lГЎВәВҘy configs khi cГғВі bid mГЎВ»вҖәi
 *   <li><b>AutoBidStrategy.java</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ dГғВ№ng PriorityQueue vГғВ  DAO Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ
 *   <li><b>V1__initial_schema.sql</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖ№nh nghГ„В©a bГЎВәВЈng auto_bid_configs
 * </ul>
 */
public class AutoBidConfigDao {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(AutoBidConfigDao.class);

  /** Danh sГғВЎch cГЎВ»в„ўt SELECT dГғВ№ng chung, trГғВЎnh copy-paste. [FIX #10] */
  private static final String SELECT_COLUMNS =
      "id, auction_id, bidder_id, max_bid, increment_amount, active, registered_at";

  private final Jdbi jdbi;

  public AutoBidConfigDao(Jdbi jdbi) {
    this.jdbi = jdbi;
  }

  /**
   * RowMapper chuyГЎВ»Ж’n ResultSet thГғВ nh AutoBidConfig object.
   *
   * <p>[FIX #11] BГЎВәВЈng auto_bid_configs khГғВҙng cГғВі cГЎВ»в„ўt created_at riГғВӘng. Thay vГғВ o Г„вҖҳГғВі dГғВ№ng
   * registered_at lГғВ m timestamp chuГЎВәВ©n. NГЎВәВҝu model Entity base class yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u createdAt, hГғВЈy override
   * getCreatedAt() trong AutoBidConfig.java trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ registeredAt Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ trГғВЎnh hack ГЎВ»Её DAO layer.
   *
   * <p>Map cГғВЎc cГЎВ»в„ўt trong bГЎВәВЈng auto_bid_configs:
   *
   * <pre>
   * | id | auction_id | bidder_id | max_bid | increment_amount | active | registered_at |
   * </pre>
   */
