  private static class AutoBidConfigMapper implements RowMapper<AutoBidConfig> {
    @Override
    public AutoBidConfig map(ResultSet rs, StatementContext ctx) throws SQLException {
      var registeredAt = rs.getTimestamp("registered_at").toLocalDateTime();

      // [FIX #11] TruyГЎВ»ВҒn registeredAt cho cГЎВәВЈ hai: registeredAt VГғвӮ¬ createdAt.
      // LГғВҪ do: bГЎВәВЈng auto_bid_configs chГЎВ»вҖ° cГғВі registered_at, khГғВҙng cГғВі created_at.
      // Recommend: thГғВӘm method getCreatedAt() trong AutoBidConfig override
      // trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ registeredAt ГўвҖ вҖҷ loГЎВәВЎi bГЎВ»ВҸ hoГғВ n toГғВ n tham sГЎВ»вҖҳ createdAt ГЎВ»Её Г„вҖҳГғВўy.
      return new AutoBidConfig(
          rs.getLong("id"),
          rs.getLong("auction_id"),
          rs.getLong("bidder_id"),
          rs.getBigDecimal("max_bid"),
          rs.getBigDecimal("increment_amount"),
          rs.getBoolean("active"),
          registeredAt,
          registeredAt // createdAt = registeredAt (bГЎВәВЈng khГғВҙng cГғВі cГЎВ»в„ўt created_at)
          );
    }
  }

  // ============================================================
  // CREATE (INSERT)
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * TГЎВәВЎo cГЎВәВҘu hГғВ¬nh auto-bid mГЎВ»вҖәi.
   *
   * <p>Г„ВҗГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГЎВ»ВҚi khi ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng bГЎВәВӯt auto-bid cho mГЎВ»в„ўt phiГғВӘn.
   *
   * <p><b>LГҶВ°u ГғВҪ:</b> NГЎВәВҝu user Г„вҖҳГғВЈ cГғВі config cho phiГғВӘn nГғВ y (do UNIQUE constraint), INSERT sГЎВәВҪ thГЎВәВҘt
   * bГЎВәВЎi. Trong trГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng hГЎВ»ВЈp Г„вҖҳГғВі, nГғВӘn gГЎВ»ВҚi update() Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt.
   *
   * @param config AutoBidConfig cГЎВәВ§n tГЎВәВЎo (chГҶВ°a cГғВі id)
   * @return AutoBidConfig Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГғВЎn id tГЎВ»В« database
   * @throws org.jdbi.v3.core.statement.UnableToExecuteStatementException nГЎВәВҝu vi phГЎВәВЎm UNIQUE
   *     constraint (user Г„вҖҳГғВЈ cГғВі config cho auction nГғВ y)
   */
  public AutoBidConfig insert(AutoBidConfig config) {
    String sql =
        """
        INSERT INTO auto_bid_configs
            (auction_id, bidder_id, max_bid, increment_amount, active, registered_at)
        VALUES
            (:auctionId, :bidderId, :maxBid, :increment, :active, :registeredAt)
        RETURNING id
        """;

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> {
          long id =
              handle
                  .createQuery(sql)
                  .bind("auctionId", config.getAuctionId())
                  .bind("bidderId", config.getBidderId())
                  .bind("maxBid", config.getMaxBid())
                  .bind("increment", config.getIncrement())
                  .bind("active", config.isActive())
                  .bind("registeredAt", config.getRegisteredAt())
                  .mapTo(Long.class)
                  .one();

          config.setId(id);
          LOGGER.debug(
              "Inserted auto-bid config: auction={}, bidder={}, max={}",
              config.getAuctionId(),
              config.getBidderId(),
              config.getMaxBid());
          return config;
        });
  }

  // ============================================================
  // READ (SELECT)
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * TГғВ¬m cГЎВәВҘu hГғВ¬nh auto-bid theo ID.
   *
   * @param id ID cГЎВ»В§a cГЎВәВҘu hГғВ¬nh
   * @return Optional chГЎВ»В©a AutoBidConfig nГЎВәВҝu tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy
   */
  public Optional<AutoBidConfig> findById(Long id) {
    String sql = "SELECT " + SELECT_COLUMNS + " FROM auto_bid_configs WHERE id = :id";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("id", id).map(new AutoBidConfigMapper()).findOne());
  }

  /**
   * TГғВ¬m cГЎВәВҘu hГғВ¬nh auto-bid cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt user trong mГЎВ»в„ўt phiГғВӘn.
   *
   * <p>Method nГғВ y quan trГЎВ»ВҚng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’:
   *
   * <ul>
   *   <li>KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra user Г„вҖҳГғВЈ cГғВі auto-bid cho phiГғВӘn nГғВ y chГҶВ°a
   *   <li>LГЎВәВҘy config Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt khi user thay Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi maxBid
   *   <li>KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi active cГЎВ»В§a auto-bid user
   * </ul>
   *
   * @param auctionId ID phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @param bidderId ID ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @return Optional chГЎВ»В©a AutoBidConfig nГЎВәВҝu tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi
   */
  public Optional<AutoBidConfig> findByAuctionAndBidder(Long auctionId, Long bidderId) {
    String sql =
        "SELECT "
            + SELECT_COLUMNS
            + " FROM auto_bid_configs WHERE auction_id = :auctionId AND bidder_id = :bidderId";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle ->
            handle
                .createQuery(sql)
                .bind("auctionId", auctionId)
                .bind("bidderId", bidderId)
                .map(new AutoBidConfigMapper())
                .findOne());
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ auto-bid configs active cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt phiГғВӘn.
   *
   * <p><b>QUAN TRГЎВ»Е’NG:</b> Method nГғВ y Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc AutoBidStrategy gГЎВ»ВҚi mГЎВ»вҖ”i khi cГғВі bid mГЎВ»вҖәi. KГЎВәВҝt quГЎВәВЈ trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ
   * sГЎВәВҜp xГЎВәВҝp theo registered_at (ai Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc ГҶВ°u tiГғВӘn).
   *
   * @param auctionId ID phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @return List cГғВЎc AutoBidConfig active, sГЎВәВҜp xГЎВәВҝp theo thГЎВ»Вқi gian Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ
   */
  public List<AutoBidConfig> findActiveByAuctionId(Long auctionId) {
    String sql =
        "SELECT "
            + SELECT_COLUMNS
            + " FROM auto_bid_configs"
            + " WHERE auction_id = :auctionId AND active = true"
            + " ORDER BY registered_at ASC";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle ->
            handle
                .createQuery(sql)
                .bind("auctionId", auctionId)
                .map(new AutoBidConfigMapper())
                .list());
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ auto-bid configs cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt user (xuyГғВӘn suГЎВ»вҖҳt cГғВЎc phiГғВӘn).
   *
   * <p>DГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ hiГЎВ»Ж’n thГЎВ»вҖ№ trong User Profile: "CГғВЎc phiГғВӘn bГЎВәВЎn Г„вҖҳang auto-bid".
   *
   * @param bidderId ID ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @return List cГғВЎc AutoBidConfig cГЎВ»В§a user Г„вҖҳГғВі
   */
  public List<AutoBidConfig> findByBidderId(Long bidderId) {
    String sql =
        "SELECT "
            + SELECT_COLUMNS
            + " FROM auto_bid_configs WHERE bidder_id = :bidderId ORDER BY registered_at DESC";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle ->
            handle
                .createQuery(sql)
                .bind("bidderId", bidderId)
                .map(new AutoBidConfigMapper())
                .list());
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ auto-bid configs cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt phiГғВӘn (kГЎВ»Ж’ cГЎВәВЈ inactive).
   *
   * <p>DГғВ№ng cho Admin Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ xem lГЎВ»вҖ№ch sГЎВ»Вӯ auto-bid cГЎВ»В§a phiГғВӘn.
   *
   * @param auctionId ID phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @return List tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ AutoBidConfig cГЎВ»В§a phiГғВӘn
   */
  public List<AutoBidConfig> findAllByAuctionId(Long auctionId) {
    String sql =
        "SELECT "
            + SELECT_COLUMNS
            + " FROM auto_bid_configs WHERE auction_id = :auctionId ORDER BY registered_at ASC";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle ->
            handle
                .createQuery(sql)
                .bind("auctionId", auctionId)
                .map(new AutoBidConfigMapper())
                .list());
  }

  // ============================================================
  // UPDATE
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * CГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt cГЎВәВҘu hГғВ¬nh auto-bid.
   *
   * <p>DГғВ№ng khi:
   *
   * <ul>
   *   <li>User thay Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi maxBid hoГЎВәВ·c increment
   *   <li>User tГЎВәВҜt auto-bid (set active = false)
   *   <li>HГЎВ»вҖЎ thГЎВ»вҖҳng vГғВҙ hiГЎВ»вҖЎu hГғВіa auto-bid khi hГЎВәВҝt budget
   * </ul>
   *
   * @param config AutoBidConfig Г„вҖҳГғВЈ cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt (phГЎВәВЈi cГғВі id)
   * @return true nГЎВәВҝu cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt thГғВ nh cГғВҙng, false nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy
   */
  public boolean update(AutoBidConfig config) {
    String sql =
        """
        UPDATE auto_bid_configs
        SET max_bid = :maxBid,
            increment_amount = :increment,
            active = :active
        WHERE id = :id
        """;

    int rowsAffected =
        jdbi.withHandle(
            handle ->
                handle
                    .createUpdate(sql)
                    .bind("maxBid", config.getMaxBid())
                    .bind("increment", config.getIncrement())
                    .bind("active", config.isActive())
                    .bind("id", config.getId())
                    .execute());

    if (rowsAffected > 0) {
      LOGGER.debug(
          "Updated auto-bid config: id={}, active={}, max={}",
          config.getId(),
          config.isActive(),
          config.getMaxBid());
      return true;
    }

    LOGGER.warn("Auto-bid config not found for update: id={}", config.getId());
    return false;
  }

  /**
   * CГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt cГЎВәВҘu hГғВ¬nh auto-bid theo auctionId vГғВ  bidderId.
   *
   * <p>Method nГғВ y hГЎВ»ВҜu ГғВӯch khi khГғВҙng cГғВі id config (chГЎВ»вҖ° biГЎВәВҝt auction vГғВ  user).
   *
   * @param auctionId ID phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @param bidderId ID ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @param maxBid giГғВЎ tГЎВ»вҖҳi Г„вҖҳa mГЎВ»вҖәi
   * @param increment bГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc giГғВЎ mГЎВ»вҖәi
   * @param active trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi active mГЎВ»вҖәi
   * @return true nГЎВәВҝu cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt thГғВ nh cГғВҙng, false nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy config
   */
  public boolean updateByAuctionAndBidder(
      Long auctionId, Long bidderId, BigDecimal maxBid, BigDecimal increment, boolean active) {
    String sql =
        """
        UPDATE auto_bid_configs
        SET max_bid = :maxBid,
            increment_amount = :increment,
            active = :active
        WHERE auction_id = :auctionId AND bidder_id = :bidderId
        """;

    int rowsAffected =
        jdbi.withHandle(
            handle ->
                handle
                    .createUpdate(sql)
                    .bind("maxBid", maxBid)
                    .bind("increment", increment)
                    .bind("active", active)
                    .bind("auctionId", auctionId)
                    .bind("bidderId", bidderId)
                    .execute());

    if (rowsAffected > 0) {
      LOGGER.debug(
          "Updated auto-bid config: auction={}, bidder={}, active={}, max={}",
          auctionId,
          bidderId,
          active,
          maxBid);
      return true;
    }

    return false;
  }

  /**
   * VГғВҙ hiГЎВ»вҖЎu hГғВіa auto-bid cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt user trong mГЎВ»в„ўt phiГғВӘn.
   *
   * <p>Г„ВҗГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГЎВ»ВҚi khi:
   *
   * <ul>
   *   <li>User tГЎВәВҜt auto-bid
   *   <li>Auto-bid hГЎВәВҝt budget (maxBid Г„вҖҳГғВЈ bГЎВ»вҖ№ vГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈt)
   *   <li>User thГЎВәВҜng phiГғВӘn (khГғВҙng cГЎВәВ§n auto-bid nГЎВ»ВҜa)
   *   <li>PhiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ kГЎВәВҝt thГғВәc
   * </ul>
   *
   * @param auctionId ID phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @param bidderId ID ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @return true nГЎВәВҝu vГғВҙ hiГЎВ»вҖЎu hГғВіa thГғВ nh cГғВҙng, false nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy config
   */
  public boolean deactivate(Long auctionId, Long bidderId) {
    String sql =
        """
        UPDATE auto_bid_configs
        SET active = false
        WHERE auction_id = :auctionId AND bidder_id = :bidderId AND active = true
        """;

    int rowsAffected =
        jdbi.withHandle(
            handle ->
                handle
                    .createUpdate(sql)
                    .bind("auctionId", auctionId)
                    .bind("bidderId", bidderId)
                    .execute());

    if (rowsAffected > 0) {
      LOGGER.info("Deactivated auto-bid: auction={}, bidder={}", auctionId, bidderId);
      return true;
    }

    return false;
  }

  /**
   * VГғВҙ hiГЎВ»вҖЎu hГғВіa tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ auto-bid configs cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt phiГғВӘn.
   *
   * <p>Г„ВҗГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГЎВ»ВҚi khi phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ kГЎВәВҝt thГғВәc (FINISHED hoГЎВәВ·c CANCELED).
   *
   * @param auctionId ID phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @return sГЎВ»вҖҳ lГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈng configs bГЎВ»вҖ№ vГғВҙ hiГЎВ»вҖЎu hГғВіa
   */
  public int deactivateAllByAuctionId(Long auctionId) {
    String sql =
        """
        UPDATE auto_bid_configs
        SET active = false
        WHERE auction_id = :auctionId AND active = true
        """;

    int rowsAffected =
        jdbi.withHandle(handle -> handle.createUpdate(sql).bind("auctionId", auctionId).execute());

    if (rowsAffected > 0) {
      LOGGER.info("Deactivated {} auto-bid configs for auction: {}", rowsAffected, auctionId);
    }

    return rowsAffected;
  }

  // ============================================================
  // DELETE (ChГЎВ»вҖ° dГғВ№ng cho test)
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * XГғВіa cГЎВәВҘu hГғВ¬nh auto-bid theo ID.
   *
   * <p><b>CHГЎВ»ЛҶ DГғв„ўNG CHO TEST.</b> KhГғВҙng gГЎВ»ВҚi method nГғВ y trong production. Trong production, chГЎВ»вҖ° cГЎВәВӯp
   * nhГЎВәВӯt active = false, khГғВҙng xГғВіa.
   *
   * @param id ID cГЎВ»В§a cГЎВәВҘu hГғВ¬nh cГЎВәВ§n xГғВіa
   * @return true nГЎВәВҝu xГғВіa thГғВ nh cГғВҙng
   */
  public boolean deleteById(Long id) {
    String sql = "DELETE FROM auto_bid_configs WHERE id = :id";

    int rowsAffected = jdbi.withHandle(handle -> handle.createUpdate(sql).bind("id", id).execute());

    return rowsAffected > 0;
  }

  /**
   * XГғВіa tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ auto-bid configs cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt phiГғВӘn.
   *
   * <p><b>CHГЎВ»ЛҶ DГғв„ўNG CHO TEST.</b>
   *
   * @param auctionId ID phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @return sГЎВ»вҖҳ lГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈng configs bГЎВ»вҖ№ xГғВіa
   */
  public int deleteByAuctionId(Long auctionId) {
    String sql = "DELETE FROM auto_bid_configs WHERE auction_id = :auctionId";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> handle.createUpdate(sql).bind("auctionId", auctionId).execute());
  }

  // ============================================================
  // HELPER METHODS
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra user Г„вҖҳГғВЈ cГғВі auto-bid config active cho phiГғВӘn nГғВ y chГҶВ°a.
   *
   * @param auctionId ID phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @param bidderId ID ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @return true nГЎВәВҝu Г„вҖҳГғВЈ cГғВі config active
   */
  public boolean hasActiveConfig(Long auctionId, Long bidderId) {
    String sql =
        """
        SELECT COUNT(*) FROM auto_bid_configs
        WHERE auction_id = :auctionId AND bidder_id = :bidderId AND active = true
        """;

    long count =
        jdbi.withHandle(
            handle ->
                handle
                    .createQuery(sql)
                    .bind("auctionId", auctionId)
                    .bind("bidderId", bidderId)
                    .mapTo(Long.class)
                    .one());

    return count > 0;
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy sГЎВ»вҖҳ lГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈng auto-bid configs active cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt phiГғВӘn.
   *
   * @param auctionId ID phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @return sГЎВ»вҖҳ lГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈng configs active
   */
  public int countActiveByAuctionId(Long auctionId) {
    String sql =
        """
        SELECT COUNT(*) FROM auto_bid_configs
        WHERE auction_id = :auctionId AND active = true
        """;

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("auctionId", auctionId).mapTo(Integer.class).one());
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\dao\BidTransactionDao.java ==========
package com.auction.dao;

import com.auction.model.BidTransaction;
import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.sql.SQLException;
import java.time.LocalDateTime;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.Jdbi;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.mapper.RowMapper;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.statement.StatementContext;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * DAO (Data Access Object) cho bГЎВәВЈng bid_transactions
 *
 * <p>Class nГғВ y chГЎВ»вҖ№u trГғВЎch nhiГЎВ»вҖЎm ghi lГЎВәВЎi lГЎВ»вҖ№ch sГЎВ»Вӯ Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ vГғВ o bГЎВәВЈng bid_transactions. BidTransaction
 * lГғВ  dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu bГЎВәВҘt biГЎВәВҝn (append-only) ГўвӮ¬вҖқ chГЎВ»вҖ° INSERT, khГғВҙng UPDATE hay DELETE. Г„ВҗiГЎВ»ВҒu nГғВ y Г„вҖҳГЎВәВЈm bГЎВәВЈo tГғВӯnh
 * minh bГЎВәВЎch vГғВ  khГЎВәВЈ nГ„Ж’ng kiГЎВ»Ж’m toГғВЎn (audit trail) cГЎВ»В§a hГЎВ»вҖЎ thГЎВ»вҖҳng
 *
 * <h3>Vai trГғВІ trong hГЎВ»вҖЎ thГЎВ»вҖҳng</h3>
 *
 * <p>MГЎВ»вҖ”i khi cГғВі mГЎВ»в„ўt bid thГғВ nh cГғВҙng (thГЎВ»В§ cГғВҙng hoГЎВәВ·c auto-bid), hГЎВ»вҖЎ thГЎВ»вҖҳng ghi lГЎВәВЎi:
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>Ai Г„вҖҳГғВЈ bid (bidderId)
 *   <li>PhiГғВӘn nГғВ o (auctionId)
 *   <li>GiГғВЎ bao nhiГғВӘu (amount)
 *   <li>LГғВәc nГғВ o (created_at)
 *   <li>LГғВ  auto-bid hay thГЎВ»В§ cГғВҙng (auto_bid flag)
 * </ul>
 *
 * <h3>ГЎВ»ВЁng dГЎВ»ВҘng cГЎВ»В§a bid history</h3>
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li><b>Bid History Chart:</b> LГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ bid cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ vГЎВәВҪ biГЎВ»Ж’u Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖң Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng (trГЎВ»ВҘc X = thГЎВ»Вқi
 *       gian, trГЎВ»ВҘc Y = giГғВЎ)
 *   <li><b>XГғВЎc Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖ№nh ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi thГЎВәВҜng:</b> TГғВ¬m bid cuГЎВ»вҖҳi cГғВ№ng (giГғВЎ cao nhГЎВәВҘt) cГЎВ»В§a phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГғВЈ kГЎВәВҝt thГғВәc
 *   <li><b>Audit trail:</b> NГЎВәВҝu cГғВі tranh chГЎВәВҘp, cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ xem lГЎВәВЎi toГғВ n bГЎВ»в„ў lГЎВ»вҖ№ch sГЎВ»Вӯ
 *   <li><b>ThГЎВ»вҖҳng kГғВӘ:</b> Г„ВҗГЎВәВҝm sГЎВ»вҖҳ bid cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»вҖ”i user, phГғВўn tГғВӯch hГғВ nh vi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
 * </ul>
 *
 * <h3>LiГғВӘn kГЎВәВҝt vГЎВ»вҖәi cГғВЎc file khГғВЎc</h3>
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li><b>BidTransaction.java</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ model class, chГЎВ»В©a dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu mГЎВ»в„ўt bid
 *   <li><b>BidService.java</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ gГЎВ»ВҚi insert() sau mГЎВ»вҖ”i bid thГғВ nh cГғВҙng
 *   <li><b>AuctionController.java</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ gГЎВ»ВҚi findByAuctionId() cho Bid History Chart
 *   <li><b>V1__initial_schema.sql</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖ№nh nghГ„В©a bГЎВәВЈng bid_transactions
 * </ul>
 */
public class BidTransactionDao {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(BidTransactionDao.class);

  /** Danh sГғВЎch cГЎВ»в„ўt SELECT dГғВ№ng chung, trГғВЎnh copy-paste. [FIX #10] */
  private static final String SELECT_COLUMNS =
      "id, auction_id, bidder_id, amount, auto_bid, created_at";

  private final Jdbi jdbi;

  public BidTransactionDao(Jdbi jdbi) {
    this.jdbi = jdbi;
  }

  /**
   * RowMapper chuyГЎВ»Ж’n ResultSet thГғВ nh BidTransaction object.
   *
   * <p>Map cГғВЎc cГЎВ»в„ўt trong bГЎВәВЈng bid_transactions:
   *
   * <pre>
   * | id | auction_id | bidder_id | amount | auto_bid | created_at |
   * </pre>
   */
  private static class BidTransactionMapper implements RowMapper<BidTransaction> {
    @Override
    public BidTransaction map(ResultSet rs, StatementContext ctx) throws SQLException {
      return new BidTransaction(
          rs.getLong("id"),
          rs.getLong("auction_id"),
          rs.getLong("bidder_id"),
          rs.getBigDecimal("amount"),
          rs.getBoolean("auto_bid"),
          rs.getTimestamp("created_at").toLocalDateTime());
    }
  }

  // ============================================================
  // CREATE (INSERT) ГўвӮ¬вҖқ ChГЎВ»вҖ° cГғВі insert, khГғВҙng update/delete
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * Ghi lГЎВәВЎi mГЎВ»в„ўt bid thГғВ nh cГғВҙng vГғВ o database (phiГғВӘn bГЎВәВЈn TRONG TRANSACTION).
   *
   * <p>Method nГғВ y Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГЎВ»ВҚi sau khi BidService Г„вҖҳГғВЈ validate vГғВ  cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt auction. NГғВі Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГЎВ»ВҚi TRONG
   * CГғв„ўNG TRANSACTION vГЎВ»вҖәi auction update Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ Г„вҖҳГЎВәВЈm bГЎВәВЈo consistency.
   *
   * <p>VГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ transaction trong BidService:
   *
   * <pre>
   * jdbi.inTransaction(handle -> {
   *     Auction auction = auctionDao.findByIdForUpdate(handle, auctionId);
   *     // validate vГғВ  update auction...
   *     auctionDao.updateInTransaction(handle, auction);
   *
   *     // Ghi bid transaction trong cГғВ№ng transaction
   *     bidTransactionDao.insert(handle, new BidTransaction(...));
   *
   *     return auction;
   * });
   * </pre>
   *
   * @param handle Handle tГЎВ»В« transaction Г„вҖҳang mГЎВ»Её (Г„вҖҳГғВЈ cГғВі connection)
   * @param transaction BidTransaction cГЎВәВ§n ghi (chГҶВ°a cГғВі id)
   * @return BidTransaction Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГғВЎn id tГЎВ»В« database
   */
  public BidTransaction insert(org.jdbi.v3.core.Handle handle, BidTransaction transaction) {
    String sql =
        """
        INSERT INTO bid_transactions (auction_id, bidder_id, amount, auto_bid, created_at)
        VALUES (:auctionId, :bidderId, :amount, :autoBid, :createdAt)
        RETURNING id
        """;

    long id =
        handle
            .createQuery(sql)
            .bind("auctionId", transaction.getAuctionId())
            .bind("bidderId", transaction.getBidderId())
            .bind("amount", transaction.getAmount())
            .bind("autoBid", transaction.isAutoBid())
            .bind("createdAt", transaction.getCreatedAt())
            .mapTo(Long.class)
            .one();

    transaction.setId(id);
    LOGGER.debug(
        "Inserted bid transaction: auction={}, bidder={}, amount={}, auto={}",
        transaction.getAuctionId(),
        transaction.getBidderId(),
        transaction.getAmount(),
        transaction.isAutoBid());

    return transaction;
  }

  /**
   * Ghi lГЎВәВЎi mГЎВ»в„ўt bid thГғВ nh cГғВҙng (phiГғВӘn bГЎВәВЈn NGOГғвӮ¬I transaction, tГЎВәВЎo connection riГғВӘng)
   *
   * <p>DГғВ№ng cho cГғВЎc trГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng hГЎВ»ВЈp khГғВҙng cГЎВәВ§n transaction vГЎВ»вҖәi auction update, vГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ: khi insert bid
   * history cho mГЎВ»ВҘc Г„вҖҳГғВӯch logging khГғВҙng critical
   *
   * @param transaction BidTransaction cГЎВәВ§n ghi
   */
  public void insert(BidTransaction transaction) {
    String sql =
        """
        INSERT INTO bid_transactions (auction_id, bidder_id, amount, auto_bid, created_at)
        VALUES (:auctionId, :bidderId, :amount, :autoBid, :createdAt)
        RETURNING id
        """;

    jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> {
          long id =
              handle
                  .createQuery(sql)
                  .bind("auctionId", transaction.getAuctionId())
                  .bind("bidderId", transaction.getBidderId())
                  .bind("amount", transaction.getAmount())
                  .bind("autoBid", transaction.isAutoBid())
                  .bind("createdAt", transaction.getCreatedAt())
                  .mapTo(Long.class)
                  .one();

          transaction.setId(id);
          LOGGER.debug(
              "Inserted bid transaction: auction={}, bidder={}, amount={}",
              transaction.getAuctionId(),
              transaction.getBidderId(),
              transaction.getAmount());

          return null;
        });
  }

  // ============================================================
  // READ (SELECT)
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ bid transactions cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ.
   *
   * <p><b>QUAN TRГЎВ»Е’NG:</b> Method nГғВ y Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc dГғВ№ng cho Bid History Chart. KГЎВәВҝt quГЎВәВЈ trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ sГЎВәВҜp xГЎВәВҝp theo
   * thГЎВ»Вқi gian tГ„Ж’ng dГЎВәВ§n (tГЎВ»В« cГ…В© Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn mГЎВ»вҖәi) Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ vГЎВәВҪ biГЎВ»Ж’u Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖң Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng (line chart) vГЎВ»вҖәi trГЎВ»ВҘc X = thГЎВ»Вқi gian.
   *
   * @param auctionId ID cГЎВ»В§a phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @return List cГғВЎc BidTransaction sГЎВәВҜp xГЎВәВҝp theo thГЎВ»Вқi gian (cГ…В© ГўвҖ вҖҷ mГЎВ»вҖәi)
   */
  public List<BidTransaction> findByAuctionId(Long auctionId) {
    String sql =
        "SELECT "
            + SELECT_COLUMNS
            + " FROM bid_transactions WHERE auction_id = :auctionId ORDER BY created_at ASC";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle ->
            handle
                .createQuery(sql)
                .bind("auctionId", auctionId)
                .map(new BidTransactionMapper())
                .list());
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ bid transactions cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng.
   *
   * <p>DГғВ№ng cho:
   *
   * <ul>
   *   <li>User profile: hiГЎВ»Ж’n thГЎВ»вҖ№ lГЎВ»вҖ№ch sГЎВ»Вӯ Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ cГЎВ»В§a bidder
   *   <li>ThГЎВ»вҖҳng kГғВӘ: Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝm sГЎВ»вҖҳ lГЎВәВ§n bid cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»вҖ”i user
   * </ul>
   *
   * @param bidderId ID cГЎВ»В§a ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @return List cГғВЎc BidTransaction sГЎВәВҜp xГЎВәВҝp theo thГЎВ»Вқi gian (mГЎВ»вҖәi ГўвҖ вҖҷ cГ…В©)
   */
  public List<BidTransaction> findByBidderId(Long bidderId) {
    String sql =
        "SELECT "
            + SELECT_COLUMNS
            + " FROM bid_transactions WHERE bidder_id = :bidderId ORDER BY created_at DESC";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle ->
            handle
                .createQuery(sql)
                .bind("bidderId", bidderId)
                .map(new BidTransactionMapper())
                .list());
  }

  /**
   * TГғВ¬m bid transaction theo ID.
   *
   * <p>DГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra bid transaction cГЎВ»ВҘ thГЎВ»Ж’, phГЎВ»ВҘc vГЎВ»ВҘ test vГғВ  debug.
   *
   * @param id ID cГЎВ»В§a bid transaction
   * @return Optional chГЎВ»В©a BidTransaction nГЎВәВҝu tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy, Optional.empty() nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng
   */
  public Optional<BidTransaction> findById(Long id) {
    String sql = "SELECT " + SELECT_COLUMNS + " FROM bid_transactions WHERE id = :id";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("id", id).map(new BidTransactionMapper()).findOne());
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy bid cuГЎВ»вҖҳi cГғВ№ng (giГғВЎ cao nhГЎВәВҘt) cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ.
   *
   * <p>DГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ xГғВЎc Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖ№nh ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi thГЎВәВҜng khi phiГғВӘn kГЎВәВҝt thГғВәc.
   *
   * <p>[FIX #7] Order by cГЎВәВЈ amount DESC lГЎВәВ«n created_at DESC. TrГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc Г„вҖҳГғВўy chГЎВ»вҖ° order by created_at ГўвҖ вҖҷ
   * edge case khi auto-bid xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ nhanh, 2 bids cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ cГғВ№ng created_at (precision Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn millisecond).
   * ThГғВӘm amount DESC Г„вҖҳГЎВәВЈm bГЎВәВЈo luГғВҙn lГЎВәВҘy bid giГғВЎ cao nhГЎВәВҘt.
   *
   * @param auctionId ID cГЎВ»В§a phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @return Optional chГЎВ»В©a BidTransaction cuГЎВ»вҖҳi cГғВ№ng, Optional.empty() nГЎВәВҝu chГҶВ°a cГғВі bid nГғВ o
   */
  public Optional<BidTransaction> findLastBid(Long auctionId) {
    String sql =
        "SELECT "
            + SELECT_COLUMNS
            + " FROM bid_transactions WHERE auction_id = :auctionId"
            + " ORDER BY amount DESC, created_at DESC LIMIT 1";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle ->
            handle
                .createQuery(sql)
                .bind("auctionId", auctionId)
                .map(new BidTransactionMapper())
                .findOne());
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ bid transactions cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt phiГғВӘn, kГғВЁm thГғВҙng tin username cГЎВ»В§a bidder.
   *
   * <p>Method nГғВ y JOIN vГЎВ»вҖәi bГЎВәВЈng users Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ lГЎВәВҘy username, giГғВәp client hiГЎВ»Ж’n thГЎВ»вҖ№ tГғВӘn ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi bid trГғВӘn
   * chart mГғВ  khГғВҙng cГЎВәВ§n gГЎВ»ВҚi thГғВӘm API.
   *
   * @param auctionId ID cГЎВ»В§a phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @return List cГғВЎc BidHistoryEntry chГЎВ»В©a BidTransaction + username
   */
  public List<BidHistoryEntry> findWithUsernames(Long auctionId) {
    String sql =
        """
        SELECT bt.id, bt.auction_id, bt.bidder_id, bt.amount, bt.auto_bid, bt.created_at,
               u.username
        FROM bid_transactions bt
        JOIN users u ON bt.bidder_id = u.id
        WHERE bt.auction_id = :auctionId
        ORDER BY bt.created_at ASC
        """;

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle ->
            handle
                .createQuery(sql)
                .bind("auctionId", auctionId)
                .map(
                    (rs, ctx) -> {
                      BidTransaction tx =
                          new BidTransaction(
                              rs.getLong("id"),
                              rs.getLong("auction_id"),
                              rs.getLong("bidder_id"),
                              rs.getBigDecimal("amount"),
                              rs.getBoolean("auto_bid"),
                              rs.getTimestamp("created_at").toLocalDateTime());
                      String username = rs.getString("username");
                      return new BidHistoryEntry(tx, username);
                    })
                .list());
  }

  /**
   * Г„ВҗГЎВәВҝm sГЎВ»вҖҳ lГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈng bid trong mГЎВ»в„ўt phiГғВӘn.
   *
   * <p>DГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ hiГЎВ»Ж’n thГЎВ»вҖ№ thГЎВ»вҖҳng kГғВӘ (vГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ: "Г„ВҗГғВЈ cГғВі 15 lГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈt Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ").
   *
   * @param auctionId ID cГЎВ»В§a phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @return sГЎВ»вҖҳ lГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈng bid transactions
   */
  public int countByAuctionId(Long auctionId) {
    String sql = "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM bid_transactions WHERE auction_id = :auctionId";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("auctionId", auctionId).mapTo(Integer.class).one());
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy giГғВЎ cao nhГЎВәВҘt cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt phiГғВӘn (cГ…В©ng chГғВӯnh lГғВ  giГғВЎ cuГЎВ»вҖҳi cГғВ№ng).
   *
   * <p>DГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra nhanh mГғВ  khГғВҙng cГЎВәВ§n load toГғВ n bГЎВ»в„ў auction.
   *
   * @param auctionId ID cГЎВ»В§a phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @return Optional chГЎВ»В©a giГғВЎ cao nhГЎВәВҘt, Optional.empty() nГЎВәВҝu chГҶВ°a cГғВі bid nГғВ o
   */
  public Optional<BigDecimal> getHighestPrice(Long auctionId) {
    String sql =
        """
        SELECT amount
        FROM bid_transactions
        WHERE auction_id = :auctionId
        ORDER BY amount DESC
        LIMIT 1
        """;

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle ->
            handle.createQuery(sql).bind("auctionId", auctionId).mapTo(BigDecimal.class).findOne());
  }

  // ============================================================
  // HELPER ГўвӮ¬вҖқ BidHistoryEntry record
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * DTO helper cho bid history kГғВЁm username.
   *
   * <p>[FIX #12] Г„ВҗГЎВ»вҖўi tГЎВ»В« inner class thГғВ nh Java 21 record ГўвӮ¬вҖқ gГЎВ»ВҚn hГҶВЎn, immutable, tГЎВ»Вұ sinh
   * equals/hashCode/toString. Г„ВҗГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc dГғВ№ng trong {@code findWithUsernames()}.
   *
   * <p><b>CГғВўn nhГЎВәВҜc:</b> NГЎВәВҝu muГЎВ»вҖҳn tГғВЎch ra file riГғВӘng, Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t vГғВ o package dto/ (vГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ: {@code
   * dto/BidHistoryEntry.java}) vГғВ¬ nГғВі thГЎВ»Вұc chГЎВәВҘt lГғВ  DTO trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ client.
   *
   * @param transaction giao dГЎВ»вҖ№ch bid
   * @param username tГғВӘn ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ (lГЎВәВҘy tГЎВ»В« bГЎВәВЈng users)
   */
  public record BidHistoryEntry(BidTransaction transaction, String username) {

    /** Shortcut: lГЎВәВҘy ID phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ. */
    public Long getAuctionId() {
      return transaction.getAuctionId();
    }

    /** Shortcut: lГЎВәВҘy ID ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ. */
    public Long getBidderId() {
      return transaction.getBidderId();
    }

    /** Shortcut: lГЎВәВҘy giГғВЎ bid. */
    public BigDecimal getAmount() {
      return transaction.getAmount();
    }

    /** Shortcut: kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra cГғВі phГЎВәВЈi auto-bid khГғВҙng. */
    public boolean isAutoBid() {
      return transaction.isAutoBid();
    }

    /** Shortcut: lГЎВәВҘy thГЎВ»Вқi Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»Ж’m bid. */
    public LocalDateTime getCreatedAt() {
      return transaction.getCreatedAt();
    }
  }

  // ============================================================
  // CLEANUP (ChГЎВ»вҖ° dГғВ№ng cho test)
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * XГғВіa tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ bid transactions cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt phiГғВӘn.
   *
   * <p><b>CHГЎВ»ЛҶ DГғв„ўNG CHO TEST.</b> KhГғВҙng gГЎВ»ВҚi method nГғВ y trong production.
   *
   * @param auctionId ID cГЎВ»В§a phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @return sГЎВ»вҖҳ lГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈng dГғВІng bГЎВ»вҖ№ xГғВіa
   */
  public int deleteByAuctionId(Long auctionId) {
    String sql = "DELETE FROM bid_transactions WHERE auction_id = :auctionId";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> handle.createUpdate(sql).bind("auctionId", auctionId).execute());
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\dao\DepositRequestDao.java ==========
package com.auction.dao;

import com.auction.model.DepositRecord;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.sql.SQLException;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.Jdbi;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.mapper.RowMapper;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.statement.StatementContext;

/** DAO cho bГЎВәВЈng deposit_requests */
public class DepositRequestDao {

  private final Jdbi jdbi;

  public DepositRequestDao(Jdbi jdbi) {
    this.jdbi = jdbi;
  }

  private static class DepositRecordMapper implements RowMapper<DepositRecord> {
    @Override
    public DepositRecord map(ResultSet rs, StatementContext ctx) throws SQLException {
      DepositRecord r = new DepositRecord();
      r.setId(rs.getLong("id"));
      r.setUserId(rs.getLong("user_id"));
      r.setAmount(rs.getBigDecimal("amount"));
      r.setStatus(rs.getString("status"));
      r.setCreatedAt(rs.getTimestamp("created_at").toLocalDateTime());
      var reviewed = rs.getTimestamp("reviewed_at");
      if (reviewed != null) {
        r.setReviewedAt(reviewed.toLocalDateTime());
      }
      // username tГЎВ»В« JOIN vГЎВ»вҖәi bГЎВәВЈng users (cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ null nГЎВәВҝu query khГғВҙng JOIN)
      try {
        r.setUsername(rs.getString("username"));
      } catch (SQLException ignored) {
      }
      return r;
    }
  }

  public DepositRecord insert(DepositRecord record) {
    String sql =
        """
        INSERT INTO deposit_requests (user_id, amount, status, created_at)
        VALUES (:userId, :amount, :status, :createdAt)
        RETURNING id
        """;
    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> {
          long id =
              handle
                  .createQuery(sql)
                  .bind("userId", record.getUserId())
                  .bind("amount", record.getAmount())
                  .bind("status", record.getStatus())
                  .bind("createdAt", record.getCreatedAt())
                  .mapTo(Long.class)
                  .one();
          record.setId(id);
          return record;
        });
  }

  public Optional<DepositRecord> findById(Long id) {
    String sql =
        """
        SELECT dr.id, dr.user_id, dr.amount, dr.status, dr.created_at, dr.reviewed_at,
               u.username
        FROM deposit_requests dr
        JOIN users u ON u.id = dr.user_id
        WHERE dr.id = :id
        """;
    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("id", id).map(new DepositRecordMapper()).findOne());
  }

  /** LГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u theo status, JOIN vГЎВ»вҖәi users Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ lГЎВәВҘy username */
  public List<DepositRecord> findByStatus(String status) {
    String sql =
        """
        SELECT dr.id, dr.user_id, dr.amount, dr.status, dr.created_at, dr.reviewed_at,
               u.username
        FROM deposit_requests dr
        JOIN users u ON u.id = dr.user_id
        WHERE dr.status = :status
        ORDER BY dr.created_at ASC
        """;
    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle ->
            handle.createQuery(sql).bind("status", status).map(new DepositRecordMapper()).list());
  }

  /** LГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt user, mГЎВ»вҖәi nhГЎВәВҘt trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc */
  public List<DepositRecord> findByUserId(Long userId) {
    String sql =
        """
        SELECT id, user_id, amount, status, created_at, reviewed_at
        FROM deposit_requests
        WHERE user_id = :userId
        ORDER BY created_at DESC
        """;
    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle ->
            handle.createQuery(sql).bind("userId", userId).map(new DepositRecordMapper()).list());
  }

  public boolean updateStatus(Long id, String newStatus) {
    String sql =
        """
        UPDATE deposit_requests
        SET status = :status, reviewed_at = NOW()
        WHERE id = :id
        """;
    int rows =
        jdbi.withHandle(
            handle -> handle.createUpdate(sql).bind("status", newStatus).bind("id", id).execute());
    return rows > 0;
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\dao\ItemDao.java ==========
package com.auction.dao;

import com.auction.model.Art;
import com.auction.model.Electronics;
import com.auction.model.Item;
import com.auction.model.Vehicle;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.sql.SQLException;
import java.time.LocalDateTime;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.Jdbi;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.mapper.RowMapper;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.statement.StatementContext;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * DAO (Data Access Object) cho bГЎВәВЈng items
 *
 * <p>Class nГғВ y chГЎВ»вҖ№u trГғВЎch nhiГЎВ»вҖЎm giao tiГЎВәВҝp vГЎВ»вҖәi bГЎВәВЈng items trong database. Г„ВҗiГЎВ»Ж’m Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·c biГЎВ»вҖЎt cГЎВ»В§a ItemDao
 * lГғВ  phГЎВәВЈi xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ polymorphism: bГЎВәВЈng items cГғВі cГЎВ»в„ўt category Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ phГғВўn biГЎВ»вҖЎt loГЎВәВЎi sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m (ELECTRONICS,
 * ART, VEHICLE), vГғВ  cГғВЎc cГЎВ»в„ўt Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·c thГғВ№ (brand, artist, year) chГЎВ»вҖ° cГғВі giГғВЎ trГЎВ»вҖ№ cho tГЎВ»В«ng loГЎВәВЎi
 *
 * <h3>Polymorphism trong ItemDao</h3>
 *
 * <p>Khi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҚc tГЎВ»В« database, RowMapper phГЎВәВЈi dГЎВ»Вұa vГғВ o cГЎВ»в„ўt "category" Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ tГЎВәВЎo Г„вҖҳГғВәng subclass:
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>category = "ELECTRONICS" ГўвҖ вҖҷ new Electronics(..., brand, ...)
 *   <li>category = "ART" ГўвҖ вҖҷ new Art(..., artist, ...)
 *   <li>category = "VEHICLE" ГўвҖ вҖҷ new Vehicle(..., year, ...)
 * </ul>
 *
 * <p>Khi ghi vГғВ o database, ItemService sГЎВәВҪ gГЎВ»ВҚi ItemFactory Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ tГЎВәВЎo Г„вҖҳГғВәng subclass, vГғВ  DAO chГЎВ»вҖ° viГЎВ»вҖЎc lГЎВәВҘy
 * cГғВЎc field chung + field Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·c thГғВ№ tГҶВ°ГҶВЎng ГЎВ»В©ng
 *
 * <h3>Factory Method pattern liГғВӘn kГЎВәВҝt</h3>
 *
 * <p>ItemFactory (trong pattern/factory/) tГЎВәВЎo Item subclass tГЎВ»В« CreateItemRequest. DAO chГЎВ»вҖ° Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҚc/ghi,
 * khГғВҙng quyГЎВәВҝt Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖ№nh logic tГЎВәВЎo object.
 *
 * <h3>LiГғВӘn kГЎВәВҝt vГЎВ»вҖәi cГғВЎc file khГғВЎc</h3>
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li><b>Item.java, Electronics.java, Art.java, Vehicle.java</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ model classes
 *   <li><b>ItemService.java</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ gГЎВ»ВҚi cГғВЎc method cГЎВ»В§a DAO nГғВ y
 *   <li><b>ItemFactory.java</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ tГЎВәВЎo subclass tГЎВ»В« request
 *   <li><b>AuctionDao.java</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ auctions tham chiГЎВәВҝu Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn items (item_id foreign key)
 *   <li><b>V1__initial_schema.sql</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖ№nh nghГ„В©a bГЎВәВЈng items
 * </ul>
 */
public class ItemDao {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ItemDao.class);

  /** Danh sГғВЎch cГЎВ»в„ўt SELECT dГғВ№ng chung, trГғВЎnh copy-paste. [FIX #10] */
  private static final String SELECT_COLUMNS =
      "id, name, description, seller_id, category, brand, artist, year, created_at, updated_at";

  private final Jdbi jdbi;

  public ItemDao(Jdbi jdbi) {
    this.jdbi = jdbi;
  }

  /**
   * RowMapper chuyГЎВ»Ж’n ResultSet thГғВ nh Item object (subclass phГғВ№ hГЎВ»ВЈp).
   *
   * <p>Г„ВҗГғВўy lГғВ  nГҶВЎi thГЎВ»Ж’ hiГЎВ»вҖЎn POLYMORPHISM khi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҚc tГЎВ»В« database. DГЎВ»Вұa vГғВ o cГЎВ»в„ўt "category", mapper tГЎВәВЎo
   * Г„вҖҳГғВәng subclass:
   *
   * <ul>
   *   <li>ELECTRONICS: Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҚc thГғВӘm cГЎВ»в„ўt "brand"
   *   <li>ART: Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҚc thГғВӘm cГЎВ»в„ўt "artist"
   *   <li>VEHICLE: Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҚc thГғВӘm cГЎВ»в„ўt "year"
   * </ul>
   *
   * <p>[FIX #4] Throw exception thay vГғВ¬ return null khi category khГғВҙng hГЎВ»ВЈp lГЎВ»вҖЎ.
   *
   * <p>[FIX #9] DГғВ№ng enhanced switch expression (Java 21).
   */
  private static class ItemMapper implements RowMapper<Item> {
    @Override
    public Item map(ResultSet rs, StatementContext ctx) throws SQLException {
      Long id = rs.getLong("id");
      String name = rs.getString("name");
      String description = rs.getString("description");
      Long sellerId = rs.getLong("seller_id");
      String category = rs.getString("category");
      LocalDateTime createdAt = rs.getTimestamp("created_at").toLocalDateTime();

      return switch (category) {
        case "ELECTRONICS" ->
            new Electronics(id, name, description, sellerId, rs.getString("brand"), createdAt);
        case "ART" -> new Art(id, name, description, sellerId, rs.getString("artist"), createdAt);
        case "VEHICLE" ->
            new Vehicle(id, name, description, sellerId, rs.getInt("year"), createdAt);
        default ->
            throw new IllegalStateException(
                "Category khГғВҙng hГЎВ»ВЈp lГЎВ»вҖЎ trong database: '"
                    + category
                    + "' (item id="
                    + id
                    + ", name="
                    + name
                    + "). "
                    + "KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu bГЎВәВЈng items hoГЎВәВ·c thГғВӘm case mГЎВ»вҖәi vГғВ o ItemMapper.");
      };
    }
  }

  // ============================================================
  // CREATE (INSERT)
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * ThГғВӘm sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m mГЎВ»вҖәi vГғВ o database.
   *
   * <p>Method nГғВ y xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ cГЎВәВЈ 3 loГЎВәВЎi sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m (Electronics, Art, Vehicle). TГғВ№y vГғВ o subclass thГЎВ»Вұc tГЎВәВҝ
   * cГЎВ»В§a item, nГғВі sГЎВәВҪ lГЎВәВҘy cГғВЎc field Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·c thГғВ№ tГҶВ°ГҶВЎng ГЎВ»В©ng.
   *
   * <p>LuГЎВ»вҖңng xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ:
   *
   * <ol>
   *   <li>ItemService nhГЎВәВӯn CreateItemRequest, dГғВ№ng ItemFactory tГЎВәВЎo Item subclass
   *   <li>GГЎВ»ВҚi itemDao.insert(item) vГЎВ»вҖәi item cГғВі id = null
   *   <li>JDBI thГЎВ»Вұc thi INSERT vГЎВ»вҖәi cГғВЎc field phГғВ№ hГЎВ»ВЈp
   *   <li>TrГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ item Г„вҖҳГғВЈ cГғВі id
   * </ol>
   *
   * @param item Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖҳi tГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈng Item (Electronics/Art/Vehicle, chГҶВ°a cГғВі id)
   * @return Item Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГғВЎn id tГЎВ»В« database
   */
  public Item insert(Item item) {
    String sql =
        """
        INSERT INTO items (name, description, seller_id, category,
                           brand, artist, year, created_at, updated_at)
        VALUES (:name, :description, :sellerId, :category,
                :brand, :artist, :year, :createdAt, :updatedAt)
        RETURNING id
        """;

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> {
          long id =
              handle
                  .createQuery(sql)
                  .bind("name", item.getName())
                  .bind("description", item.getDescription())
                  .bind("sellerId", item.getSellerId())
                  .bind("category", item.getCategory())
                  .bind("brand", getBrand(item))
                  .bind("artist", getArtist(item))
                  .bind("year", getYear(item))
                  .bind("createdAt", item.getCreatedAt())
                  .bind("updatedAt", item.getCreatedAt()) // mГЎВ»вҖәi tГЎВәВЎo, updatedAt = createdAt
                  .mapTo(Long.class)
                  .one();

          item.setId(id);
          LOGGER.debug(
              "Inserted item: id={}, name={}, category={}, seller={}",
              id,
              item.getName(),
              item.getCategory(),
              item.getSellerId());
          return item;
        });
  }

  /** LГЎВәВҘy brand nГЎВәВҝu item lГғВ  Electronics, ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc lГЎВәВЎi trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ null. */
  private String getBrand(Item item) {
    if (item instanceof Electronics electronics) {
      return electronics.getBrand();
    }
    return null;
  }

  /** LГЎВәВҘy artist nГЎВәВҝu item lГғВ  Art, ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc lГЎВәВЎi trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ null. */
  private String getArtist(Item item) {
    if (item instanceof Art art) {
      return art.getArtist();
    }
    return null;
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy year nГЎВәВҝu item lГғВ  Vehicle, ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc lГЎВәВЎi trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ null.
   *
   * <p>[FIX #2] Г„ВҗГЎВ»вҖўi kiГЎВ»Ж’u trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ tГЎВ»В« {@code int} sang {@code Integer} (boxed). TrГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ {@code null}
   * cho non-Vehicle items ГўвҖ вҖҷ cГЎВ»в„ўt year trong DB nhГЎВәВӯn NULL thay vГғВ¬ giГғВЎ trГЎВ»вҖ№ 0 vГғВҙ nghГ„В©a (Electronics
   * khГғВҙng cГғВі nГ„Ж’m sГЎВәВЈn xuГЎВәВҘt).
   *
   * @param item sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m cГЎВәВ§n lГЎВәВҘy year
   * @return nГ„Ж’m sГЎВәВЈn xuГЎВәВҘt nГЎВәВҝu lГғВ  Vehicle, null nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng
   */
  private Integer getYear(Item item) {
    if (item instanceof Vehicle vehicle) {
      return vehicle.getYear();
    }
    return null;
  }

  // ============================================================
  // READ (SELECT)
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * TГғВ¬m sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m theo ID.
   *
   * @param id ID cГЎВ»В§a sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m
   * @return Optional chГЎВ»В©a Item nГЎВәВҝu tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy, Optional.empty() nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng
   */
  public Optional<Item> findById(Long id) {
    String sql = "SELECT " + SELECT_COLUMNS + " FROM items WHERE id = :id";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("id", id).map(new ItemMapper()).findOne());
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi bГғВЎn.
   *
   * <p>DГғВ№ng cho:
   *
   * <ul>
   *   <li>Seller xem danh sГғВЎch sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m cГЎВ»В§a mГғВ¬nh
   *   <li>Khi tГЎВәВЎo auction, chГЎВ»вҖ° hiГЎВ»Ж’n thГЎВ»вҖ№ items cГЎВ»В§a seller Г„вҖҳГғВі
   * </ul>
   *
   * @param sellerId ID cГЎВ»В§a ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi bГғВЎn
   * @return List cГғВЎc Item cГЎВ»В§a seller Г„вҖҳГғВі
   */
  public List<Item> findBySellerId(Long sellerId) {
    String sql =
        "SELECT "
            + SELECT_COLUMNS
            + " FROM items WHERE seller_id = :sellerId ORDER BY created_at DESC";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("sellerId", sellerId).map(new ItemMapper()).list());
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m trong hГЎВ»вҖЎ thГЎВ»вҖҳng.
   *
   * @return List chГЎВ»В©a tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ Item
   */
  public List<Item> findAll() {
    String sql = "SELECT " + SELECT_COLUMNS + " FROM items ORDER BY created_at DESC";

    return jdbi.withHandle(handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).map(new ItemMapper()).list());
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m theo category.
   *
   * @param category "ELECTRONICS", "ART", hoГЎВәВ·c "VEHICLE"
   * @return List cГғВЎc Item thuГЎВ»в„ўc category Г„вҖҳГғВі
   */
  public List<Item> findByCategory(String category) {
    String sql =
        "SELECT "
            + SELECT_COLUMNS
            + " FROM items WHERE category = :category ORDER BY created_at DESC";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("category", category).map(new ItemMapper()).list());
  }

  /**
   * TГғВ¬m kiГЎВәВҝm sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m theo tГғВӘn (chГЎВ»В©a keyword, khГғВҙng phГғВўn biГЎВ»вҖЎt hoa thГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng).
   *
   * <p>DГғВ№ng cho chГЎВ»В©c nГ„Ж’ng tГғВ¬m kiГЎВәВҝm sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m trГғВӘn client.
   *
   * <p>[FIX #8] Escape kГғВҪ tГЎВ»Вұ Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·c biГЎВ»вҖЎt cГЎВ»В§a LIKE (%, _) trong keyword. TrГғВЎnh lГЎВ»вҖ”i khi user nhГЎВәВӯp kГғВҪ tГЎВ»Вұ
   * Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·c biГЎВ»вҖЎt vГғВ o ГғВҙ tГғВ¬m kiГЎВәВҝm. VГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ: search "100%" sГЎВәВҪ chГЎВ»вҖ° match items cГғВі Г„вҖҳГғВәng chuГЎВ»вҖ”i "100%" thay vГғВ¬
   * match mГЎВ»ВҚi item bГЎВәВҜt Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§u bГЎВәВұng "100".
   *
   * @param keyword tГЎВ»В« khГғВіa cГЎВәВ§n tГғВ¬m
   * @return List cГғВЎc Item cГғВі tГғВӘn chГЎВ»В©a keyword
   */
  public List<Item> searchByName(String keyword) {
    String sql =
        "SELECT "
            + SELECT_COLUMNS
            + " FROM items WHERE LOWER(name) LIKE LOWER(:keyword) ESCAPE '\\'"
            + " ORDER BY created_at DESC";

    // [FIX #8] Escape kГғВҪ tГЎВ»Вұ Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·c biГЎВ»вҖЎt trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc khi ghГғВ©p vГғВ o pattern
    String escaped = keyword.replace("\\", "\\\\").replace("%", "\\%").replace("_", "\\_");
    String searchPattern = "%" + escaped + "%";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle ->
            handle.createQuery(sql).bind("keyword", searchPattern).map(new ItemMapper()).list());
  }

  // ============================================================
  // UPDATE
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * CГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt thГғВҙng tin sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m.
   *
   * <p>Seller cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ sГЎВ»Вӯa tГғВӘn, mГғВҙ tГЎВәВЈ, vГғВ  cГғВЎc field Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·c thГғВ№ cГЎВ»В§a sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m. KhГғВҙng cho phГғВ©p sГЎВ»Вӯa
   * seller_id (khГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ chuyГЎВ»Ж’n sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m sang ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi khГғВЎc).
   *
   * @param item Item Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt (phГЎВәВЈi cГғВі id)
   * @return true nГЎВәВҝu cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt thГғВ nh cГғВҙng, false nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy item
   */
  public boolean update(Item item) {
    String sql =
        """
        UPDATE items
        SET name = :name,
            description = :description,
            brand = :brand,
            artist = :artist,
            year = :year,
            updated_at = :updatedAt
        WHERE id = :id
        """;

    int rowsAffected =
        jdbi.withHandle(
            handle ->
                handle
                    .createUpdate(sql)
                    .bind("name", item.getName())
                    .bind("description", item.getDescription())
                    .bind("brand", getBrand(item))
                    .bind("artist", getArtist(item))
                    .bind("year", getYear(item))
                    .bind("updatedAt", LocalDateTime.now())
                    .bind("id", item.getId())
                    .execute());

    if (rowsAffected > 0) {
      LOGGER.debug("Updated item: id={}, name={}", item.getId(), item.getName());
      return true;
    }

    LOGGER.warn("Item not found for update: id={}", item.getId());
    return false;
  }

  // ============================================================
  // DELETE
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * XГғВіa sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m.
   *
   * <p><b>LГҶВ°u ГғВҪ:</b> Do cГғВі ON DELETE CASCADE trong bГЎВәВЈng auctions, khi xГғВіa item, tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu
   * giГғВЎ liГғВӘn quan cГ…В©ng bГЎВ»вҖ№ xГғВіa.
   *
   * <p>ChГЎВ»вҖ° Seller (chГЎВ»В§ sГЎВ»Её hГЎВ»ВҜu) hoГЎВәВ·c Admin mГЎВ»вҖәi cГғВі quyГЎВ»ВҒn xГғВіa.
   *
   * @param id ID cГЎВ»В§a sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m cГЎВәВ§n xГғВіa
   * @return true nГЎВәВҝu xГғВіa thГғВ nh cГғВҙng, false nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy
   */
  public boolean delete(Long id) {
    String sql = "DELETE FROM items WHERE id = :id";

    int rowsAffected = jdbi.withHandle(handle -> handle.createUpdate(sql).bind("id", id).execute());

    if (rowsAffected > 0) {
      LOGGER.info("Deleted item: id={}", id);
      return true;
    }

    LOGGER.warn("Item not found for deletion: id={}", id);
    return false;
  }

  /**
   * XГғВіa tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi bГғВЎn.
   *
   * <p><b>CHГЎВ»ЛҶ DГғв„ўNG CHO TEST.</b> KhГғВҙng gГЎВ»ВҚi trong production.
   *
   * @param sellerId ID cГЎВ»В§a ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi bГғВЎn
   * @return sГЎВ»вҖҳ lГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈng sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m bГЎВ»вҖ№ xГғВіa
   */
  public int deleteBySellerId(Long sellerId) {
    String sql = "DELETE FROM items WHERE seller_id = :sellerId";

    int rowsAffected =
        jdbi.withHandle(handle -> handle.createUpdate(sql).bind("sellerId", sellerId).execute());

    LOGGER.debug("Deleted {} items for seller: {}", rowsAffected, sellerId);
    return rowsAffected;
  }

  // ============================================================
  // HELPER METHODS
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m cГғВі tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi khГғВҙng.
   *
   * @param id ID cГЎВәВ§n kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra
   * @return true nГЎВәВҝu tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi, false nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng
   */
  public boolean existsById(Long id) {
    String sql = "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM items WHERE id = :id";

    long count =
        jdbi.withHandle(handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("id", id).mapTo(Long.class).one());

    return count > 0;
  }

  /**
   * KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m cГғВі thuГЎВ»в„ўc vГЎВ»ВҒ seller khГғВҙng.
   *
   * <p>DГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ xГғВЎc thГЎВ»Вұc khi Seller muГЎВ»вҖҳn sГЎВ»Вӯa/xГғВіa item hoГЎВәВ·c tГЎВәВЎo auction.
   *
   * @param itemId ID sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m
   * @param sellerId ID ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi bГғВЎn
   * @return true nГЎВәВҝu sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m thuГЎВ»в„ўc vГЎВ»ВҒ seller Г„вҖҳГғВі
   */
  public boolean belongsToSeller(Long itemId, Long sellerId) {
    String sql = "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM items WHERE id = :itemId AND seller_id = :sellerId";

    long count =
        jdbi.withHandle(
            handle ->
                handle
                    .createQuery(sql)
                    .bind("itemId", itemId)
                    .bind("sellerId", sellerId)
                    .mapTo(Long.class)
                    .one());

    return count > 0;
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy sГЎВ»вҖҳ lГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈng sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt seller.
   *
   * @param sellerId ID ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi bГғВЎn
   * @return sГЎВ»вҖҳ lГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈng sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m
   */
  public int countBySellerId(Long sellerId) {
    String sql = "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM items WHERE seller_id = :sellerId";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("sellerId", sellerId).mapTo(Integer.class).one());
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\dao\PasswordResetRequestDao.java ==========
package com.auction.dao;

import com.auction.model.PasswordResetRecord;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.sql.SQLException;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.Jdbi;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.mapper.RowMapper;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.statement.StatementContext;

/** DAO cho bГЎВәВЈng password_reset_requests */
public class PasswordResetRequestDao {

  private final Jdbi jdbi;

  public PasswordResetRequestDao(Jdbi jdbi) {
    this.jdbi = jdbi;
  }

  private static class Mapper implements RowMapper<PasswordResetRecord> {
    @Override
    public PasswordResetRecord map(ResultSet rs, StatementContext ctx) throws SQLException {
      PasswordResetRecord r = new PasswordResetRecord();
      r.setId(rs.getLong("id"));
      r.setUserId(rs.getLong("user_id"));
      r.setStatus(rs.getString("status"));
      r.setCreatedAt(rs.getTimestamp("created_at").toLocalDateTime());
      var reviewed = rs.getTimestamp("reviewed_at");
      if (reviewed != null) {
        r.setReviewedAt(reviewed.toLocalDateTime());
      }
      try {
        r.setUsername(rs.getString("username"));
        r.setEmail(rs.getString("email"));
      } catch (SQLException ignored) {
      }
      return r;
    }
  }

  /** TГЎВәВЎo yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u mГЎВ»вҖәi vГЎВ»вҖәi status PENDING */
  public PasswordResetRecord insert(PasswordResetRecord record) {
    String sql =
        """
        INSERT INTO password_reset_requests (user_id, status, created_at)
        VALUES (:userId, :status, :createdAt)
        RETURNING id
        """;
    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> {
          long id =
              handle
                  .createQuery(sql)
                  .bind("userId", record.getUserId())
                  .bind("status", record.getStatus())
                  .bind("createdAt", record.getCreatedAt())
                  .mapTo(Long.class)
                  .one();
          record.setId(id);
          return record;
        });
  }

  /** TГғВ¬m theo ID, JOIN users Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ lГЎВәВҘy username vГғВ  email */
  public Optional<PasswordResetRecord> findById(Long id) {
    String sql =
        """
        SELECT pr.id, pr.user_id, pr.status, pr.created_at, pr.reviewed_at,
               u.username, u.email
        FROM password_reset_requests pr
        JOIN users u ON u.id = pr.user_id
        WHERE pr.id = :id
        """;
    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("id", id).map(new Mapper()).findOne());
  }

  /** LГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u theo status, JOIN users Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ lГЎВәВҘy username vГғВ  email */
  public List<PasswordResetRecord> findByStatus(String status) {
    String sql =
        """
        SELECT pr.id, pr.user_id, pr.status, pr.created_at, pr.reviewed_at,
               u.username, u.email
        FROM password_reset_requests pr
        JOIN users u ON u.id = pr.user_id
        WHERE pr.status = :status
        ORDER BY pr.created_at ASC
        """;
    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("status", status).map(new Mapper()).list());
  }

  /** KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra user Г„вҖҳГғВЈ cГғВі yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u PENDING chГҶВ°a */
  public boolean hasPendingRequest(Long userId) {
    String sql =
        "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM password_reset_requests WHERE user_id = :userId AND status = 'PENDING'";
    long count =
        jdbi.withHandle(
            handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("userId", userId).mapTo(Long.class).one());
    return count > 0;
  }

  /** CГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt status vГғВ  thГЎВ»Вқi gian duyГЎВ»вҖЎt */
  public boolean updateStatus(Long id, String newStatus) {
    String sql =
        """
        UPDATE password_reset_requests
        SET status = :status, reviewed_at = NOW()
        WHERE id = :id
        """;
    int rows =
        jdbi.withHandle(
            handle -> handle.createUpdate(sql).bind("status", newStatus).bind("id", id).execute());
    return rows > 0;
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\dao\UserDao.java ==========
package com.auction.dao;

import com.auction.model.Admin;
import com.auction.model.Bidder;
import com.auction.model.Seller;
import com.auction.model.User;
import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.sql.SQLException;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.Jdbi;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.mapper.RowMapper;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.statement.StatementContext;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * DAO (Data Access Object) cho bГЎВәВЈng users
 *
 * <p>Class nГғВ y chГЎВ»вҖ№u trГғВЎch nhiГЎВ»вҖЎm giao tiГЎВәВҝp vГЎВ»вҖәi database, thГЎВ»Вұc hiГЎВ»вҖЎn cГғВЎc thao tГғВЎc CRUD (Create, Read,
 * Update, Delete) trГғВӘn bГЎВәВЈng users. DAO layer nГЎВәВұm giГЎВ»ВҜa Service layer vГғВ  Database, giГғВәp tГғВЎch biГЎВ»вҖЎt
 * logic nghiГЎВ»вҖЎp vГЎВ»ВҘ (Service) khГЎВ»ВҸi logic truy vГЎВәВҘn SQL
 *
 * <p>LuГЎВ»вҖңng dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu:
 *
 * <pre>
 * Service (UserService)
 *   ГўвҖ вҖҷ gГЎВ»ВҚi userDao.findByUsername(...)
 *     ГўвҖ вҖҷ JDBI thГЎВ»Вұc thi SQL query
 *       ГўвҖ вҖҷ RowMapper chuyГЎВ»Ж’n ResultSet ГўвҖ вҖҷ User object (Bidder/Seller/Admin)
 *         ГўвҖ вҖҷ trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ Optional&lt;User&gt;
 * </pre>
 *
 * <p>Г„ВҗiГЎВ»Ж’m quan trГЎВ»ВҚng: RowMapper phГЎВәВЈi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҚc cГЎВ»в„ўt "role" Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ quyГЎВәВҝt Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖ№nh tГЎВәВЎo Г„вҖҳГғВәng subclass:
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>role = "BIDDER" ГўвҖ вҖҷ new Bidder(...)
 *   <li>role = "SELLER" ГўвҖ вҖҷ new Seller(...)
 *   <li>role = "ADMIN" ГўвҖ вҖҷ new Admin(...)
 * </ul>
 *
 * <p>Г„ВҗiГЎВ»ВҒu nГғВ y thГЎВ»Ж’ hiГЎВ»вҖЎn POLYMORPHISM: cГғВ№ng mГЎВ»в„ўt cГғВўu query SELECT * FROM users, RowMapper tГЎВ»Вұ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng tГЎВәВЎo
 * Г„вҖҳГғВәng loГЎВәВЎi User mГғВ  khГғВҙng cГЎВәВ§n code if-else rГЎВәВЈi rГғВЎc.
 *
 * <p>LiГғВӘn kГЎВәВҝt vГЎВ»вҖәi cГғВЎc file khГғВЎc:
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li><b>User.java, Bidder.java, Seller.java, Admin.java</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ model classes
 *   <li><b>DatabaseConfig.java</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ cung cГЎВәВҘp Jdbi instance
 *   <li><b>UserService.java</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ gГЎВ»ВҚi cГғВЎc method cГЎВ»В§a DAO nГғВ y
 *   <li><b>V1__initial_schema.sql</b> ГўвӮ¬вҖқ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖ№nh nghГ„В©a bГЎВәВЈng users
 * </ul>
 */
public class UserDao {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(UserDao.class);

  /** Danh sГғВЎch cГЎВ»в„ўt SELECT dГғВ№ng chung, trГғВЎnh copy-paste */
  private static final String SELECT_COLUMNS =
      "id, username, password_hash, email, role, created_at, balance";

  private final Jdbi jdbi;

  /**
   * Constructor ГўвӮ¬вҖқ nhГЎВәВӯn Jdbi tГЎВ»В« DatabaseConfig
   *
   * <p>Trong App.java:
   *
   * <pre>
   * Jdbi jdbi = DatabaseConfig.create();
   * UserDao userDao = new UserDao(jdbi);
   * </pre>
   *
   * @param jdbi instance tГЎВ»В« DatabaseConfig, dГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ tГЎВәВЎo connection vГғВ  thГЎВ»Вұc thi SQL
   */
  public UserDao(Jdbi jdbi) {
    this.jdbi = jdbi;
  }

  /**
   * RowMapper chuyГЎВ»Ж’n ResultSet (1 dГғВІng tГЎВ»В« bГЎВәВЈng users) thГғВ nh User object
   *
   * <p>JDBI tГЎВ»Вұ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng gГЎВ»ВҚi mapper nГғВ y cho mГЎВ»вҖ”i dГғВІng trong ResultSet. Mapper Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҚc giГғВЎ trГЎВ»вҖ№ cГғВЎc cГЎВ»в„ўt, dГЎВ»Вұa
   * vГғВ o cГЎВ»в„ўt "role" Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ tГЎВәВЎo subclass phГғВ№ hГЎВ»ВЈp
   *
   * <p>VГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ:
   *
   * <pre>
   * | id | username | password_hash | email   | role   | created_at |
   * | 1  | alice    | $2a$10$...    | a@x.com | BIDDER | 2024-01-01 |
   * ГўвҖ вҖҷ new Bidder(1L, "alice", "$2a$10$...", "a@x.com", createdAt)
   * </pre>
   *
   * <p>[FIX #4] Throw exception thay vГғВ¬ return null khi gГЎВәВ·p role khГғВҙng hГЎВ»ВЈp lГЎВ»вҖЎ.
   *
   * <p>[FIX #9] DГғВ№ng enhanced switch expression (Java 21) ГўвӮ¬вҖқ gГЎВ»ВҚn hГҶВЎn, compiler bГЎВәВҜt thiГЎВәВҝu case.
   */
  private static class UserMapper implements RowMapper<User> {
    @Override
    public User map(ResultSet rs, StatementContext ctx) throws SQLException {
      Long id = rs.getLong("id");
      String username = rs.getString("username");
      String passwordHash = rs.getString("password_hash");
      String email = rs.getString("email");
      String role = rs.getString("role");
      var createdAt = rs.getTimestamp("created_at").toLocalDateTime();

      // POLYMORPHISM: tГЎВәВЎo Г„вҖҳГғВәng subclass dГЎВ»Вұa vГғВ o role
      User user =
          switch (role) {
            case "BIDDER" -> new Bidder(id, username, passwordHash, email, createdAt);
            case "SELLER" -> new Seller(id, username, passwordHash, email, createdAt);
            case "ADMIN" -> new Admin(id, username, passwordHash, email, createdAt);
            default ->
                throw new IllegalStateException(
                    "Role khГғВҙng hГЎВ»ВЈp lГЎВ»вҖЎ trong database: '"
                        + role
                        + "' (user id="
                        + id
                        + ", username="
                        + username
                        + "). "
                        + "KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu bГЎВәВЈng users hoГЎВәВ·c thГғВӘm case mГЎВ»вҖәi vГғВ o UserMapper.");
          };

      BigDecimal balance = rs.getBigDecimal("balance");
      user.setBalance(balance != null ? balance : BigDecimal.ZERO);
      return user;
    }
  }

  // ============================================================
  // CREATE (INSERT)
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * ThГғВӘm user mГЎВ»вҖәi vГғВ o database
   *
   * <p>Method nГғВ y Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГЎВ»ВҚi khi ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ thГғВ nh cГғВҙng (UserService.register()).
   *
   * <p>LuГЎВ»вҖңng xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ:
   *
   * <ol>
   *   <li>UserService Г„вҖҳГғВЈ hash password bГЎВәВұng BCrypt
   *   <li>GГЎВ»ВҚi userDao.insert(user) vГЎВ»вҖәi user cГғВі id = null (chГҶВ°a cГғВі)
   *   <li>JDBI thГЎВ»Вұc thi INSERT, sГЎВ»Вӯ dГЎВ»ВҘng RETURNING id Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ lГЎВәВҘy ID database sinh ra
   *   <li>CГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt id vГғВ o user object (setId)
   *   <li>TrГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ user Г„вҖҳГғВЈ cГғВі id
   * </ol>
   *
   * @param user Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖҳi tГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈng User (chГҶВ°a cГғВі id, Г„вҖҳГғВЈ cГғВі passwordHash)
   * @return User Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГғВЎn id tГЎВ»В« database
   * @throws org.jdbi.v3.core.statement.UnableToExecuteStatementException nГЎВәВҝu INSERT thГЎВәВҘt bГЎВәВЎi (vГғВӯ
   *     dГЎВ»ВҘ: duplicate username do UNIQUE constraint)
   */
  public User insert(User user) {
    String sql =
        """
        INSERT INTO users (username, password_hash, email, role, created_at, balance)
        VALUES (:username, :passwordHash, :email, :role, :createdAt, :balance)
        RETURNING id
        """;

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> {
          long id =
              handle
                  .createQuery(sql)
                  .bind("username", user.getUsername())
                  .bind("passwordHash", user.getPasswordHash())
                  .bind("email", user.getEmail())
                  .bind("role", user.getRole())
                  .bind("createdAt", user.getCreatedAt())
                  .bind(
                      "balance",
                      user.getBalance() != null ? user.getBalance() : java.math.BigDecimal.ZERO)
                  .mapTo(Long.class)
                  .one();

          user.setId(id);
          LOGGER.debug(
              "Inserted user: {} (id={}, role={})", user.getUsername(), id, user.getRole());
          return user;
        });
  }

  // ============================================================
  // READ (SELECT)
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * TГғВ¬m user theo ID.
   *
   * <p>DГғВ№ng khi cГЎВәВ§n lГЎВәВҘy thГғВҙng tin user tГЎВ»В« JWT token (userId nГЎВәВұm trong token) hoГЎВәВ·c khi cГЎВәВ§n kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra
   * owner cГЎВ»В§a item/auction.
   *
   * @param id ID cГЎВ»В§a user cГЎВәВ§n tГғВ¬m
   * @return Optional chГЎВ»В©a User nГЎВәВҝu tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy, Optional.empty() nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng
   */
  public Optional<User> findById(Long id) {
    String sql = "SELECT " + SELECT_COLUMNS + " FROM users WHERE id = :id";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("id", id).map(new UserMapper()).findOne());
  }

  /**
   * TГғВ¬m user theo username (dГғВ№ng cho Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp).
   *
   * <p>Г„ВҗГғВўy lГғВ  method quan trГЎВ»ВҚng nhГЎВәВҘt cГЎВ»В§a UserDao, Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГЎВ»ВҚi trong login flow.
   *
   * <p>LuГЎВ»вҖңng Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp:
   *
   * <ol>
   *   <li>Client gГЎВ»Вӯi username/password
   *   <li>UserService.login() gГЎВ»ВҚi findByUsername(username)
   *   <li>NГЎВәВҝu tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy user, dГғВ№ng BCrypt.verify() so sГғВЎnh password
   *   <li>NГЎВәВҝu Г„вҖҳГғВәng ГўвҖ вҖҷ tГЎВәВЎo JWT token vГғВ  trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ
   * </ol>
   *
   * @param username tГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp
   * @return Optional chГЎВ»В©a User nГЎВәВҝu tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy, Optional.empty() nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng
   */
  public Optional<User> findByUsername(String username) {
    String sql = "SELECT " + SELECT_COLUMNS + " FROM users WHERE username = :username";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle ->
            handle.createQuery(sql).bind("username", username).map(new UserMapper()).findOne());
  }

  /**
   * TГғВ¬m user theo email (dГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra email Г„вҖҳГғВЈ tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi khi Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ).
   *
   * @param email email cГЎВәВ§n kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra
   * @return Optional chГЎВ»В©a User nГЎВәВҝu tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy, Optional.empty() nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng
   */
  public Optional<User> findByEmail(String email) {
    String sql = "SELECT " + SELECT_COLUMNS + " FROM users WHERE email = :email";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("email", email).map(new UserMapper()).findOne());
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ user trong hГЎВ»вҖЎ thГЎВ»вҖҳng (dГғВ nh cho Admin).
   *
   * <p>Admin Panel sГЎВәВҪ gГЎВ»ВҚi method nГғВ y Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ hiГЎВ»Ж’n thГЎВ»вҖ№ danh sГғВЎch ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng, cho phГғВ©p admin xГғВіa hoГЎВәВ·c vГғВҙ
   * hiГЎВ»вҖЎu hГғВіa tГғВ i khoГЎВәВЈn vi phГЎВәВЎm.
   *
   * @return List chГЎВ»В©a tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ User (cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ rГЎВ»вҖ”ng nГЎВәВҝu chГҶВ°a cГғВі user nГғВ o)
   */
  public List<User> findAll() {
    String sql = "SELECT " + SELECT_COLUMNS + " FROM users ORDER BY id";

    return jdbi.withHandle(handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).map(new UserMapper()).list());
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ user vГЎВ»вҖәi mГЎВ»в„ўt role cГЎВ»ВҘ thГЎВ»Ж’.
   *
   * <p>VГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ: lГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ Seller Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ hiГЎВ»Ж’n thГЎВ»вҖ№ trong Admin Panel, hoГЎВәВ·c lГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ Bidder Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ thГЎВ»вҖҳng kГғВӘ.
   *
   * @param role "BIDDER", "SELLER", hoГЎВәВ·c "ADMIN"
   * @return List chГЎВ»В©a cГғВЎc user cГғВі role tГҶВ°ГҶВЎng ГЎВ»В©ng
   */
  public List<User> findByRole(String role) {
    String sql = "SELECT " + SELECT_COLUMNS + " FROM users WHERE role = :role ORDER BY id";

    return jdbi.withHandle(
        handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("role", role).map(new UserMapper()).list());
  }

  // ============================================================
  // UPDATE
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * CГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt thГғВҙng tin user.
   *
   * <p>Cho phГғВ©p user thay Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi email, password. KhГғВҙng cho phГғВ©p thay Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi username (username lГғВ  unique
   * identifier, khГғВҙng nГғВӘn thay Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi sau khi tГЎВәВЎo).
   *
   * @param user Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖҳi tГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈng User Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt thГғВҙng tin (phГЎВәВЈi cГғВі id)
   * @return true nГЎВәВҝu cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt thГғВ nh cГғВҙng, false nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy user
   */
  public boolean update(User user) {
    String sql =
        """
        UPDATE users
        SET password_hash = :passwordHash,
            email = :email,
            balance = :balance
        WHERE id = :id
        """;

    int rowsAffected =
        jdbi.withHandle(
            handle ->
                handle
                    .createUpdate(sql)
                    .bind("passwordHash", user.getPasswordHash())
                    .bind("email", user.getEmail())
                    .bind(
                        "balance",
                        user.getBalance() != null ? user.getBalance() : java.math.BigDecimal.ZERO)
                    .bind("id", user.getId())
                    .execute());

    if (rowsAffected > 0) {
      LOGGER.debug("Updated user: id={}, username={}", user.getId(), user.getUsername());
      return true;
    }

    LOGGER.warn("User not found for update: id={}", user.getId());
    return false;
  }

  /**
   * CГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt sГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ° bГЎВәВұng mГЎВ»в„ўt giГғВЎ trГЎВ»вҖ№ delta (cГЎВ»в„ўng hoГЎВәВ·c trГЎВ»В«) theo cГғВЎch atomic ГўвӮ¬вҖқ trГғВЎnh race condition
   * khi nhiГЎВ»ВҒu phiГғВӘn kГЎВәВҝt thГғВәc cГғВ№ng lГғВәc vГЎВ»вҖәi cГғВ№ng mГЎВ»в„ўt bidder.
   *
   * @param userId ID ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng
   * @param delta sГЎВ»вҖҳ tiГЎВ»ВҒn thay Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi (dГҶВ°ГҶВЎng = cГЎВ»в„ўng, ГғВўm = trГЎВ»В«)
   */
  public void updateBalance(Long userId, BigDecimal delta) {
    jdbi.withHandle(
        handle ->
            handle
                .createUpdate("UPDATE users SET balance = balance + :delta WHERE id = :userId")
                .bind("delta", delta)
                .bind("userId", userId)
                .execute());
  }

  // ============================================================
  // DELETE
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * XГғВіa user khГЎВ»ВҸi database.
   *
   * <p>LГҶВ°u ГғВҪ: do cГғВі ON DELETE CASCADE trong bГЎВәВЈng items vГғВ  auctions, khi xГғВіa user, tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m
   * vГғВ  phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ cГЎВ»В§a user Г„вҖҳГғВі cГ…В©ng bГЎВ»вҖ№ xГғВіa.
   *
   * <p>ChГЎВ»вҖ° Admin mГЎВ»вҖәi cГғВі quyГЎВ»ВҒn gГЎВ»ВҚi method nГғВ y.
   *
   * @param id ID cГЎВ»В§a user cГЎВәВ§n xГғВіa
   * @return true nГЎВәВҝu xГғВіa thГғВ nh cГғВҙng, false nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy user
   */
  public boolean delete(Long id) {
    String sql = "DELETE FROM users WHERE id = :id";

    int rowsAffected = jdbi.withHandle(handle -> handle.createUpdate(sql).bind("id", id).execute());

    if (rowsAffected > 0) {
      LOGGER.info("Deleted user with id: {}", id);
      return true;
    }

    LOGGER.warn("User not found for deletion: id={}", id);
    return false;
  }

  // ============================================================
  // HELPER METHODS
  // ============================================================

  /**
   * KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra username Г„вҖҳГғВЈ tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi chГҶВ°a (dГғВ№ng trong register Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ trГғВЎnh duplicate).
   *
   * @param username tГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp cГЎВәВ§n kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra
   * @return true nГЎВәВҝu username Г„вҖҳГғВЈ tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi, false nГЎВәВҝu chГҶВ°a
   */
  public boolean existsByUsername(String username) {
    String sql = "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM users WHERE username = :username";

    long count =
        jdbi.withHandle(
            handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("username", username).mapTo(Long.class).one());

    return count > 0;
  }

  /**
   * KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra email Г„вҖҳГғВЈ tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi chГҶВ°a.
   *
   * @param email email cГЎВәВ§n kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra
   * @return true nГЎВәВҝu email Г„вҖҳГғВЈ tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi, false nГЎВәВҝu chГҶВ°a
   */
  public boolean existsByEmail(String email) {
    String sql = "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM users WHERE email = :email";

    long count =
        jdbi.withHandle(
            handle -> handle.createQuery(sql).bind("email", email).mapTo(Long.class).one());

    return count > 0;
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\dto\AuctionResponse.java ==========
package com.auction.dto;

import com.auction.model.Auction;
import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.time.LocalDateTime;

/**
 * DTO trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ thГғВҙng tin phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ cho client ГўвӮ¬вҖқ phiГғВӘn bГЎВәВЈn "an toГғВ n" cГЎВ»В§a Auction
 *
 * <p>TГЎВәВЎi sao cГЎВәВ§n AuctionResponse thay vГғВ¬ trГЎВәВЈ thГЎВәВіng Auction?
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>Auction chГЎВ»В©a cГғВЎc field nГЎВ»в„ўi bГЎВ»в„ў mГғВ  client khГғВҙng cГЎВәВ§n biГЎВәВҝt
 *   <li>CГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ muГЎВ»вҖҳn thГғВӘm/bГЎВ»вҖәt field tГғВ№y API mГғВ  khГғВҙng ГЎВәВЈnh hГҶВ°ГЎВ»Еёng model
 *   <li>TГғВЎch biГЎВ»вҖЎt tГЎВәВ§ng data (model) vГғВ  tГЎВәВ§ng presentation (DTO) ГўвӮ¬вҖқ Г„вҖҳГғВәng nguyГғВӘn tГЎВәВҜc MVC
 *   <li>Trong tГҶВ°ГҶВЎng lai cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ cГЎВәВ§n nhiГЎВ»ВҒu response format khГғВЎc nhau cho cГғВ№ng 1 entity
 * </ul>
 *
 * <p>AuctionResponse bГЎВ»вҖў sung thГғВӘm thГғВҙng tin phГғВЎi sinh mГғВ  client cГЎВәВ§n:
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>itemName ГўвӮ¬вҖқ tГғВӘn sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m (thay vГғВ¬ chГЎВ»вҖ° itemId, client khГғВҙng cГЎВәВ§n query thГғВӘm)
 *   <li>leadingBidderUsername ГўвӮ¬вҖқ tГғВӘn ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГЎВәВ«n Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§u (thay vГғВ¬ chГЎВ»вҖ° leadingBidderId)
 *   <li>remainingTimeMs ГўвӮ¬вҖқ thГЎВ»Вқi gian cГғВІn lГЎВәВЎi tГғВӯnh sГЎВәВөn (client khГғВҙng cГЎВәВ§n tГЎВ»Вұ tГғВӯnh)
 *   <li>itemBrand ГўвӮ¬вҖқ hГғВЈng sГЎВәВЈn xuГЎВәВҘt (chГЎВ»вҖ° cГғВі khi category = ELECTRONICS)
 *   <li>itemArtist ГўвӮ¬вҖқ nghГЎВ»вҖЎ sГ„В© (chГЎВ»вҖ° cГғВі khi category = ART)
 *   <li>itemYear ГўвӮ¬вҖқ nГ„Ж’m sГЎВәВЈn xuГЎВәВҘt (chГЎВ»вҖ° cГғВі khi category = VEHICLE)
 * </ul>
 *
 * <p>Method tГ„В©nh fromAuction() giГғВәp chuyГЎВ»Ж’n Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi Auction ГўвҖ вҖҷ AuctionResponse mГЎВ»в„ўt cГғВЎch tiГЎВ»вҖЎn lГЎВ»ВЈi, trГғВЎnh
 * viГЎВәВҝt lГЎВәВЎi code mapping ГЎВ»Её nhiГЎВ»ВҒu nГҶВЎi
 */
public class AuctionResponse {

  private Long id;
  private Long itemId;
  private String itemName;
  private String itemCategory;
  private String itemDescription;
  private String itemBrand; // ELECTRONICS only
  private String itemArtist; // ART only
  private Integer itemYear; // VEHICLE only
  private BigDecimal startingPrice;
  private BigDecimal currentPrice;
  private Long leadingBidderId;
  private String leadingBidderUsername;
  private LocalDateTime startTime;
  private LocalDateTime endTime;
  private String status;
  private long remainingTimeMs;

  public AuctionResponse() {}

  /**
   * Factory method chuyГЎВ»Ж’n Auction model ГўвҖ вҖҷ AuctionResponse DTO
   *
   * <p>itemName vГғВ  leadingBidderUsername cГЎВәВ§n query thГғВӘm tГЎВ»В« DB, nГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ Controller/Service set sau.
   * Method nГғВ y chГЎВ»вҖ° map cГғВЎc field cГғВі sГЎВәВөn trong Auction
   *
   * @param auction Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖҳi tГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈng Auction tГЎВ»В« database
   * @return AuctionResponse chГЎВ»В©a thГғВҙng tin cГҶВЎ bГЎВәВЈn, thiГЎВәВҝu itemName vГғВ  leadingBidderUsername
   */
  public static AuctionResponse fromAuction(Auction auction) {
    AuctionResponse response = new AuctionResponse();
    response.id = auction.getId();
    response.itemId = auction.getItemId();
    response.startingPrice = auction.getStartingPrice();
    response.currentPrice = auction.getCurrentPrice();
    response.leadingBidderId = auction.getLeadingBidderId();
    response.startTime = auction.getStartTime();
    response.endTime = auction.getEndTime();
    response.status = auction.getStatus();
    response.remainingTimeMs = auction.getRemainingTimeMs();
    return response;
  }

  // === Getters & Setters ===

  public Long getId() {
    return id;
  }

  public void setId(Long id) {
    this.id = id;
  }

  public Long getItemId() {
    return itemId;
  }

  public void setItemId(Long itemId) {
    this.itemId = itemId;
  }

  public String getItemName() {
    return itemName;
  }

  public void setItemName(String itemName) {
    this.itemName = itemName;
  }

  public String getItemCategory() {
    return itemCategory;
  }

  public void setItemCategory(String itemCategory) {
    this.itemCategory = itemCategory;
  }

  public String getItemDescription() {
    return itemDescription;
  }

  public void setItemDescription(String itemDescription) {
    this.itemDescription = itemDescription;
  }

  public String getItemBrand() {
    return itemBrand;
  }

  public void setItemBrand(String itemBrand) {
    this.itemBrand = itemBrand;
  }

  public String getItemArtist() {
    return itemArtist;
  }

  public void setItemArtist(String itemArtist) {
    this.itemArtist = itemArtist;
  }

  public Integer getItemYear() {
    return itemYear;
  }

  public void setItemYear(Integer itemYear) {
    this.itemYear = itemYear;
  }

  public BigDecimal getStartingPrice() {
    return startingPrice;
  }

  public void setStartingPrice(BigDecimal startingPrice) {
    this.startingPrice = startingPrice;
  }

  public BigDecimal getCurrentPrice() {
    return currentPrice;
  }

  public void setCurrentPrice(BigDecimal currentPrice) {
    this.currentPrice = currentPrice;
  }

  public Long getLeadingBidderId() {
    return leadingBidderId;
  }

  public void setLeadingBidderId(Long leadingBidderId) {
    this.leadingBidderId = leadingBidderId;
  }

  public String getLeadingBidderUsername() {
    return leadingBidderUsername;
  }

  public void setLeadingBidderUsername(String leadingBidderUsername) {
    this.leadingBidderUsername = leadingBidderUsername;
  }

  public LocalDateTime getStartTime() {
    return startTime;
  }

  public void setStartTime(LocalDateTime startTime) {
    this.startTime = startTime;
  }
