      return;
    }

    scheduledTask =
        scheduler.scheduleAtFixedRate(
            this::scanAndTransition,
            0, // delay ban Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§u: chГЎВәВЎy ngay khi start
            SCAN_INTERVAL_SECONDS,
            TimeUnit.SECONDS);

    LOG.info("AuctionScheduler Г„вҖҳГғВЈ khГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng ГўвӮ¬вҖқ quГғВ©t mГЎВ»вҖ”i {}s", SCAN_INTERVAL_SECONDS);
  }

  /**
   * DГЎВ»В«ng scheduler khi server shutdown.
   *
   * <p>GГЎВ»ВҚi trong shutdown hook cГЎВ»В§a {@code App.java} Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ giГЎВәВЈi phГғВіng thread pool.
   */
  public void stop() {
    if (scheduledTask != null) {
      scheduledTask.cancel(false); // khГғВҙng interrupt task Г„вҖҳang chГЎВәВЎy giГЎВ»ВҜa chГЎВ»В«ng
    }
    scheduler.shutdown();
    try {
      if (!scheduler.awaitTermination(5, TimeUnit.SECONDS)) {
        scheduler.shutdownNow();
      }
    } catch (InterruptedException ie) {
      scheduler.shutdownNow();
      Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
    }
    running.set(false);
    LOG.info("AuctionScheduler Г„вҖҳГғВЈ dГЎВ»В«ng");
  }

  // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ Core scan logic ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬

  /**
   * HГғВ m chГғВӯnh Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГЎВ»ВҚi mГЎВ»вҖ”i {@value #SCAN_INTERVAL_SECONDS} giГғВўy.
   *
   * <p>ThГЎВ»В© tГЎВ»Вұ xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ: chuyГЎВ»Ж’n OPENГўвҖ вҖҷRUNNING trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc, rГЎВ»вҖңi RUNNINGГўвҖ вҖҷFINISHED. Г„ВҗiГЎВ»ВҒu nГғВ y xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ Г„вҖҳГғВәng edge case
   * startTime == endTime.
   */
  void scanAndTransition() {
    try {
      LocalDateTime now = LocalDateTime.now();
      LOG.debug("Scheduler scan tГЎВәВЎi {}", now);

      openToRunning(now);
      runningToFinished(now);

    } catch (Exception e) {
      // BГЎВәВҜt tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ exception Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ scheduler khГғВҙng chГЎВәВҝt ГғВўm thГЎВәВ§m.
      // NГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng cГғВі try-catch nГғВ y, mГЎВ»в„ўt RuntimeException sГЎВәВҪ cancel scheduledTask.
      LOG.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i trong AuctionScheduler.scanAndTransition()", e);
    }
  }

  // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ OPEN ГўвҖ вҖҷ RUNNING ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬

  /**
   * ChuyГЎВ»Ж’n cГғВЎc phiГғВӘn tГЎВ»В« OPEN sang RUNNING khi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn giГЎВ»Вқ bГЎВәВҜt Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§u.
   *
   * @param now thГЎВ»Вқi Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»Ж’m hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi
   */
  private void openToRunning(LocalDateTime now) {
    List<Auction> openAuctions = auctionDao.findByStatus("OPEN");

    for (Auction auction : openAuctions) {
      if (auction.getStartTime() == null) {
        continue;
      }

      if (!auction.getStartTime().isAfter(now)) {
        try {
          auction.setStatus("RUNNING");
          auctionDao.update(auction);
          LOG.info(
              "PhiГғВӘn #{} chuyГЎВ»Ж’n OPEN ГўвҖ вҖҷ RUNNING (startTime={})",
              auction.getId(),
              auction.getStartTime());
        } catch (Exception e) {
          LOG.error("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ chuyГЎВ»Ж’n phiГғВӘn #{} sang RUNNING", auction.getId(), e);
        }
      }
    }
  }

  // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ RUNNING ГўвҖ вҖҷ FINISHED ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬

  /**
   * ChuyГЎВ»Ж’n cГғВЎc phiГғВӘn tГЎВ»В« RUNNING sang FINISHED khi hГЎВәВҝt giГЎВ»Вқ.
   *
   * <p>Sau khi cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt DB, broadcast AUCTION_ENDED qua WebSocket Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ client Г„вҖҳang xem phiГғВӘn
   * nhГЎВәВӯn Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc thГғВҙng bГғВЎo ngay lГЎВәВӯp tГЎВ»В©c.
   *
   * @param now thГЎВ»Вқi Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»Ж’m hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi
   */
  private void runningToFinished(LocalDateTime now) {
    List<Auction> runningAuctions = auctionDao.findByStatus("RUNNING");

    for (Auction auction : runningAuctions) {
      if (auction.getEndTime() == null) {
        continue;
      }

      if (!auction.getEndTime().isAfter(now)) {
        try {
          settleAndClose(auction);
          notifyAuctionEnded(auction);
        } catch (Exception e) {
          LOG.error("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ kГЎВәВҝt thГғВәc phiГғВӘn #{}", auction.getId(), e);
        }
      }
    }
  }

  /**
   * Thanh toГғВЎn vГғВ  Г„вҖҳГғВіng phiГғВӘn: - NГЎВәВҝu cГғВі ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi thГЎВәВҜng: trГЎВ»В« tiГЎВ»ВҒn bidder, cГЎВ»в„ўng tiГЎВ»ВҒn seller, status ГўвҖ вҖҷ
   * PAID. - NГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng ai bid: status ГўвҖ вҖҷ FINISHED.
   */
  private void settleAndClose(Auction auction) {
    Long winnerId = auction.getLeadingBidderId();

    if (winnerId != null) {
      BigDecimal price = auction.getCurrentPrice();

      userDao
          .findById(winnerId)
          .ifPresent(
              winner -> {
                BigDecimal balance =
                    winner.getBalance() != null ? winner.getBalance() : BigDecimal.ZERO;
                if (balance.compareTo(price) >= 0) {
                  userDao.updateBalance(winnerId, price.negate());
                  LOG.info("PhiГғВӘn #{}: trГЎВ»В« {} tГЎВ»В« bidder #{}", auction.getId(), price, winnerId);
                } else {
                  LOG.warn(
                      "PhiГғВӘn #{}: bidder #{} khГғВҙng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»В§ sГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ° ({}) Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ thanh toГғВЎn {}. KhГғВҙng trГЎВ»В«.",
                      auction.getId(),
                      winnerId,
                      balance,
                      price);
                }
              });

      // CГЎВ»в„ўng tiГЎВ»ВҒn seller (atomic ГўвӮ¬вҖқ same race condition applies)
      Long sellerId = auction.getSellerId();
      if (sellerId == null) {
        sellerId = itemDao.findById(auction.getItemId()).map(Item::getSellerId).orElse(null);
      }
      if (sellerId != null) {
        userDao.updateBalance(sellerId, price);
        LOG.info("PhiГғВӘn #{}: cГЎВ»в„ўng {} cho seller #{}", auction.getId(), price, sellerId);
      }

      auction.setStatus("PAID");
    } else {
      auction.setStatus("FINISHED");
    }

    auctionDao.update(auction);
    LOG.info(
        "PhiГғВӘn #{} ГўвҖ вҖҷ {} (endTime={}, winner={})",
        auction.getId(),
        auction.getStatus(),
        auction.getEndTime(),
        winnerId);
  }

  // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ Notification ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬

  /**
   * GГЎВ»Вӯi thГғВҙng bГғВЎo AUCTION_ENDED Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ client Г„вҖҳang xem phiГғВӘn nГғВ y.
   *
   * <p>Message chГЎВ»В©a: auctionId, winnerId, winningPrice. Client nhГЎВәВӯn message ГўвҖ вҖҷ disable nГғВәt bid ГўвҖ вҖҷ
   * hiГЎВ»Ж’n thГЎВ»вҖ№ "NgГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi thГЎВәВҜng: ...".
   *
   * @param auction phiГғВӘn vГЎВ»В«a kГЎВәВҝt thГғВәc
   */
  private void notifyAuctionEnded(Auction auction) {
    try {
      String winnerName = null;
      if (auction.getLeadingBidderId() != null) {
        winnerName =
            userDao.findById(auction.getLeadingBidderId()).map(User::getUsername).orElse(null);
      }
      BidUpdateMessage msg =
          BidUpdateMessage.auctionEnded(
              auction.getId(), auction.getCurrentPrice(), auction.getLeadingBidderId(), winnerName);
      eventManager.notifyAuctionEnd(auction.getId(), msg);

    } catch (Exception e) {
      LOG.error("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ broadcast AUCTION_ENDED cho phiГғВӘn #{}", auction.getId(), e);
    }
  }

  /** TrГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi chГЎВәВЎy hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi ГўвӮ¬вҖқ dГғВ№ng trong health check endpoint. */
  public boolean isRunning() {
    return running.get();
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\service\AuctionService.java ==========
package com.auction.service;

import com.auction.dao.AuctionDao;
import com.auction.dao.ItemDao;
import com.auction.dao.UserDao;
import com.auction.dto.AuctionResponse;
import com.auction.dto.CreateAuctionRequest;
import com.auction.exception.AuctionClosedException;
import com.auction.exception.NotFoundException;
import com.auction.exception.UnauthorizedException;
import com.auction.model.Art;
import com.auction.model.Auction;
import com.auction.model.Electronics;
import com.auction.model.Item;
import com.auction.model.Vehicle;
import com.auction.pattern.state.AuctionState;
import com.auction.pattern.state.CanceledState;
import com.auction.pattern.state.FinishedState;
import com.auction.pattern.state.OpenState;
import com.auction.pattern.state.PaidState;
import com.auction.pattern.state.RunningState;
import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.util.List;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/** Service xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ logic nghiГЎВ»вҖЎp vГЎВ»ВҘ cho Auction (phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ). */
public class AuctionService {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(AuctionService.class);

  private final AuctionDao auctionDao;
  private final ItemDao itemDao;
  private final UserDao userDao;

  public AuctionService(AuctionDao auctionDao, ItemDao itemDao, UserDao userDao) {
    this.auctionDao = auctionDao;
    this.itemDao = itemDao;
    this.userDao = userDao;
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ auctions, cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ filter theo status.
   *
   * <p>GET /api/auctions?status=RUNNING ГўвҖ вҖҷ chГЎВ»вҖ° lГЎВәВҘy auctions Г„вҖҳang chГЎВәВЎy. GET /api/auctions ГўвҖ вҖҷ lГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt
   * cГЎВәВЈ.
   */
  public List<Auction> getAllAuctions(String status) {
    if (status != null && !status.isBlank()) {
      return auctionDao.findByStatus(status.toUpperCase());
    }
    return auctionDao.findAll();
  }

  /**
   * Alias cho getAllAuctions ГўвӮ¬вҖқ dГғВ№ng bГЎВ»Еёi AuctionController.
   *
   * @param status filter theo trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi (cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ null Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ lГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ)
   * @return danh sГғВЎch AuctionResponse Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc enrich
   */
  public List<AuctionResponse> getAll(String status) {
    return getAllAuctions(status).stream().map(this::enrichAuctionResponse).toList();
  }

  /**
   * Alias cho getAuctionById ГўвӮ¬вҖқ dГғВ№ng bГЎВ»Еёi AuctionController.
   *
   * @param id ID cГЎВ»В§a auction
   * @return AuctionResponse Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§y Г„вҖҳГЎВ»В§ thГғВҙng tin
   * @throws NotFoundException nГЎВәВҝu auction khГғВҙng tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi
   */
  public AuctionResponse getById(Long id) {
    return getAuctionById(id);
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy chi tiГЎВәВҝt 1 auction, trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ AuctionResponse (bao gГЎВ»вҖңm itemName, leadingBidderUsername).
   *
   * <p>AuctionResponse chГЎВ»В©a nhiГЎВ»ВҒu thГғВҙng tin hГҶВЎn Auction model: - itemName, itemCategory: lГЎВәВҘy tГЎВ»В«
   * bГЎВәВЈng items - leadingBidderUsername: lГЎВәВҘy tГЎВ»В« bГЎВәВЈng users
   *
   * @param id ID cГЎВ»В§a auction
   * @return AuctionResponse Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§y Г„вҖҳГЎВ»В§ thГғВҙng tin
   * @throws NotFoundException nГЎВәВҝu auction khГғВҙng tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi
   */
  public AuctionResponse getAuctionById(Long id) {
    // TГғВ¬m auction
    Auction auction =
        auctionDao
            .findById(id)
            .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("Auction not found with id: " + id));

    // ChuyГЎВ»Ж’n Auction ГўвҖ вҖҷ AuctionResponse (thГғВӘm itemName, leadingBidderUsername)
    return enrichAuctionResponse(auction);
  }

  /**
   * TГЎВәВЎo phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ mГЎВ»вҖәi ГўвӮ¬вҖқ seller Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc xГғВЎc thГЎВ»Вұc bГЎВ»Еёi AuctionController.
   *
   * @param req dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu tГЎВ»В« client
   * @param sellerId ID seller tГЎВ»В« JWT
   */
  public Auction create(CreateAuctionRequest req, Long sellerId) {
    if (req.getItemId() == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Item ID is required");
    }
    if (req.getStartingPrice() == null || req.getStartingPrice().signum() <= 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Starting price must be greater than 0");
    }
    if (req.getStartTime() == null || req.getEndTime() == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Start time and end time are required");
    }
    if (!req.getEndTime().isAfter(req.getStartTime())) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("End time must be after start time");
    }

    Item item =
        itemDao
            .findById(req.getItemId())
            .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("Item not found with id: " + req.getItemId()));

    if (!item.getSellerId().equals(sellerId)) {
      throw new UnauthorizedException("You can only create auctions for your own items");
    }

    Auction auction =
        new Auction(req.getItemId(), req.getStartingPrice(), req.getStartTime(), req.getEndTime());
    auction.setSellerId(sellerId);
    auctionDao.insert(auction);
    LOGGER.info("Auction created (via create): itemId={}, seller={}", req.getItemId(), sellerId);
    return auction;
  }

  /**
   * CГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt giГғВЎ khГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»Ж’m cГЎВ»В§a phiГғВӘn (simplified ГўвӮ¬вҖқ chГЎВ»вҖ° nhГЎВәВӯn BigDecimal). KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi qua
   * State pattern trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc khi sГЎВ»Вӯa.
   */
  public Auction update(Long auctionId, BigDecimal newPrice, Long sellerId) {
    Auction auction =
        auctionDao
            .findById(auctionId)
            .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("Auction not found: " + auctionId));

    // DГғВ№ng State pattern Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ validate ГўвӮ¬вҖқ OpenState cho phГғВ©p, RunningState/FinishedState tГЎВ»В« chГЎВ»вҖҳi
    getState(auction).edit(auction);

    auction.setStartingPrice(newPrice);
    auction.setCurrentPrice(newPrice);
    auctionDao.update(auction);
    return auction;
  }

  /**
   * CГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ vГғВ  trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ AuctionResponse ГўвӮ¬вҖқ dГғВ№ng bГЎВ»Еёi AuctionController.
   *
   * <p>ChГЎВ»вҖ° cho phГғВ©p sГЎВ»Вӯa khi status = OPEN. Seller chГЎВ»вҖ° Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc sГЎВ»Вӯa phiГғВӘn cГЎВ»В§a item mГғВ¬nh.
   *
   * @param auctionId ID phiГғВӘn cГЎВәВ§n sГЎВ»Вӯa
   * @param request dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu mГЎВ»вҖәi (startingPrice, startTime, endTime)
   * @param userId ID seller tГЎВ»В« JWT
   * @return AuctionResponse Г„вҖҳГғВЈ cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt
   */
  public AuctionResponse update(Long auctionId, CreateAuctionRequest request, Long userId) {
    Auction auction =
        auctionDao
            .findById(auctionId)
            .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("Auction not found with id: " + auctionId));

    if (!"OPEN".equals(auction.getStatus())) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Can only edit auctions with OPEN status. Current status: " + auction.getStatus());
    }

    Item item =
        itemDao
            .findById(auction.getItemId())
            .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("Item not found"));

    if (!item.getSellerId().equals(userId)) {
      throw new UnauthorizedException("You can only edit your own auctions");
    }

    if (request.getStartingPrice() != null && request.getStartingPrice().signum() > 0) {
      auction.setStartingPrice(request.getStartingPrice());
      auction.setCurrentPrice(request.getStartingPrice());
    }
    if (request.getStartTime() != null) {
      auction.setStartTime(request.getStartTime());
    }
    if (request.getEndTime() != null) {
      auction.setEndTime(request.getEndTime());
    }

    auctionDao.update(auction);
    LOGGER.info("Auction updated: id={}", auctionId);
    return enrichAuctionResponse(auction);
  }

  /**
   * HГЎВ»В§y phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ (soft delete ГўвӮ¬вҖқ chuyГЎВ»Ж’n status sang CANCELED).
   *
   * <p>PhГғВўn quyГЎВ»ВҒn:
   *
   * <ul>
   *   <li>ADMIN ГўвҖ вҖҷ hГЎВ»В§y Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc bГЎВәВҘt kГЎВ»Ві phiГғВӘn nГғВ o ГЎВ»Её mГЎВ»ВҚi trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi.
   *   <li>SELLER ГўвҖ вҖҷ chГЎВ»вҖ° hГЎВ»В§y phiГғВӘn cГЎВ»В§a chГғВӯnh mГғВ¬nh, khi status lГғВ  OPEN hoГЎВәВ·c RUNNING (trГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng hГЎВ»ВЈp bГЎВәВҘt
   *       khГЎВәВЈ khГғВЎng).
   *   <li>CГғВЎc role khГғВЎc ГўвҖ вҖҷ {@link UnauthorizedException}.
   * </ul>
   *
   * @param auctionId ID phiГғВӘn cГЎВәВ§n hГЎВ»В§y
   * @param userId ID ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi thГЎВ»Вұc hiГЎВ»вҖЎn (tГЎВ»В« JWT)
   * @param role role cГЎВ»В§a ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi thГЎВ»Вұc hiГЎВ»вҖЎn ("ADMIN" hoГЎВәВ·c "SELLER")
   * @throws NotFoundException nГЎВәВҝu auction khГғВҙng tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi
   * @throws UnauthorizedException nГЎВәВҝu SELLER cГЎВ»вҖҳ hГЎВ»В§y phiГғВӘn cГЎВ»В§a ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi khГғВЎc, hoГЎВәВ·c role khГғВҙng hГЎВ»ВЈp lГЎВ»вҖЎ
   * @throws IllegalStateException nГЎВәВҝu SELLER cГЎВ»вҖҳ hГЎВ»В§y phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГғВЈ FINISHED / PAID / CANCELED
   */
  public void delete(Long auctionId, Long userId, String role) {
    Auction auction =
        auctionDao
            .findById(auctionId)
            .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("Auction not found: " + auctionId));

    // ADMIN: Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc hГЎВ»В§y bГЎВәВҘt chГЎВәВҘp mГЎВ»ВҚi trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi
    if ("ADMIN".equals(role)) {
      auction.setStatus("CANCELED");
      auctionDao.update(auction);
      LOGGER.info("ADMIN (userId={}) Г„вҖҳГғВЈ cГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЎng chГЎВәВҝ hГЎВ»В§y phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ #{}", userId, auctionId);
      return;
    }

    // SELLER: chГЎВ»вҖ° hГЎВ»В§y phiГғВӘn cГЎВ»В§a chГғВӯnh mГғВ¬nh, khi status = OPEN hoГЎВәВ·c RUNNING
    if ("SELLER".equals(role)) {
      Long actualSellerId = auction.getSellerId();
      if (actualSellerId == null) {
        Item item =
            itemDao
                .findById(auction.getItemId())
                .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("Item not found"));
        actualSellerId = item.getSellerId();
      }

      if (!actualSellerId.equals(userId)) {
        throw new UnauthorizedException("BГЎВәВЎn khГғВҙng cГғВі quyГЎВ»ВҒn hГЎВ»В§y phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ cГЎВ»В§a ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi khГғВЎc!");
      }

      String status = auction.getStatus();
      if (!"OPEN".equals(status) && !"RUNNING".equals(status)) {
        throw new IllegalStateException(
            "ChГЎВ»вҖ° cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ hГЎВ»В§y phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ khi Г„вҖҳang ГЎВ»Её trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi OPEN hoГЎВәВ·c RUNNING."
                + " TrГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi: "
                + status);
      }

      auction.setStatus("CANCELED");
      auctionDao.update(auction);
      LOGGER.info(
          "SELLER (userId={}) Г„вҖҳГғВЈ hГЎВ»В§y phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ #{} (trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc: {})",
          userId,
          auctionId,
          status);
      return;
    }

    // CГғВЎc role khГғВЎc (BIDDER, ...) khГғВҙng Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc phГғВ©p
    throw new UnauthorizedException("BГЎВәВЎn khГғВҙng cГғВі quyГЎВ»ВҒn thГЎВ»Вұc hiГЎВ»вҖЎn thao tГғВЎc nГғВ y.");
  }

  /**
   * XГғВіa cГЎВ»В©ng phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ khГЎВ»ВҸi DB (chГЎВ»вҖ° ADMIN). XГғВіa toГғВ n bГЎВ»в„ў bid_transactions vГғВ  auto_bid_configs
   * liГғВӘn quan trong cГғВ№ng mГЎВ»в„ўt transaction.
   */
  public void hardDelete(Long auctionId) {
    auctionDao
        .findById(auctionId)
        .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("Auction not found: " + auctionId));
    auctionDao.hardDelete(auctionId);
    LOGGER.info("Admin hard-deleted auction #{}", auctionId);
  }

  /**
   * Г„ВҗГЎВәВ·t giГғВЎ thГғВҙng qua State pattern (dГғВ№ng trong test vГғВ  AuctionScheduler). KhГғВҙng persist xuГЎВ»вҖҳng DB ГўвӮ¬вҖқ
   * chГЎВ»вҖ° validate state vГғВ  update in-memory.
   */
  public void placeBidViaState(Long auctionId, Long bidderId, BigDecimal amount) {
    Auction auction =
        auctionDao
            .findById(auctionId)
            .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("Auction not found: " + auctionId));
    getState(auction).placeBid(auction, amount, bidderId);
  }

  /**
   * ChuyГЎВ»Ж’n trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi OPEN ГўвҖ вҖҷ RUNNING. ChГЎВ»вҖ° hГЎВ»ВЈp lГЎВ»вҖЎ khi auction Г„вҖҳang ГЎВ»Её OPEN. GГЎВ»ВҚi bГЎВ»Еёi AuctionScheduler.
   *
   * @throws AuctionClosedException nГЎВәВҝu auction khГғВҙng ГЎВ»Её trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi OPEN
   */
  public void transitionToRunning(Long auctionId) {
    Auction auction =
        auctionDao
            .findById(auctionId)
            .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("Auction not found: " + auctionId));

    if (!"OPEN".equals(auction.getStatus())) {
      throw new AuctionClosedException(
          "KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ chuyГЎВ»Ж’n sang RUNNING tГЎВ»В« trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi: " + auction.getStatus());
    }

    auction.setStatus("RUNNING");
    auctionDao.update(auction);
    LOGGER.info("Auction #{} ГўвҖ вҖҷ RUNNING", auctionId);
  }

  /**
   * ChuyГЎВ»Ж’n trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi RUNNING ГўвҖ вҖҷ FINISHED. ChГЎВ»вҖ° hГЎВ»ВЈp lГЎВ»вҖЎ khi auction Г„вҖҳang ГЎВ»Её RUNNING. GГЎВ»ВҚi bГЎВ»Еёi
   * AuctionScheduler.
   */
  public void transitionToFinished(Long auctionId) {
    Auction auction =
        auctionDao
            .findById(auctionId)
            .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("Auction not found: " + auctionId));

    if (!"RUNNING".equals(auction.getStatus())) {
      throw new AuctionClosedException(
          "KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ chuyГЎВ»Ж’n sang FINISHED tГЎВ»В« trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi: " + auction.getStatus());
    }

    auction.setStatus("FINISHED");
    auctionDao.update(auction);
    LOGGER.info("Auction #{} ГўвҖ вҖҷ FINISHED", auctionId);
  }

  /**
   * TrГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ AuctionState tГҶВ°ГҶВЎng ГЎВ»В©ng vГЎВ»вҖәi trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi cГЎВ»В§a auction. DГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ delegate behavior
   * theo State pattern.
   *
   * @param auction auction cГЎВәВ§n resolve state
   * @return AuctionState implementation tГҶВ°ГҶВЎng ГЎВ»В©ng
   */
  public AuctionState getState(Auction auction) {
    return switch (auction.getStatus()) {
      case "OPEN" -> new OpenState();
      case "RUNNING" -> new RunningState();
      case "FINISHED" -> new FinishedState();
      case "PAID" -> new PaidState();
      case "CANCELED" -> new CanceledState();
      default -> throw new IllegalStateException("Unknown auction status: " + auction.getStatus());
    };
  }

  /**
   * BГЎВ»вҖў sung thГғВҙng tin itemName, leadingBidderUsername vГғВ  cГғВЎc field riГғВӘng theo category (itemBrand,
   * itemArtist, itemYear) vГғВ o AuctionResponse.
   *
   * <p>AuctionResponse.fromAuction() chГЎВ»вҖ° copy dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu tГЎВ»В« Auction model. Method nГғВ y bГЎВ»вҖў sung thГғВӘm
   * thГғВҙng tin tГЎВ»В« bГЎВәВЈng items vГғВ  users, bao gГЎВ»вҖңm cГғВЎc field Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·c thГғВ№ theo loГЎВәВЎi sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m:
   *
   * <ul>
   *   <li>ELECTRONICS ГўвҖ вҖҷ itemBrand (hГғВЈng sГЎВәВЈn xuГЎВәВҘt)
   *   <li>ART ГўвҖ вҖҷ itemArtist (nghГЎВ»вҖЎ sГ„В©)
   *   <li>VEHICLE ГўвҖ вҖҷ itemYear (nГ„Ж’m sГЎВәВЈn xuГЎВәВҘt)
   * </ul>
   */
  private AuctionResponse enrichAuctionResponse(Auction auction) {
    AuctionResponse response = AuctionResponse.fromAuction(auction);

    // BГЎВ»вҖў sung itemName, itemCategory, itemDescription + category-specific fields
    itemDao
        .findById(auction.getItemId())
        .ifPresent(
            item -> {
              response.setItemName(item.getName());
              response.setItemCategory(item.getCategory());
              response.setItemDescription(item.getDescription());

              // BГЎВ»вҖў sung field Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·c thГғВ№ theo loГЎВәВЎi sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m (dГғВ№ng pattern matching Java 21)
              if (item instanceof Electronics electronics) {
                response.setItemBrand(electronics.getBrand());
              } else if (item instanceof Art art) {
                response.setItemArtist(art.getArtist());
              } else if (item instanceof Vehicle vehicle) {
                response.setItemYear(vehicle.getYear());
              }
            });

    // BГЎВ»вҖў sung leadingBidderUsername
    if (auction.getLeadingBidderId() != null) {
      userDao
          .findById(auction.getLeadingBidderId())
          .ifPresent(user -> response.setLeadingBidderUsername(user.getUsername()));
    }

    return response;
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\service\BidService.java ==========
package com.auction.service;

import com.auction.dao.AuctionDao;
import com.auction.dao.AutoBidConfigDao;
import com.auction.dao.BidTransactionDao;
import com.auction.dao.UserDao;
import com.auction.dto.BidUpdateMessage;
import com.auction.exception.InvalidBidException;
import com.auction.exception.NotFoundException;
import com.auction.model.Auction;
import com.auction.model.BidTransaction;
import com.auction.model.User;
import com.auction.pattern.observer.AuctionEventManager;
import com.auction.pattern.strategy.AutoBidStrategy;
import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicBoolean;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicReference;
import org.jdbi.v3.core.Jdbi;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * Service xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ logic Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t giГғВЎ ГўвӮ¬вҖқ trung tГғВўm cГЎВ»В§a toГғВ n bГЎВ»в„ў hГЎВ»вҖЎ thГЎВ»вҖҳng Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ.
 *
 * <p><b>LuГЎВ»вҖңng xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ {@code placeBid()}:</b>
 *
 * <pre>
 *   1. Validate input (giГғВЎ > 0)
 *   2. jdbi.inTransaction():
 *      a. findByIdForUpdate ГўвҖ вҖҷ SELECT FOR UPDATE khГғВіa row
 *      b. auctionService.getState(auction).placeBid() ГўвҖ вҖҷ State pattern validate + update in-memory
 *      c. Anti-sniping: nГЎВәВҝu cГғВІn &lt; 30s ГўвҖ вҖҷ gia hГЎВәВЎn 60s
 *      d. updateInTransaction ГўвҖ вҖҷ lГҶВ°u giГғВЎ + endTime atomically
 *      e. bidTransactionDao.insert(handle) ГўвҖ вҖҷ ghi bid trong cГғВ№ng transaction
 *   3. Notify TIME_EXTENDED nГЎВәВҝu anti-sniping triggered
 *   4. Notify BID_UPDATE qua WebSocket
 *   5. triggerAutoBid() nГЎВәВҝu lГғВ  manual bid
 * </pre>
 *
 * <p><b>Concurrency:</b> {@code SELECT FOR UPDATE} trong transaction bГЎВәВЈo vГЎВ»вҖЎ khi nhiГЎВ»ВҒu server
 * instance chГЎВәВЎy song song. KhГғВҙng cГЎВәВ§n {@code synchronized} trong ГЎВ»В©ng dГЎВ»ВҘng.
 */
public class BidService {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(BidService.class);

  private static final long ANTI_SNIPE_THRESHOLD_MS = 30_000L;
  private static final long ANTI_SNIPE_EXTENSION_SECONDS = 60L;

  private final AuctionDao auctionDao;
  private final BidTransactionDao bidTransactionDao;
  private final AutoBidConfigDao autoBidConfigDao;
  private final AuctionEventManager eventManager;
  private final Jdbi jdbi;
  private final AuctionService auctionService;
  private final UserDao userDao;
  private final AutoBidStrategy autoBidStrategy;

  public BidService(
      AuctionDao auctionDao,
      BidTransactionDao bidTransactionDao,
      AutoBidConfigDao autoBidConfigDao,
      AuctionEventManager eventManager,
      Jdbi jdbi,
      AuctionService auctionService,
      UserDao userDao) {
    this.auctionDao = auctionDao;
    this.bidTransactionDao = bidTransactionDao;
    this.autoBidConfigDao = autoBidConfigDao;
    this.eventManager = eventManager;
    this.jdbi = jdbi;
    this.auctionService = auctionService;
    this.userDao = userDao;
    this.autoBidStrategy = new AutoBidStrategy(autoBidConfigDao);
  }

  /**
   * Г„ВҗГЎВәВ·t giГғВЎ cho mГЎВ»в„ўt phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ.
   *
   * @param auctionId ID phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @param bidderId ID ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t giГғВЎ (tГЎВ»В« JWT token)
   * @param amount sГЎВ»вҖҳ tiГЎВ»ВҒn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t giГғВЎ (phГЎВәВЈi > currentPrice)
   * @param isAutoBid {@code true} nГЎВәВҝu Г„вҖҳГғВўy lГғВ  auto-bid
   * @return BidTransaction Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc lГҶВ°u vГғВ o DB
   */
  public BidTransaction placeBid(
      Long auctionId, Long bidderId, BigDecimal amount, boolean isAutoBid) {

    if (amount == null || amount.signum() <= 0) {
      throw new InvalidBidException("GiГғВЎ bid phГЎВәВЈi lГЎВ»вҖәn hГҶВЎn 0");
    }

    User bidder =
        userDao
            .findById(bidderId)
            .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("Bidder not found: " + bidderId));
    BigDecimal balance = bidder.getBalance() != null ? bidder.getBalance() : BigDecimal.ZERO;
    if (balance.compareTo(amount) < 0) {
      throw new InvalidBidException(
          "SГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ° khГғВҙng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»В§. SГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ° hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi: "
              + balance
              + ", giГғВЎ bid: "
              + amount
              + ". Vui lГғВІng nГЎВәВЎp thГғВӘm tiГЎВ»ВҒn.");
    }

    AtomicReference<Auction> auctionRef = new AtomicReference<>();
    AtomicBoolean antiSnipeTriggered = new AtomicBoolean(false);

    BidTransaction savedTransaction =
        jdbi.inTransaction(
            handle -> {
              Auction auction;
              try {
                auction = auctionDao.findByIdForUpdate(handle, auctionId);
              } catch (IllegalStateException e) {
                throw new NotFoundException("Auction not found with id: " + auctionId);
              }
              auctionRef.set(auction);

              // State pattern: validates amount > currentPrice, bidderId != sellerId,
              // and updates auction in-memory. Throws on failure.
              auctionService.getState(auction).placeBid(auction, amount, bidderId);

              if (auction.getRemainingTimeMs() < ANTI_SNIPE_THRESHOLD_MS) {
                auction.setEndTime(auction.getEndTime().plusSeconds(ANTI_SNIPE_EXTENSION_SECONDS));
                antiSnipeTriggered.set(true);
              }

              // Single atomic write: persists both price update and any endTime extension
              auctionDao.updateInTransaction(handle, auction);
              BidTransaction tx = new BidTransaction(auctionId, bidderId, amount, isAutoBid);
              return bidTransactionDao.insert(handle, tx);
            });

    Auction auction = auctionRef.get();

    LOGGER.info(
        "Bid Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t thГғВ nh cГғВҙng: auction={}, bidder={}, amount={}, autoBid={}",
        auctionId,
        bidderId,
        amount,
        isAutoBid);

    if (antiSnipeTriggered.get()) {
      BidUpdateMessage timeMsg = BidUpdateMessage.timeExtended(auctionId, auction.getEndTime());
      eventManager.notifyTimeExtended(auctionId, timeMsg);
      LOGGER.info(
          "Anti-sniping kГғВӯch hoГЎВәВЎt cho phiГғВӘn #{}: gia hГЎВәВЎn thГғВӘm {}s",
          auctionId,
          ANTI_SNIPE_EXTENSION_SECONDS);
    }

    notifyBidUpdate(auction, auctionId, bidderId, amount, isAutoBid);

    if (!isAutoBid) {
      triggerAutoBid(auctionId, amount, bidderId);
    }

    return savedTransaction;
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy lГЎВ»вҖ№ch sГЎВ»Вӯ bid cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ.
   *
   * @param auctionId ID phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ
   * @return danh sГғВЎch BidTransaction sГЎВәВҜp xГЎВәВҝp theo thГЎВ»Вқi gian tГ„Ж’ng dГЎВәВ§n
   * @throws NotFoundException nГЎВәВҝu auction khГғВҙng tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi
   */
  public List<BidTransaction> getBidHistory(Long auctionId) {
    if (!auctionDao.existsById(auctionId)) {
      throw new NotFoundException("Auction not found with id: " + auctionId);
    }
    return bidTransactionDao.findByAuctionId(auctionId);
  }

  // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ Private helpers ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬

  private void notifyBidUpdate(
      Auction auction, Long auctionId, Long bidderId, BigDecimal amount, boolean isAutoBid) {
    try {
      String username = userDao.findById(bidderId).map(User::getUsername).orElse(null);
      BidUpdateMessage msg =
          BidUpdateMessage.bidUpdate(
              auctionId, amount, bidderId, username, auction.getEndTime(), isAutoBid);
      eventManager.notifyBidUpdate(auctionId, msg);
    } catch (Exception e) {
      LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i khi notify BID_UPDATE cho phiГғВӘn #{}: {}", auctionId, e.getMessage());
    }
  }

  private void triggerAutoBid(Long auctionId, BigDecimal currentPrice, Long leadingBidderId) {
    try {
      autoBidStrategy.executeAll(
          auctionId,
          currentPrice,
          leadingBidderId,
          (aid, bid, amt) -> this.placeBid(aid, bid, amt, true));
    } catch (Exception e) {
      LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i khi xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ auto-bid cho phiГғВӘn #{}: {}", auctionId, e.getMessage());
    }
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\service\ItemService.java ==========
package com.auction.service;

import com.auction.dao.ItemDao;
import com.auction.dto.CreateItemRequest;
import com.auction.exception.NotFoundException;
import com.auction.exception.UnauthorizedException;
import com.auction.model.Item;
import com.auction.pattern.factory.ItemFactory;
import java.util.List;

/**
 * Service xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ toГғВ n bГЎВ»в„ў business logic liГғВӘn quan Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m (Item).
 *
 * <h2>TrГғВЎch nhiГЎВ»вҖЎm cГЎВ»В§a ItemService</h2>
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>TГЎВәВЎo item Г„вҖҳГғВәng subclass thГғВҙng qua {@link ItemFactory} (Factory Method pattern)
 *   <li>KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra quyГЎВ»ВҒn sГЎВ»Её hГЎВ»ВҜu (ownership) trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc khi cho phГғВ©p sГЎВ»Вӯa/xГғВіa
 *   <li>Delegate tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ SQL operation xuГЎВ»вҖҳng {@link ItemDao}
 * </ul>
 *
 * <h2>VГЎВ»вҖ№ trГғВӯ trong kiГЎВәВҝn trГғВәc</h2>
 *
 * <pre>
 * ItemController (A viГЎВәВҝt)
 *       ГўвҖқвҖҡ  gГЎВ»ВҚi
 *       ГўвҖ“Вј
 * ItemService  ГўвҖ”вҖһГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ bГЎВәВЎn Г„вҖҳang ГЎВ»Её Г„вҖҳГғВўy
 *   ГўвҖқвҖҡ         ГўвҖқвҖҡ
 *   ГўвҖқвҖҡ dГғВ№ng    ГўвҖқвҖҡ delegate SQL
 *   ГўвҖ“Вј         ГўвҖ“Вј
 * ItemFactory  ItemDao (A viГЎВәВҝt)
 * </pre>
 *
 * <h2>NguyГғВӘn tГЎВәВҜc phГғВўn tГЎВәВ§ng</h2>
 *
 * <p>ItemService khГғВҙng biГЎВәВҝt vГЎВ»ВҒ HTTP, khГғВҙng biГЎВәВҝt vГЎВ»ВҒ SQL. NГғВі chГЎВ»вҖ° biГЎВәВҝt vГЎВ»ВҒ business rules: "ai Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc tГЎВәВЎo
 * item?", "ai Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc sГЎВ»Вӯa item?", "item Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc tГЎВәВЎo bГЎВәВұng cГғВЎch nГғВ o?" MГЎВ»ВҚi chi tiГЎВәВҝt HTTP thuГЎВ»в„ўc vГЎВ»ВҒ
 * Controller, mГЎВ»ВҚi chi tiГЎВәВҝt SQL thuГЎВ»в„ўc vГЎВ»ВҒ DAO.
 */
public class ItemService {

  private final ItemDao itemDao;

  /**
   * Constructor injection ГўвӮ¬вҖқ ItemDao Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc inject tГЎВ»В« bГғВӘn ngoГғВ i Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ dГЎВ»вҖҰ mock trong test.
   *
   * @param itemDao DAO Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ thГЎВ»Вұc hiГЎВ»вҖЎn cГғВЎc thao tГғВЎc SQL trГғВӘn bГЎВәВЈng items
   */
  public ItemService(ItemDao itemDao) {
    this.itemDao = itemDao;
  }

  /**
   * TГЎВәВЎo sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m mГЎВ»вҖәi cho seller.
   *
   * <p>LuГЎВ»вҖңng xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ:
   *
   * <ol>
   *   <li>Delegate sang {@link ItemFactory#create} Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ tГЎВәВЎo Г„вҖҳГғВәng subclass theo category
   *   <li>Persist item mГЎВ»вҖәi xuГЎВ»вҖҳng database qua {@link ItemDao#insert}
   *   <li>TrГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ item Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГғВЎn id tГЎВ»В« DB
   * </ol>
   *
   * @param req request chГЎВ»В©a name, description, category, categoryDetail
   * @param sellerId ID cГЎВ»В§a seller Г„вҖҳang tГЎВәВЎo ГўвӮ¬вҖқ lГҶВ°u vГғВ o item Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ check ownership sau nГғВ y
   * @return item Г„вҖҳГғВЈ lГҶВ°u vГғВ o DB vГЎВ»вҖәi id Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГғВЎn
   * @throws IllegalArgumentException nГЎВәВҝu category khГғВҙng hГЎВ»ВЈp lГЎВ»вҖЎ (tГЎВ»В« ItemFactory)
   */
  public Item create(CreateItemRequest req, Long sellerId) {
    // Factory tГЎВәВЎo Г„вҖҳГғВәng subclass (Electronics/Art/Vehicle) dГЎВ»Вұa trГғВӘn req.getCategory()
    Item item = ItemFactory.create(req, sellerId);

    // Persist xuГЎВ»вҖҳng DB ГўвӮ¬вҖқ DAO trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ item vГЎВ»вҖәi id Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГғВЎn
    return itemDao.insert(item);
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m trong hГЎВ»вҖЎ thГЎВ»вҖҳng.
   *
   * <p>KhГғВҙng cГғВі filter ГўвӮ¬вҖқ dГғВ№ng cho admin hoГЎВәВ·c danh sГғВЎch cГғВҙng khai. Xem {@link #getBySellerId} nГЎВәВҝu
   * cГЎВәВ§n lГЎВ»ВҚc theo seller.
   *
   * @return danh sГғВЎch tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ items, cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ rГЎВ»вҖ”ng nГЎВәВҝu chГҶВ°a cГғВі item nГғВ o
   */
  public List<Item> getAll() {
    return itemDao.findAll();
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m cГЎВ»В§a mГЎВ»в„ўt seller cГЎВ»ВҘ thГЎВ»Ж’.
   *
   * <p>DГғВ№ng trong form tГЎВәВЎo phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ: seller chГЎВ»ВҚn item cГЎВ»В§a mГғВ¬nh tГЎВ»В« danh sГғВЎch nГғВ y.
   *
   * @param sellerId ID cГЎВ»В§a seller cГЎВәВ§n lГЎВәВҘy danh sГғВЎch item
   * @return danh sГғВЎch items cГЎВ»В§a seller, cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ rГЎВ»вҖ”ng
   */
  public List<Item> getBySellerId(Long sellerId) {
    return itemDao.findBySellerId(sellerId);
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy thГғВҙng tin chi tiГЎВәВҝt mГЎВ»в„ўt sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m theo ID.
   *
   * @param id ID cГЎВ»В§a item cГЎВәВ§n lГЎВәВҘy
   * @return item tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy
   * @throws NotFoundException nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng cГғВі item vГЎВ»вҖәi id nГғВ y
   */
  public Item getById(Long id) {
    return itemDao
        .findById(id)
        .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("SГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m #" + id + " khГғВҙng tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi"));
  }

  /**
   * CГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt thГғВҙng tin sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m.
   *
   * <p>ChГЎВ»вҖ° seller sГЎВ»Её hГЎВ»ВҜu item mГЎВ»вҖәi Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc phГғВ©p cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt. Admin khГғВҙng cГғВі quyГЎВ»ВҒn sГЎВ»Вӯa item (chГЎВ»вҖ° cГғВі quyГЎВ»ВҒn
   * xГғВіa).
   *
   * @param id ID cГЎВ»В§a item cГЎВәВ§n cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt
   * @param updatedItem item vГЎВ»вҖәi thГғВҙng tin mГЎВ»вҖәi (name, description, v.v.)
   * @param requesterId ID cГЎВ»В§a ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi Г„вҖҳang thГЎВ»Вұc hiГЎВ»вҖЎn request (tГЎВ»В« JWT)
   * @throws NotFoundException nГЎВәВҝu item khГғВҙng tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi
   * @throws UnauthorizedException nГЎВәВҝu requester khГғВҙng phГЎВәВЈi seller sГЎВ»Её hГЎВ»ВҜu item nГғВ y
   */
  public Item update(Long id, Item updatedItem, Long requesterId) {
    Item existing = getById(id); // throw NotFoundException nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng cГғВі
    checkOwnership(existing, requesterId, "cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt");

    updatedItem.setId(id);
    updatedItem.setSellerId(existing.getSellerId()); // sellerId khГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ thay Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi
    itemDao.update(updatedItem);
    return updatedItem;
  }

  /**
   * CГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m tГЎВ»В« request DTO ГўвӮ¬вҖқ dГғВ№ng bГЎВ»Еёi ItemController.
   *
   * <p>DГғВ№ng {@link ItemFactory} Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ tГЎВәВЎo lГЎВәВЎi subclass Г„вҖҳГғВәng loГЎВәВЎi tГЎВ»В« request, sau Г„вҖҳГғВі delegate sang
   * {@link #update(Long, Item, Long)}.
   *
   * @param id ID cГЎВ»В§a item cГЎВәВ§n cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt
   * @param request dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu mГЎВ»вҖәi tГЎВ»В« client
   * @param requesterId ID ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi thГЎВ»Вұc hiГЎВ»вҖЎn (tГЎВ»В« JWT)
   * @return item Г„вҖҳГғВЈ cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt
   */
  public Item update(Long id, CreateItemRequest request, Long requesterId) {
    Item existing = getById(id);
    checkOwnership(existing, requesterId, "cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt");

    Item updatedItem = ItemFactory.create(request, existing.getSellerId());
    updatedItem.setId(id);
    itemDao.update(updatedItem);
    return updatedItem;
  }

  /**
   * XГғВіa sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m khГЎВ»ВҸi hГЎВ»вҖЎ thГЎВ»вҖҳng.
   *
   * <p>Seller chГЎВ»вҖ° Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc xГғВіa item cГЎВ»В§a mГғВ¬nh. Admin cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ xГғВіa bГЎВәВҘt kГЎВ»Ві item nГғВ o.
   *
   * <p><b>LГҶВ°u ГғВҪ:</b> NГЎВәВҝu item Г„вҖҳang Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc dГғВ№ng trong phiГғВӘn RUNNING, viГЎВ»вҖЎc xГғВіa cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ gГғВўy lГЎВ»вҖ”i foreign
   * key constraint ГЎВ»Её DB ГўвӮ¬вҖқ cГЎВәВ§n xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ cascade hay block ГЎВ»Её tГЎВәВ§ng DB.
   *
   * @param id ID cГЎВ»В§a item cГЎВәВ§n xГғВіa
   * @param requesterId ID cГЎВ»В§a ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi thГЎВ»Вұc hiГЎВ»вҖЎn request
   * @param requesterRole role cГЎВ»В§a ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi thГЎВ»Вұc hiГЎВ»вҖЎn ("SELLER", "ADMIN")
   * @throws NotFoundException nГЎВәВҝu item khГғВҙng tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi
   * @throws UnauthorizedException nГЎВәВҝu SELLER cГЎВ»вҖҳ xГғВіa item cГЎВ»В§a ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi khГғВЎc
   */
  public void delete(Long id, Long requesterId, String requesterRole) {
    Item existing = getById(id); // throw NotFoundException nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng cГғВі

    // Admin cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ xГғВіa mГЎВ»ВҚi item. Seller chГЎВ»вҖ° xГғВіa item cГЎВ»В§a mГғВ¬nh
    if (!"ADMIN".equals(requesterRole)) {
      checkOwnership(existing, requesterId, "xГғВіa");
    }

    itemDao.delete(id);
  }

  /**
   * KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra quyГЎВ»ВҒn sГЎВ»Её hГЎВ»ВҜu: ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi request phГЎВәВЈi lГғВ  seller cГЎВ»В§a item.
   *
   * @param item item cГЎВәВ§n kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra
   * @param requesterId ID ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi Г„вҖҳang request
   * @param action tГғВӘn hГғВ nh Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng (dГғВ№ng trong error message, vГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ: "cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt", "xГғВіa")
   * @throws UnauthorizedException nГЎВәВҝu requesterId khГғВЎc sellerId cГЎВ»В§a item
   */
  private void checkOwnership(Item item, Long requesterId, String action) {
    if (!item.getSellerId().equals(requesterId)) {
      throw new UnauthorizedException(
          "BГЎВәВЎn khГғВҙng cГғВі quyГЎВ»ВҒn "
              + action
              + " sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m #"
              + item.getId()
              + " vГғВ¬ bГЎВәВЎn khГғВҙng phГЎВәВЈi ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi tГЎВәВЎo sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m nГғВ y");
    }
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\service\PasswordResetService.java ==========
package com.auction.service;

import at.favre.lib.crypto.bcrypt.BCrypt;
import com.auction.dao.PasswordResetRequestDao;
import com.auction.dao.UserDao;
import com.auction.exception.DuplicateException;
import com.auction.exception.NotFoundException;
import com.auction.model.PasswordResetRecord;
import com.auction.model.User;
import java.util.List;

/**
 * DГЎВ»вҖ№ch vГЎВ»ВҘ quГЎВәВЈn lГғВҪ yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t lГЎВәВЎi mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u qua Admin.
 *
 * <p>LuГЎВ»вҖңng hoГЎВәВЎt Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng:
 *
 * <ol>
 *   <li>User gГЎВ»ВҚi {@link #requestReset(String)} vГЎВ»вҖәi email Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ ГўвҖ вҖҷ tГЎВәВЎo bГЎВәВЈn ghi PENDING.
 *   <li>Admin xem danh sГғВЎch PENDING qua {@link #getPendingRequests()}.
 *   <li>Admin duyГЎВ»вҖЎt qua {@link #approveReset(Long)} ГўвҖ вҖҷ mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u reset vГЎВ»ВҒ {@code "123456"}.
 *   <li>HoГЎВәВ·c Admin tГЎВ»В« chГЎВ»вҖҳi qua {@link #rejectReset(Long)}.
 * </ol>
 */
public class PasswordResetService {

  private static final String DEFAULT_PASSWORD = "123456";

  private final UserDao userDao;
  private final PasswordResetRequestDao resetDao;

  public PasswordResetService(UserDao userDao, PasswordResetRequestDao resetDao) {
    this.userDao = userDao;
    this.resetDao = resetDao;
  }

  /**
   * TГЎВәВЎo yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t lГЎВәВЎi mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u cho tГғВ i khoГЎВәВЈn cГғВі email tГҶВ°ГҶВЎng ГЎВ»В©ng.
   *
   * @param email email Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ
   * @throws NotFoundException nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy tГғВ i khoГЎВәВЈn
   * @throws DuplicateException nГЎВәВҝu user Г„вҖҳГғВЈ cГғВі yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u Г„вҖҳang chГЎВ»Вқ xГғВ©t duyГЎВ»вҖЎt
   */
  public void requestReset(String email) {
    User user =
        userDao
            .findByEmail(email.toLowerCase().trim())
            .orElseThrow(
                () -> new NotFoundException("KhГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy tГғВ i khoГЎВәВЈn vГЎВ»вҖәi email: " + email));

    if (resetDao.hasPendingRequest(user.getId())) {
      throw new DuplicateException("BГЎВәВЎn Г„вҖҳГғВЈ cГғВі yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u Г„вҖҳang chГЎВ»Вқ Admin xГғВ©t duyГЎВ»вҖЎt.");
    }

    resetDao.insert(new PasswordResetRecord(user.getId()));
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy danh sГғВЎch yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u Г„вҖҳang chГЎВ»Вқ duyГЎВ»вҖЎt ГўвӮ¬вҖқ dГғВ nh cho Admin.
   *
   * @return danh sГғВЎch PasswordResetRecord cГғВі status = PENDING
   */
  public List<PasswordResetRecord> getPendingRequests() {
    return resetDao.findByStatus("PENDING");
  }

  /**
   * Admin phГғВӘ duyГЎВ»вҖЎt: Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t lГЎВәВЎi mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u vГЎВ»ВҒ {@code "123456"}, Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi status ГўвҖ вҖҷ APPROVED.
   *
   * @param requestId ID cГЎВ»В§a yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u
   * @throws NotFoundException nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u hoГЎВәВ·c tГғВ i khoГЎВәВЈn
   * @throws IllegalStateException nГЎВәВҝu yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ rГЎВ»вҖңi
   */
  public void approveReset(Long requestId) {
    PasswordResetRecord record =
        resetDao
            .findById(requestId)
            .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("KhГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u: " + requestId));

    if (!"PENDING".equals(record.getStatus())) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("YГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u nГғВ y Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ rГЎВ»вҖңi.");
    }

    User user =
        userDao
            .findById(record.getUserId())
            .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("User not found: " + record.getUserId()));

    user.setPasswordHash(BCrypt.withDefaults().hashToString(12, DEFAULT_PASSWORD.toCharArray()));
    userDao.update(user);
    resetDao.updateStatus(requestId, "APPROVED");
  }

  /**
   * Admin tГЎВ»В« chГЎВ»вҖҳi yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u: Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi status ГўвҖ вҖҷ REJECTED, khГғВҙng thay Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u.
   *
   * @param requestId ID cГЎВ»В§a yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u
   * @throws NotFoundException nГЎВәВҝu khГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u
   * @throws IllegalStateException nГЎВәВҝu yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ rГЎВ»вҖңi
   */
  public void rejectReset(Long requestId) {
    PasswordResetRecord record =
        resetDao
            .findById(requestId)
            .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("KhГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u: " + requestId));

    if (!"PENDING".equals(record.getStatus())) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("YГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u nГғВ y Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ rГЎВ»вҖңi.");
    }

    resetDao.updateStatus(requestId, "REJECTED");
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\service\UserService.java ==========
package com.auction.service;

import at.favre.lib.crypto.bcrypt.BCrypt;
import com.auction.config.JwtUtil;
import com.auction.dao.DepositRequestDao;
import com.auction.dao.UserDao;
import com.auction.dto.ChangePasswordRequest;
import com.auction.dto.LoginRequest;
import com.auction.dto.RegisterRequest;
import com.auction.dto.UserResponse;
import com.auction.exception.DuplicateException;
import com.auction.exception.NotFoundException;
import com.auction.exception.UnauthorizedException;
import com.auction.model.Bidder;
import com.auction.model.DepositRecord;
import com.auction.model.Seller;
import com.auction.model.User;
import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.util.List;

/** Service xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ logic nghiГЎВ»вҖЎp vГЎВ»ВҘ cho User. */
public class UserService {
  private final UserDao userDao;
  private final DepositRequestDao depositRequestDao;

  public UserService(UserDao userDao, DepositRequestDao depositRequestDao) {
    this.userDao = userDao;
    this.depositRequestDao = depositRequestDao;
  }

  public User register(RegisterRequest req) {
    if (req.getUsername() == null || req.getUsername().trim().isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Username khГғВҙng Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ trГЎВ»вҖҳng");
    }

    String emailRegex = "^[A-Za-z0-9+_.-]+@(.+)$";
    if (req.getEmail() == null || !req.getEmail().matches(emailRegex)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Г„ВҗГЎВ»вҖ№nh dГЎВәВЎng email khГғВҙng hГЎВ»ВЈp lГЎВ»вҖЎ.");
    }

    if (req.getPassword() == null || req.getPassword().length() < 6) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("MГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u phГЎВәВЈi cГғВі ГғВӯt nhГЎВәВҘt 6 kГғВҪ tГЎВ»Вұ.");
    }

    if (userDao.findByUsername(req.getUsername()).isPresent()) {
      throw new DuplicateException("Username '" + req.getUsername() + "' Г„вҖҳГғВЈ tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi!");
    }

    String hashedPassword = BCrypt.withDefaults().hashToString(12, req.getPassword().toCharArray());

    // Java 21 enhanced switch expression ГўвӮ¬вҖқ Issue 7
    User newUser =
        switch (req.getRole().toUpperCase()) {
          case "BIDDER" -> new Bidder();
          case "SELLER" -> new Seller();
          default -> throw new IllegalArgumentException("Role khГғВҙng hГЎВ»ВЈp lГЎВ»вҖЎ: " + req.getRole());
        };

    newUser.setUsername(req.getUsername());
    newUser.setPasswordHash(hashedPassword);
    newUser.setEmail(req.getEmail());

    return userDao.insert(newUser);
  }

  public String login(LoginRequest req) {
    User user =
        userDao
            .findByUsername(req.getUsername())
            .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("KhГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy tГғВ i khoГЎВәВЈn vГЎВ»вҖәi username nГғВ y."));

    BCrypt.Result result =
        BCrypt.verifyer().verify(req.getPassword().toCharArray(), user.getPasswordHash());
    if (!result.verified) {
      throw new UnauthorizedException("Sai mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u.");
    }

    return JwtUtil.createToken(user.getId(), user.getUsername(), user.getRole());
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy role cГЎВ»В§a user theo username ГўвӮ¬вҖқ dГғВ№ng sau Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ cho client.
   *
   * @param username tГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp
   * @return role: "BIDDER", "SELLER", hoГЎВәВ·c "ADMIN"
   * @throws NotFoundException nГЎВәВҝu username khГғВҙng tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi
   */
  public String getRoleByUsername(String username) {
    return userDao
        .findByUsername(username)
        .map(User::getRole)
        .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("KhГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy user: " + username));
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy thГғВҙng tin user theo ID.
   *
   * @param userId ID cГЎВ»В§a user
   * @return UserResponse chГЎВ»В©a thГғВҙng tin user (khГғВҙng cГғВі passwordHash)
   * @throws NotFoundException nГЎВәВҝu user khГғВҙng tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi
   */
  public UserResponse findById(Long userId) {
    User user =
        userDao
            .findById(userId)
            .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("User not found: " + userId));
    return UserResponse.from(user);
  }

  /**
   * Г„ВҗГЎВ»вҖўi mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u ГўвӮ¬вҖқ xГғВЎc minh mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u cГ…В© trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc khi cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt.
   *
   * @param userId ID user tГЎВ»В« JWT
   * @param req request chГЎВ»В©a currentPassword vГғВ  newPassword
   * @throws NotFoundException nГЎВәВҝu user khГғВҙng tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi
   * @throws UnauthorizedException nГЎВәВҝu mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi sai
   */
  public void changePassword(Long userId, ChangePasswordRequest req) {
    if (req.getNewPassword() == null || req.getNewPassword().length() < 6) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("MГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u mГЎВ»вҖәi phГЎВәВЈi cГғВі ГғВӯt nhГЎВәВҘt 6 kГғВҪ tГЎВ»Вұ.");
    }

    User user =
        userDao
            .findById(userId)
            .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("User not found: " + userId));

    BCrypt.Result result =
        BCrypt.verifyer().verify(req.getCurrentPassword().toCharArray(), user.getPasswordHash());
    if (!result.verified) {
      throw new UnauthorizedException("MГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi khГғВҙng Г„вҖҳГғВәng.");
    }

    String newHash = BCrypt.withDefaults().hashToString(12, req.getNewPassword().toCharArray());
    user.setPasswordHash(newHash);
    userDao.update(user);
  }

  /**
   * GГЎВ»Вӯi yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn ГўвӮ¬вҖқ tГЎВәВЎo bГЎВәВЈn ghi PENDING, chГЎВ»Вқ Admin xГғВЎc nhГЎВәВӯn.
   *
   * @param userId ID user tГЎВ»В« JWT
   * @param amount sГЎВ»вҖҳ tiГЎВ»ВҒn muГЎВ»вҖҳn nГЎВәВЎp (phГЎВәВЈi > 0)
   * @return DepositRecord vГЎВ»В«a tГЎВәВЎo (status = PENDING)
   */
  public DepositRecord requestDeposit(Long userId, BigDecimal amount) {
    if (amount == null || amount.signum() <= 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("SГЎВ»вҖҳ tiГЎВ»ВҒn nГЎВәВЎp phГЎВәВЈi lГЎВ»вҖәn hГҶВЎn 0.");
    }
    userDao.findById(userId).orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("User not found: " + userId));
    return depositRequestDao.insert(new DepositRecord(userId, amount));
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy danh sГғВЎch yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn Г„вҖҳang chГЎВ»Вқ duyГЎВ»вҖЎt ГўвӮ¬вҖқ dГғВ nh cho Admin.
   *
   * @return danh sГғВЎch DepositRecord cГғВі status = PENDING
   */
  public List<DepositRecord> getPendingDeposits() {
    return depositRequestDao.findByStatus("PENDING");
  }

  /**
   * Admin phГғВӘ duyГЎВ»вҖЎt yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn: cГЎВ»в„ўng tiГЎВ»ВҒn vГғВ o sГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ° user, Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi status ГўвҖ вҖҷ APPROVED.
   *
   * @param requestId ID cГЎВ»В§a deposit request
   * @return UserResponse sau khi cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt sГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ°
   */
  public UserResponse approveDeposit(Long requestId) {
    DepositRecord record =
        depositRequestDao
            .findById(requestId)
            .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("Deposit request not found: " + requestId));

    if (!"PENDING".equals(record.getStatus())) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("YГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u nГғВ y Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ rГЎВ»вҖңi.");
    }

    User user =
        userDao
            .findById(record.getUserId())
            .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("User not found: " + record.getUserId()));

    BigDecimal current = user.getBalance() != null ? user.getBalance() : BigDecimal.ZERO;
    user.setBalance(current.add(record.getAmount()));
    userDao.update(user);
    depositRequestDao.updateStatus(requestId, "APPROVED");
    return UserResponse.from(user);
  }

  /**
   * Admin tГЎВ»В« chГЎВ»вҖҳi yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn: Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi status ГўвҖ вҖҷ REJECTED, khГғВҙng cГЎВ»в„ўng tiГЎВ»ВҒn.
   *
   * @param requestId ID cГЎВ»В§a deposit request
   * @return userId cГЎВ»В§a ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi gГЎВ»Вӯi yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u ГўвӮ¬вҖқ dГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ notify WebSocket
   */
  public Long rejectDeposit(Long requestId) {
    DepositRecord record =
        depositRequestDao
            .findById(requestId)
            .orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("Deposit request not found: " + requestId));

    if (!"PENDING".equals(record.getStatus())) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("YГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u nГғВ y Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc xГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ rГЎВ»вҖңi.");
    }
    depositRequestDao.updateStatus(requestId, "REJECTED");
    return record.getUserId();
  }

  /**
   * LГЎВәВҘy tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ user ГўвӮ¬вҖқ dГғВ nh cho Admin.
   *
   * @return danh sГғВЎch UserResponse cГЎВ»В§a toГғВ n bГЎВ»в„ў ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng
   */
  public List<UserResponse> getAll() {
    return userDao.findAll().stream().map(UserResponse::from).toList();
  }

  /**
   * XГғВіa user theo ID ГўвӮ¬вҖқ chГЎВ»вҖ° Admin cГғВі quyГЎВ»ВҒn gГЎВ»ВҚi.
   *
   * @param userId ID user cГЎВәВ§n xГғВіa
   * @throws NotFoundException nГЎВәВҝu user khГғВҙng tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi
   */
  public void delete(Long userId) {
    userDao.findById(userId).orElseThrow(() -> new NotFoundException("User not found: " + userId));
    userDao.delete(userId);
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\ui\controller\AdminPanelController.java ==========
package com.auction.ui.controller;

import com.auction.dto.AuctionResponse;

import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.net.http.HttpResponse;

import java.time.format.DateTimeFormatter;

import javafx.animation.KeyFrame;
import javafx.animation.Timeline;
import javafx.application.Platform;
