                                            NotificationStore.getInstance()
                                                .add(
                                                    "SГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ° tГ„Ж’ng +"
                                                        + VND.format(diff)
                                                        + " ГўвӮ¬вҖқ yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc duyГЎВ»вҖЎt");
                                          }
                                          lastKnownBalance = bal;
                                        });
                                  }
                                }
                              } catch (Exception e) {
                                LOGGER.debug("Balance poll lГЎВ»вҖ”i: {}", e.getMessage());
                              }
                            })));
    balancePollTimeline.setCycleCount(Timeline.INDEFINITE);
    balancePollTimeline.play();
  }

  private void stopBalancePoll() {
    if (balancePollTimeline != null) {
      balancePollTimeline.stop();
      balancePollTimeline = null;
    }
  }

  private void setStatus(String text) {
    statusLabel.setText(text);
    statusLabel.setVisible(true);
    statusLabel.setManaged(true);
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\ui\controller\ChangePasswordController.java ==========
package com.auction.ui.controller;

import com.auction.ui.util.Navigable;
import com.auction.ui.util.SceneManager;
import com.auction.util.RestClient;
import java.net.http.HttpResponse;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import javafx.animation.KeyFrame;
import javafx.animation.Timeline;
import javafx.application.Platform;
import javafx.fxml.FXML;
import javafx.scene.control.Button;
import javafx.scene.control.Label;
import javafx.scene.control.PasswordField;
import javafx.util.Duration;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * Controller cho mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u (change-password.fxml).
 *
 * <p><b>MГЎВ»ВҘc Г„вҖҳГғВӯch:</b> Cho phГғВ©p ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp thay Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u bГЎВәВұng cГғВЎch nhГЎВәВӯp mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u
 * hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi vГғВ  mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u mГЎВ»вҖәi. GГЎВ»Вӯi request Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn {@code PUT /api/users/me/password}.
 *
 * <p><b>VГЎВ»вҖ№ trГғВӯ trong kiГЎВәВҝn trГғВәc:</b> Г„ВҗГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»ВҒu hГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәng Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn tГЎВ»В« mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh Profile. YГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГғВЈ
 * xГғВЎc thГЎВ»Вұc (JWT token trong SceneManager).
 */
public class ChangePasswordController implements Navigable {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ChangePasswordController.class);

  @FXML private PasswordField currentPasswordField;
  @FXML private PasswordField newPasswordField;
  @FXML private PasswordField confirmPasswordField;
  @FXML private Label statusLabel;
  @FXML private Button changeButton;

  @Override
  public void onNavigatedTo() {
    clearForm();
  }

  /** XГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u ГўвӮ¬вҖқ validate rГЎВ»вҖңi gГЎВ»Вӯi PUT request. */
  @FXML
  public void handleChangePassword() {
    String current = currentPasswordField.getText();
    String newPass = newPasswordField.getText();
    String confirm = confirmPasswordField.getText();

    if (current.isEmpty() || newPass.isEmpty()) {
      showStatus("Vui lГғВІng Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»ВҒn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§y Г„вҖҳГЎВ»В§ thГғВҙng tin.", true);
      return;
    }
    if (newPass.length() < 6) {
      showStatus("MГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u mГЎВ»вҖәi phГЎВәВЈi cГғВі ГғВӯt nhГЎВәВҘt 6 kГғВҪ tГЎВ»Вұ.", true);
      return;
    }
    if (!newPass.equals(confirm)) {
      showStatus("Hai mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u mГЎВ»вҖәi khГғВҙng khГЎВ»вҖәp.", true);
      return;
    }

    changeButton.setDisable(true);
    hideStatus();

    Map<String, String> body = new HashMap<>();
    body.put("currentPassword", current);
    body.put("newPassword", newPass);

    Thread.ofVirtual()
        .start(
            () -> {
              try {
                HttpResponse<String> response = RestClient.put("/api/users/me/password", body);
                Platform.runLater(
                    () -> {
                      int code = response.statusCode();
                      if (code == 200 || code == 204) {
                        showStatus(
                            "Г„ВҗГЎВ»вҖўi mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u thГғВ nh cГғВҙng! TГЎВ»Вұ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng xuГЎВәВҘt sau 3 giГғВўy...", false);
                        new Timeline(
                                new KeyFrame(
                                    Duration.seconds(3), ev -> SceneManager.getInstance().logout()))
                            .play();
                      } else {
                        showStatus("Г„ВҗГЎВ»вҖўi mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u thГЎВәВҘt bГЎВәВЎi. MГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi khГғВҙng Г„вҖҳГғВәng.", true);
                        changeButton.setDisable(false);
                      }
                    });
              } catch (Exception e) {
                LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u", e);
                Platform.runLater(
                    () -> {
                      showStatus("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn server.", true);
                      changeButton.setDisable(false);
                    });
              }
            });
  }

  @FXML
  public void goBack() {
    SceneManager.getInstance().navigateBack("profile.fxml");
  }

  private void showStatus(String msg, boolean isError) {
    statusLabel.setText(msg);
    statusLabel.setStyle(isError ? "-fx-text-fill: #e53935;" : "-fx-text-fill: #43a047;");
    statusLabel.setVisible(true);
    statusLabel.setManaged(true);
  }

  private void hideStatus() {
    statusLabel.setVisible(false);
    statusLabel.setManaged(false);
  }

  private void clearForm() {
    if (currentPasswordField != null) {
      currentPasswordField.clear();
    }
    if (newPasswordField != null) {
      newPasswordField.clear();
    }
    if (confirmPasswordField != null) {
      confirmPasswordField.clear();
    }
    hideStatus();
    if (changeButton != null) {
      changeButton.setDisable(false);
    }
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\ui\controller\CreateAuctionController.java ==========
package com.auction.ui.controller;

import com.auction.model.Item;
import com.auction.ui.util.Navigable;
import com.auction.ui.util.SceneManager;
import com.auction.util.RestClient;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.JavaTimeModule;
import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.net.http.HttpResponse;
import java.time.LocalDate;
import java.time.LocalDateTime;
import java.time.LocalTime;
import java.time.format.DateTimeFormatter;
import java.time.format.DateTimeParseException;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import javafx.application.Platform;
import javafx.collections.FXCollections;
import javafx.fxml.FXML;
import javafx.scene.control.Button;
import javafx.scene.control.ComboBox;
import javafx.scene.control.DatePicker;
import javafx.scene.control.Label;
import javafx.scene.control.ListCell;
import javafx.scene.control.TextField;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * Controller cho mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh tГЎВәВЎo phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ (create-auction.fxml).
 *
 * <p><b>MГЎВ»ВҘc Г„вҖҳГғВӯch:</b> Cho phГғВ©p SELLER tГЎВәВЎo phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ mГЎВ»вҖәi bГЎВәВұng cГғВЎch chГЎВ»ВҚn sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m, Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t giГғВЎ khГЎВ»Еёi
 * Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»Ж’m vГғВ  lГғВӘn lГЎВ»вҖ№ch thГЎВ»Вқi gian bГЎВәВҜt Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§u/kГЎВәВҝt thГғВәc. GГЎВ»Вӯi request Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn {@code POST /api/auctions}.
 *
 * <p><b>CГғВЎc phГҶВ°ГҶВЎng thГЎВ»В©c chГғВӯnh:</b>
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>{@link #onNavigatedTo()} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ Load danh sГғВЎch sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m cГЎВ»В§a seller vГғВ o ComboBox.
 *   <li>{@link #handleCreate()} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ Validate vГғВ  gГЎВ»Вӯi request tГЎВәВЎo phiГғВӘn.
 *   <li>{@link #goToCreateItem()} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ ChuyГЎВ»Ж’n sang mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh tГЎВәВЎo sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m mГЎВ»вҖәi.
 * </ul>
 *
 * <p><b>VГЎВ»вҖ№ trГғВӯ trong kiГЎВәВҝn trГғВәc:</b> CreateAuctionController phГЎВ»ВҘ thuГЎВ»в„ўc vГғВ o ItemController (GET
 * /api/items Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ lГЎВәВҘy danh sГғВЎch) vГғВ  AuctionController (POST /api/auctions Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ tГЎВәВЎo phiГғВӘn).
 * AuctionScheduler phГғВӯa server sГЎВәВҪ tГЎВ»Вұ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng chuyГЎВ»Ж’n trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi phiГғВӘn tГЎВ»В« OPEN ГўвҖ вҖҷ RUNNING ГўвҖ вҖҷ FINISHED.
 */
public class CreateAuctionController implements Navigable {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(CreateAuctionController.class);
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER =
      new ObjectMapper().registerModule(new JavaTimeModule());
  private static final DateTimeFormatter TIME_FMT = DateTimeFormatter.ofPattern("HH:mm");

  @FXML private ComboBox<Item> itemCombo;
  @FXML private TextField startingPriceField;
  @FXML private DatePicker startDatePicker;
  @FXML private TextField startTimeField;
  @FXML private DatePicker endDatePicker;
  @FXML private TextField endTimeField;
  @FXML private Label statusLabel;
  @FXML private Button createButton;

  // ========== NAVIGABLE LIFECYCLE ==========

  /** Load danh sГғВЎch sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m cГЎВ»В§a seller tГЎВ»В« API khi vГғВ o mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh. */
  @Override
  public void onNavigatedTo() {
    clearForm();
    loadMyItems();
  }

  // ========== FXML ACTIONS ==========

  /**
   * XГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ tГЎВәВЎo phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ. Validate: sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m Г„вҖҳГғВЈ chГЎВ»ВҚn, giГғВЎ > 0, thГЎВ»Вқi gian hГЎВ»ВЈp lГЎВ»вҖЎ, endTime >
   * startTime.
   */
  @FXML
  public void handleCreate() {
    Item selectedItem = itemCombo.getValue();
    String priceText = startingPriceField.getText().trim();
    LocalDate startDate = startDatePicker.getValue();
    String startTimeStr = startTimeField.getText().trim();
    LocalDate endDate = endDatePicker.getValue();
    String endTimeStr = endTimeField.getText().trim();

    if (selectedItem == null) {
      showStatus("Vui lГғВІng chГЎВ»ВҚn sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m.", true);
      return;
    }

    BigDecimal startingPrice;
    try {
      startingPrice = new BigDecimal(priceText.replace(",", ""));
      if (startingPrice.compareTo(BigDecimal.ZERO) <= 0) {
        showStatus("GiГғВЎ khГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»Ж’m phГЎВәВЈi lГЎВ»вҖәn hГҶВЎn 0.", true);
        return;
      }
    } catch (NumberFormatException e) {
      showStatus("GiГғВЎ khГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»Ж’m khГғВҙng hГЎВ»ВЈp lГЎВ»вҖЎ.", true);
      return;
    }

    if (startDate == null || startTimeStr.isEmpty()) {
      showStatus("Vui lГғВІng nhГЎВәВӯp ngГғВ y vГғВ  giГЎВ»Вқ bГЎВәВҜt Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§u.", true);
      return;
    }
    if (endDate == null || endTimeStr.isEmpty()) {
      showStatus("Vui lГғВІng nhГЎВәВӯp ngГғВ y vГғВ  giГЎВ»Вқ kГЎВәВҝt thГғВәc.", true);
      return;
    }

    LocalDateTime startTime;
    LocalDateTime endTime;
    try {
      startTime = LocalDateTime.of(startDate, LocalTime.parse(startTimeStr, TIME_FMT));
      endTime = LocalDateTime.of(endDate, LocalTime.parse(endTimeStr, TIME_FMT));
    } catch (DateTimeParseException e) {
      showStatus("Г„ВҗГЎВ»вҖ№nh dГЎВәВЎng giГЎВ»Вқ khГғВҙng hГЎВ»ВЈp lГЎВ»вҖЎ. Vui lГғВІng dГғВ№ng HH:mm (vd: 09:00).", true);
      return;
    }

    if (!endTime.isAfter(startTime)) {
      showStatus("ThГЎВ»Вқi gian kГЎВәВҝt thГғВәc phГЎВәВЈi sau thГЎВ»Вқi gian bГЎВәВҜt Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§u.", true);
      return;
    }

    createButton.setDisable(true);
    hideStatus();

    Map<String, Object> body = new HashMap<>();
    body.put("itemId", selectedItem.getId());
    body.put("startingPrice", startingPrice);
    body.put("startTime", startTime.toString());
    body.put("endTime", endTime.toString());

    Thread.ofVirtual()
        .start(
            () -> {
              try {
                HttpResponse<String> response = RestClient.post("/api/auctions", body);
                if (response.statusCode() == 201) {
                  // FIX: HiГЎВ»Ж’n thГЎВ»вҖ№ thГғВҙng bГғВЎo thГғВ nh cГғВҙng, sau Г„вҖҳГғВі navigate vГЎВ»ВҒ auction-list
                  Platform.runLater(
                      () -> {
                        showStatus("TГЎВәВЎo phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ thГғВ nh cГғВҙng!", false);
                        createButton.setDisable(false);
                      });
                  Thread.sleep(1500);
                  Platform.runLater(
                      () -> SceneManager.getInstance().navigateTo("auction-list.fxml"));
                } else {
                  String msg = extractMessage(response.body(), "TГЎВәВЎo phiГғВӘn thГЎВәВҘt bГЎВәВЎi.");
                  Platform.runLater(
                      () -> {
                        showStatus(msg, true);
                        createButton.setDisable(false);
                      });
                }
              } catch (Exception e) {
                LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i tГЎВәВЎo phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ", e);
                Platform.runLater(
                    () -> {
                      showStatus("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn server.", true);
                      createButton.setDisable(false);
                    });
              }
            });
  }

  /** ChuyГЎВ»Ж’n sang mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh tГЎВәВЎo sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m mГЎВ»вҖәi. */
  @FXML
  public void goToCreateItem() {
    SceneManager.getInstance().navigateTo("create-item.fxml");
  }

  /** Quay lГЎВәВЎi danh sГғВЎch phiГғВӘn. */
  @FXML
  public void goBack() {
    SceneManager.getInstance().navigateBack("auction-list.fxml");
  }

  // ========== DATA LOADING ==========

  /** Load danh sГғВЎch sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m thuГЎВ»в„ўc seller hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi tГЎВ»В« GET /api/items?sellerId=X. */
  private void loadMyItems() {
    Long sellerId = SceneManager.getInstance().getCurrentUserId();
    Thread.ofVirtual()
        .start(
            () -> {
              try {
                HttpResponse<String> response = RestClient.get("/api/items?sellerId=" + sellerId);
                if (response.statusCode() == 200) {
                  List<Item> items = RestClient.parseList(response.body(), Item.class);
                  Platform.runLater(
                      () -> {
                        itemCombo.setItems(FXCollections.observableArrayList(items));
                        itemCombo.setCellFactory(
                            lv ->
                                new ListCell<>() {
                                  @Override
                                  protected void updateItem(Item item, boolean empty) {
                                    super.updateItem(item, empty);
                                    setText(empty || item == null ? null : item.getName());
                                  }
                                });
                        itemCombo.setButtonCell(
                            new ListCell<>() {
                              @Override
                              protected void updateItem(Item item, boolean empty) {
                                super.updateItem(item, empty);
                                setText(
                                    empty || item == null
                                        ? "ChГЎВ»ВҚn sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m cГЎВ»В§a bГЎВәВЎn"
                                        : item.getName());
                              }
                            });
                        if (items.isEmpty()) {
                          showStatus("BГЎВәВЎn chГҶВ°a cГғВі sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m nГғВ o. HГғВЈy tГЎВәВЎo sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc.", true);
                        }
                      });
                }
              } catch (Exception e) {
                LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i load danh sГғВЎch sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m", e);
                Platform.runLater(() -> showStatus("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ tГЎВәВЈi danh sГғВЎch sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m.", true));
              }
            });
  }

  // ========== PRIVATE HELPERS ==========

  private void showStatus(String msg, boolean isError) {
    statusLabel.setText(msg);
    statusLabel.setStyle("");
    statusLabel.getStyleClass().setAll(isError ? "error-label" : "status-label");
    statusLabel.setVisible(true);
    statusLabel.setManaged(true);
  }

  private void hideStatus() {
    statusLabel.setVisible(false);
    statusLabel.setManaged(false);
    statusLabel.setStyle("");
    statusLabel.getStyleClass().setAll("status-label");
  }

  private void clearForm() {
    if (itemCombo != null) {
      itemCombo.setValue(null);
    }
    if (startingPriceField != null) {
      startingPriceField.clear();
    }
    if (startDatePicker != null) {
      startDatePicker.setValue(null);
    }
    if (startTimeField != null) {
      startTimeField.clear();
    }
    if (endDatePicker != null) {
      endDatePicker.setValue(null);
    }
    if (endTimeField != null) {
      endTimeField.clear();
    }
    hideStatus();
    if (createButton != null) {
      createButton.setDisable(false);
    }
  }

  private String extractMessage(String body, String fallback) {
    try {
      return MAPPER.readTree(body).path("message").asText(fallback);
    } catch (Exception e) {
      return fallback;
    }
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\ui\controller\CreateItemController.java ==========
package com.auction.ui.controller;

import com.auction.ui.util.Navigable;
import com.auction.ui.util.SceneManager;
import com.auction.util.RestClient;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.net.http.HttpResponse;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import javafx.application.Platform;
import javafx.fxml.FXML;
import javafx.scene.control.Button;
import javafx.scene.control.ComboBox;
import javafx.scene.control.Label;
import javafx.scene.control.TextArea;
import javafx.scene.control.TextField;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * Controller cho mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh tГЎВәВЎo sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m mГЎВ»вҖәi (create-item.fxml).
 *
 * <p><b>MГЎВ»ВҘc Г„вҖҳГғВӯch:</b> Cho phГғВ©p SELLER tГЎВәВЎo sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m mГЎВ»вҖәi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°a vГғВ o Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ. GГЎВ»Вӯi request Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn {@code
 * POST /api/items} vГЎВ»вҖәi thГғВҙng tin tГғВӘn, mГғВҙ tГЎВәВЈ, danh mГЎВ»ВҘc vГғВ  chi tiГЎВәВҝt danh mГЎВ»ВҘc (brand/artist/nГ„Ж’m sГЎВәВЈn
 * xuГЎВәВҘt tГғВ№y loГЎВәВЎi sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m).
 *
 * <p><b>CГғВЎc phГҶВ°ГҶВЎng thГЎВ»В©c chГғВӯnh:</b>
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>{@link #handleCategoryChange()} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ CГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt label "Chi tiГЎВәВҝt danh mГЎВ»ВҘc" theo loГЎВәВЎi chГЎВ»ВҚn.
 *   <li>{@link #handleCreate()} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ Validate vГғВ  gГЎВ»Вӯi request tГЎВәВЎo sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m.
 *   <li>{@link #goBack()} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ Quay lГЎВәВЎi mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh tГЎВәВЎo phiГғВӘn hoГЎВәВ·c danh sГғВЎch.
 * </ul>
 *
 * <p><b>VГЎВ»вҖ№ trГғВӯ trong kiГЎВәВҝn trГғВәc:</b> CreateItemController sГЎВ»Вӯ dГЎВ»ВҘng Factory Method Pattern (qua
 * ItemService/ItemController phГғВӯa server) Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ tГЎВәВЎo Г„вҖҳГғВәng subclass Item (Electronics, Art, Vehicle) dГЎВ»Вұa
 * trГғВӘn category. SELLER cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ tГЎВәВЎo sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc, sau Г„вҖҳГғВі chГЎВ»ВҚn sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m Г„вҖҳГғВі khi tГЎВәВЎo phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ.
 */
public class CreateItemController implements Navigable {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(CreateItemController.class);
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER = new ObjectMapper();

  @FXML private TextField nameField;
  @FXML private TextArea descriptionField;
  @FXML private ComboBox<String> categoryCombo;
  @FXML private Label categoryDetailLabel;
  @FXML private TextField categoryDetailField;
  @FXML private Label statusLabel;
  @FXML private Button createButton;

  // ========== NAVIGABLE LIFECYCLE ==========

  /** Reset form khi navigate Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh nГғВ y. */
  @Override
  public void onNavigatedTo() {
    clearForm();
  }

  // ========== FXML ACTIONS ==========

  /**
   * CГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt label vГғВ  prompt cГЎВ»В§a trГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng chi tiГЎВәВҝt danh mГЎВ»ВҘc theo category Г„вҖҳГғВЈ chГЎВ»ВҚn. - ELECTRONICS ГўвҖ вҖҷ
   * "ThГҶВ°ГҶВЎng hiГЎВ»вҖЎu" (vd: Apple, Samsung) - ART ГўвҖ вҖҷ "NghГЎВ»вҖЎ sГ„В©" (vd: Van Gogh) - VEHICLE ГўвҖ вҖҷ "NГ„Ж’m sГЎВәВЈn xuГЎВәВҘt"
   * (vd: 2022)
   */
  @FXML
  public void handleCategoryChange() {
    String category = categoryCombo.getValue();
    if (category == null) {
      return;
    }
    switch (category) {
      case "ELECTRONICS" -> {
        categoryDetailLabel.setText("ThГҶВ°ГҶВЎng hiГЎВ»вҖЎu *");
        categoryDetailField.setPromptText("Vd: Apple, Samsung, Sony...");
      }
      case "ART" -> {
        categoryDetailLabel.setText("NghГЎВ»вҖЎ sГ„В© *");
        categoryDetailField.setPromptText("Vd: Van Gogh, Picasso...");
      }
      case "VEHICLE" -> {
        categoryDetailLabel.setText("NГ„Ж’m sГЎВәВЈn xuГЎВәВҘt *");
        categoryDetailField.setPromptText("Vd: 2022");
      }
      default -> {
        categoryDetailLabel.setText("Chi tiГЎВәВҝt danh mГЎВ»ВҘc *");
        categoryDetailField.setPromptText("NhГЎВәВӯp thГғВҙng tin chi tiГЎВәВҝt");
      }
    }
  }

  /**
   * XГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ tГЎВәВЎo sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m mГЎВ»вҖәi. Validate phГғВӯa client: tГғВӘn khГғВҙng trГЎВ»вҖҳng, category Г„вҖҳГғВЈ chГЎВ»ВҚn, categoryDetail
   * khГғВҙng trГЎВ»вҖҳng. GГЎВ»Вӯi {@code POST /api/items} vГЎВ»вҖәi body JSON, hiГЎВ»Ж’n thГЎВ»вҖ№ kГЎВәВҝt quГЎВәВЈ.
   */
  @FXML
  public void handleCreate() {
    String name = nameField.getText().trim();
    String description = descriptionField.getText().trim();
    String category = categoryCombo.getValue();
    String categoryDetail = categoryDetailField.getText().trim();

    if (name.isEmpty()) {
      showStatus("TГғВӘn sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m khГғВҙng Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ trГЎВ»вҖҳng.", true);
      return;
    }
    if (category == null) {
      showStatus("Vui lГғВІng chГЎВ»ВҚn danh mГЎВ»ВҘc.", true);
      return;
    }
    if (categoryDetail.isEmpty()) {
      showStatus("Vui lГғВІng nhГЎВәВӯp thГғВҙng tin chi tiГЎВәВҝt danh mГЎВ»ВҘc.", true);
      return;
    }

    createButton.setDisable(true);
    hideStatus();

    Map<String, String> body = new HashMap<>();
    body.put("name", name);
    body.put("description", description);
    body.put("category", category);
    body.put("categoryDetail", categoryDetail);

    Thread.ofVirtual()
        .start(
            () -> {
              try {
                HttpResponse<String> response = RestClient.post("/api/items", body);
                if (response.statusCode() == 201) {
                  // FIX 1: HiГЎВ»Ж’n thГЎВ»вҖ№ thГғВҙng bГғВЎo thГғВ nh cГғВҙng trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc khi navigate
                  Platform.runLater(() -> showStatus("TГЎВәВЎo sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m thГғВ nh cГғВҙng!", false));
                  Thread.sleep(1500);
                  Platform.runLater(
                      () -> {
                        // FIX 2: DГғВ№ng navigateBack thay vГғВ¬ navigateTo Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ khГғВҙng push
                        // create-item.fxml vГғВ o backStack ГўвӮ¬вҖқ trГғВЎnh Back trong create-auction
                        // lГЎВәВЎi quay vГЎВ»ВҒ create-item thay vГғВ¬ auction-list
                        SceneManager.getInstance().invalidateCache("create-auction.fxml");
                        SceneManager.getInstance().navigateBack("create-auction.fxml");
                      });
                } else {
                  String msg = extractMessage(response.body(), "TГЎВәВЎo sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m thГЎВәВҘt bГЎВәВЎi.");
                  Platform.runLater(
                      () -> {
                        showStatus(msg, true);
                        createButton.setDisable(false);
                      });
                }
              } catch (Exception e) {
                LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i tГЎВәВЎo sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m", e);
                Platform.runLater(
                    () -> {
                      showStatus("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn server.", true);
                      createButton.setDisable(false);
                    });
              }
            });
  }

  /** Quay lГЎВәВЎi mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh tГЎВәВЎo phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ. */
  @FXML
  public void goBack() {
    SceneManager.getInstance().navigateBack("create-auction.fxml");
  }

  // ========== PRIVATE HELPERS ==========

  private void showStatus(String msg, boolean isError) {
    statusLabel.setText(msg);
    statusLabel.setStyle(isError ? "-fx-text-fill: #e53935;" : "-fx-text-fill: #43a047;");
    statusLabel.setVisible(true);
    statusLabel.setManaged(true);
  }

  private void hideStatus() {
    statusLabel.setVisible(false);
    statusLabel.setManaged(false);
  }

  private void clearForm() {
    if (nameField != null) {
      nameField.clear();
    }
    if (descriptionField != null) {
      descriptionField.clear();
    }
    if (categoryCombo != null) {
      categoryCombo.setValue(null);
    }
    if (categoryDetailField != null) {
      categoryDetailField.clear();
    }
    if (categoryDetailLabel != null) {
      categoryDetailLabel.setText("Chi tiГЎВәВҝt danh mГЎВ»ВҘc *");
    }
    hideStatus();
    if (createButton != null) {
      createButton.setDisable(false);
    }
  }

  private String extractMessage(String body, String fallback) {
    try {
      return MAPPER.readTree(body).path("message").asText(fallback);
    } catch (Exception e) {
      return fallback;
    }
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\ui\controller\DepositController.java ==========
package com.auction.ui.controller;

import com.auction.model.DepositRecord;
import com.auction.ui.util.Navigable;
import com.auction.ui.util.SceneManager;
import com.auction.util.NotificationStore;
import com.auction.util.RestClient;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.net.http.HttpResponse;
import java.text.NumberFormat;
import java.time.format.DateTimeFormatter;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import javafx.animation.KeyFrame;
import javafx.animation.Timeline;
import javafx.application.Platform;
import javafx.collections.FXCollections;
import javafx.collections.ObservableList;
import javafx.fxml.FXML;
import javafx.scene.control.Button;
import javafx.scene.control.Label;
import javafx.scene.control.ListView;
import javafx.scene.control.TextField;
import javafx.util.Duration;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * Controller cho mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn (deposit.fxml).
 *
 * <p><b>MГЎВ»ВҘc Г„вҖҳГғВӯch:</b> Cho phГғВ©p BIDDER nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn vГғВ o tГғВ i khoГЎВәВЈn Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ tham gia Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ. GГЎВ»Вӯi request Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn
 * {@code POST /api/users/me/deposit}.
 *
 * <p><b>VГЎВ»вҖ№ trГғВӯ trong kiГЎВәВҝn trГғВәc:</b> Г„ВҗГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»ВҒu hГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәng Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn tГЎВ»В« mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh Profile. YГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГғВЈ
 * xГғВЎc thГЎВ»Вұc.
 */
public class DepositController implements Navigable {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(DepositController.class);
  private static final NumberFormat VND = NumberFormat.getCurrencyInstance(Locale.of("vi", "VN"));
  private static final DateTimeFormatter DATE_FMT = DateTimeFormatter.ofPattern("dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm");
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER =
      new ObjectMapper().registerModule(new com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.JavaTimeModule());

  @FXML private Label balanceLabel;
  @FXML private TextField amountField;
  @FXML private Label statusLabel;
  @FXML private Button depositButton;
  @FXML private ListView<String> historyList;

  private final ObservableList<String> historyItems = FXCollections.observableArrayList();
  private Timeline depositPollTimeline;
  private final Map<Long, String> knownStatuses = new HashMap<>();

  @Override
  public void onNavigatedTo() {
    if (amountField != null) {
      amountField.clear();
    }
    hideStatus();
    if (historyList != null) {
      historyList.setItems(historyItems);
    }
    loadBalance();
    loadHistory();
    startDepositPoll();
  }

  @Override
  public void onNavigatedFrom() {
    stopDepositPoll();
  }

  /** XГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn ГўвӮ¬вҖқ validate sГЎВ»вҖҳ tiГЎВ»ВҒn vГғВ  gГЎВ»Вӯi POST request. */
  @FXML
  public void handleDeposit() {
    String amountText = amountField.getText().trim().replace(",", "");
    BigDecimal amount;
    try {
      amount = new BigDecimal(amountText);
      if (amount.compareTo(BigDecimal.ZERO) <= 0) {
        showStatus("SГЎВ»вҖҳ tiГЎВ»ВҒn nГЎВәВЎp phГЎВәВЈi lГЎВ»вҖәn hГҶВЎn 0.", true);
        return;
      }
    } catch (NumberFormatException e) {
      showStatus("SГЎВ»вҖҳ tiГЎВ»ВҒn khГғВҙng hГЎВ»ВЈp lГЎВ»вҖЎ.", true);
      return;
    }

    depositButton.setDisable(true);
    hideStatus();

    Map<String, Object> body = new HashMap<>();
    body.put("amount", amount);

    Thread.ofVirtual()
        .start(
            () -> {
              try {
                HttpResponse<String> response = RestClient.post("/api/users/me/deposit", body);
                Platform.runLater(
                    () -> {
                      if (response.statusCode() == 202) {
                        showStatus(
                            "YГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u nГЎВәВЎp "
                                + VND.format(amount)
                                + " Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГЎВ»Вӯi. ChГЎВ»Вқ Admin xГғВЎc nhГЎВәВӯn.",
                            false);
                        amountField.clear();
                        loadHistory();
                      } else {
                        String errMsg =
                            "GГЎВ»Вӯi yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u thГЎВәВҘt bГЎВәВЎi (HTTP " + response.statusCode() + ").";
                        try {
                          var node = MAPPER.readTree(response.body());
                          if (node.has("message")) {
                            errMsg = node.get("message").asText();
                          }
                        } catch (Exception ignored) {
                        }
                        showStatus(errMsg, true);
                      }
                      depositButton.setDisable(false);
                    });
              } catch (Exception e) {
                LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn", e);
                Platform.runLater(
                    () -> {
                      showStatus("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn server.", true);
                      depositButton.setDisable(false);
                    });
              }
            });
  }

  @FXML
  public void goBack() {
    SceneManager.getInstance().navigateBack("profile.fxml");
  }

  private void loadBalance() {
    Thread.ofVirtual()
        .start(
            () -> {
              try {
                HttpResponse<String> response = RestClient.get("/api/users/me");
                if (response.statusCode() == 200) {
                  var node = MAPPER.readTree(response.body());
                  if (node.has("balance")) {
                    BigDecimal balance = node.get("balance").decimalValue();
                    Platform.runLater(
                        () -> balanceLabel.setText("SГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ° hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi: " + VND.format(balance)));
                  }
                }
              } catch (Exception e) {
                LOGGER.debug("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ load sГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ°: {}", e.getMessage());
              }
            });
  }

  private void loadHistory() {
    boolean notify = !knownStatuses.isEmpty();
    Thread.ofVirtual()
        .start(
            () -> {
              try {
                HttpResponse<String> response = RestClient.get("/api/users/me/deposit-requests");
                if (response.statusCode() == 200) {
                  List<DepositRecord> records =
                      RestClient.parseList(response.body(), DepositRecord.class);
                  Platform.runLater(() -> applyDepositRecords(records, notify));
                } else {
                  LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i load lГЎВ»вҖ№ch sГЎВ»Вӯ nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn: HTTP {}", response.statusCode());
                }
              } catch (Exception e) {
                LOGGER.error("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ load lГЎВ»вҖ№ch sГЎВ»Вӯ nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn", e);
              }
            });
  }

  /**
   * ГғВҒp dГЎВ»ВҘng danh sГғВЎch DepositRecord lГғВӘn UI. NГЎВәВҝu notify=true thГғВ¬ so sГғВЎnh trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi vГғВ  gГЎВ»Вӯi thГғВҙng bГғВЎo
   * khi cГғВі thay Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi.
   */
  private void applyDepositRecords(List<DepositRecord> records, boolean notify) {
    var items = FXCollections.<String>observableArrayList();
    boolean balanceChanged = false;
    for (DepositRecord r : records) {
      String curr = r.getStatus() != null ? r.getStatus() : "PENDING";
      String statusText =
          switch (curr) {
            case "APPROVED" -> "ГўЕ“вҖң Г„ВҗГғВЈ duyГЎВ»вҖЎt";
            case "REJECTED" -> "ГўЕ“вҖ” TГЎВ»В« chГЎВ»вҖҳi";
            default -> "ГўВҸВі ChГЎВ»Вқ duyГЎВ»вҖЎt";
          };
      String dateStr = r.getCreatedAt() != null ? r.getCreatedAt().format(DATE_FMT) : "ГўвӮ¬вҖқ";
      String amtStr = r.getAmount() != null ? VND.format(r.getAmount()) : "ГўвӮ¬вҖқ";
      items.add(amtStr + "  |  " + statusText + "  |  " + dateStr);

      if (r.getId() != null) {
        String prev = knownStatuses.get(r.getId());
        if (notify && prev != null && !prev.equals(curr)) {
          String notif =
              switch (curr) {
                case "APPROVED" -> "NГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn " + amtStr + " Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc duyГЎВ»вҖЎt ГўЕ“вҖң";
                case "REJECTED" -> "NГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn " + amtStr + " bГЎВ»вҖ№ tГЎВ»В« chГЎВ»вҖҳi ГўЕ“вҖ”";
                default -> "TrГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn " + amtStr + " Г„вҖҳГғВЈ thay Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi";
              };
          NotificationStore.getInstance().add(notif);
          showStatus(notif, "REJECTED".equals(curr));
          if ("APPROVED".equals(curr)) {
            balanceChanged = true;
          }
        }
        knownStatuses.put(r.getId(), curr);
      }
    }
    historyItems.setAll(items);
    if (balanceChanged) {
      loadBalance();
    }
  }

  private void startDepositPoll() {
    stopDepositPoll();
    depositPollTimeline =
        new Timeline(
            new KeyFrame(
                Duration.seconds(4),
                e ->
                    Thread.ofVirtual()
                        .start(
                            () -> {
                              try {
                                HttpResponse<String> response =
                                    RestClient.get("/api/users/me/deposit-requests");
                                if (response.statusCode() == 200) {
                                  List<DepositRecord> records =
                                      RestClient.parseList(response.body(), DepositRecord.class);
                                  Platform.runLater(() -> applyDepositRecords(records, true));
                                }
                              } catch (Exception e2) {
                                LOGGER.debug("Deposit poll lГЎВ»вҖ”i: {}", e2.getMessage());
                              }
                            })));
    depositPollTimeline.setCycleCount(Timeline.INDEFINITE);
    depositPollTimeline.play();
  }

  private void stopDepositPoll() {
    if (depositPollTimeline != null) {
      depositPollTimeline.stop();
      depositPollTimeline = null;
    }
  }

  private void showStatus(String msg, boolean isError) {
    statusLabel.setText(msg);
    statusLabel.setStyle(isError ? "-fx-text-fill: #e53935;" : "-fx-text-fill: #43a047;");
    statusLabel.setVisible(true);
    statusLabel.setManaged(true);
  }

  private void hideStatus() {
    if (statusLabel != null) {
      statusLabel.setVisible(false);
      statusLabel.setManaged(false);
    }
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\ui\controller\ForgotPasswordController.java ==========
package com.auction.ui.controller;

import com.auction.ui.util.Navigable;
import com.auction.ui.util.SceneManager;
import com.auction.util.RestClient;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.net.http.HttpResponse;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import javafx.application.Platform;
import javafx.fxml.FXML;
import javafx.scene.control.Button;
import javafx.scene.control.Label;
import javafx.scene.control.TextField;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * Controller cho mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh quГғВӘn mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u (forgot-password.fxml).
 *
 * <p>LuГЎВ»вҖңng: User nhГЎВәВӯp email ГўвҖ вҖҷ gГЎВ»ВҚi {@code POST /api/auth/forgot-password} ГўвҖ вҖҷ tГЎВәВЎo yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u PENDING ГўвҖ вҖҷ
 * Admin xГғВ©t duyГЎВ»вҖЎt trong Admin Panel ГўвҖ вҖҷ mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc reset vГЎВ»ВҒ {@code "123456"}.
 */
public class ForgotPasswordController implements Navigable {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ForgotPasswordController.class);
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER = new ObjectMapper();

  @FXML private TextField emailField;
  @FXML private Label statusLabel;
  @FXML private Button submitButton;

  @Override
  public void onNavigatedTo() {
    if (emailField != null) {
      emailField.clear();
    }
    if (submitButton != null) {
      submitButton.setDisable(false);
    }
    hideStatus();
  }

  /** GГЎВ»Вӯi yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t lГЎВәВЎi mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u ГўвӮ¬вҖқ tГЎВәВЎo bГЎВәВЈn ghi PENDING Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ Admin duyГЎВ»вҖЎt. */
  @FXML
  public void handleSubmit() {
    String email = emailField.getText().trim();
    if (email.isEmpty() || !email.matches("^[A-Za-z0-9+_.-]+@(.+)$")) {
      showStatus("Vui lГғВІng nhГЎВәВӯp Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖ№a chГЎВ»вҖ° email hГЎВ»ВЈp lГЎВ»вҖЎ.", true);
      return;
    }

    submitButton.setDisable(true);
    hideStatus();

    Thread.ofVirtual()
        .start(
            () -> {
              try {
                Map<String, String> body = new HashMap<>();
                body.put("email", email);
                HttpResponse<String> response = RestClient.post("/api/auth/forgot-password", body);

                if (response.statusCode() == 200) {
                  String msg = extractMessage(response.body(), "Г„ВҗГғВЈ gГЎВ»Вӯi yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u thГғВ nh cГғВҙng.");
                  Platform.runLater(() -> showStatus(msg, false));
                } else {
                  String msg =
                      extractMessage(response.body(), "KhГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy tГғВ i khoГЎВәВЈn vГЎВ»вҖәi email nГғВ y.");
                  Platform.runLater(
                      () -> {
                        showStatus(msg, true);
                        submitButton.setDisable(false);
                      });
                }
              } catch (Exception e) {
                LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i gГЎВ»Вӯi yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u quГғВӘn mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u", e);
                Platform.runLater(
                    () -> {
                      showStatus("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn server. Vui lГғВІng thГЎВ»Вӯ lГЎВәВЎi.", true);
                      submitButton.setDisable(false);
                    });
              }
            });
  }

  /** Quay vГЎВ»ВҒ mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp. */
  @FXML
  public void goBack() {
    SceneManager.getInstance().navigateBack("login.fxml");
  }

  private String extractMessage(String responseBody, String fallback) {
    try {
      JsonNode json = MAPPER.readTree(responseBody);
      return json.has("message") ? json.get("message").asText() : fallback;
    } catch (Exception e) {
      return fallback;
    }
  }

  private void showStatus(String msg, boolean isError) {
    statusLabel.setText(msg);
    statusLabel.setStyle(isError ? "-fx-text-fill: #e53935;" : "-fx-text-fill: #43a047;");
    statusLabel.setVisible(true);
    statusLabel.setManaged(true);
  }

  private void hideStatus() {
    if (statusLabel != null) {
      statusLabel.setVisible(false);
      statusLabel.setManaged(false);
    }
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\ui\controller\LoginController.java ==========
package com.auction.ui.controller;

import com.auction.ui.util.Navigable;
import com.auction.ui.util.SceneManager;
import com.auction.util.RestClient;
import com.auction.util.UserBalanceWatcher;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.net.http.HttpResponse;
import javafx.application.Platform;
import javafx.fxml.FXML;
import javafx.scene.control.Button;
import javafx.scene.control.Label;
import javafx.scene.control.PasswordField;
import javafx.scene.control.TextField;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * Controller cho mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp (login.fxml).
 *
 * <p><b>MГЎВ»ВҘc Г„вҖҳГғВӯch:</b> XГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ luГЎВ»вҖңng Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng: nhГЎВәВӯn username/password, gГЎВ»ВҚi REST API {@code
 * POST /api/auth/login}, lГҶВ°u JWT token vГғВ o {@link SceneManager}, vГғВ  Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»ВҒu hГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәng Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh phГғВ№ hГЎВ»ВЈp
 * theo role.
 *
 * <p><b>CГғВЎc phГҶВ°ГҶВЎng thГЎВ»В©c chГғВӯnh:</b>
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>{@link #handleLogin()} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ GГЎВ»ВҚi API Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp, lГҶВ°u session, Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»ВҒu hГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәng.
 *   <li>{@link #goToRegister()} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ ChuyГЎВ»Ж’n sang mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ.
 *   <li>{@link #goToForgotPassword()} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ ChuyГЎВ»Ж’n sang mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh quГғВӘn mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u.
 *   <li>{@link #onDataReceived(Object)} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ NhГЎВәВӯn role hint tГЎВ»В« WelcomeController.
 * </ul>
 *
 * <p><b>VГЎВ»вҖ№ trГғВӯ trong kiГЎВәВҝn trГғВәc:</b> LoginController nhГЎВәВӯn dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu tГЎВ»В« WelcomeController (role hint),
 * giao tiГЎВәВҝp vГЎВ»вҖәi server qua {@link RestClient}, vГғВ  lГҶВ°u trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi session vГғВ o {@link SceneManager}
 * (JWT token, username, role, userId).
 */
public class LoginController implements Navigable {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(LoginController.class);
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER = new ObjectMapper();

  @FXML private TextField usernameField;
  @FXML private PasswordField passwordField;
  @FXML private Label errorLabel;
  @FXML private Label roleHintLabel;
  @FXML private Button loginButton;

  private String expectedRole;

  // ========== NAVIGABLE LIFECYCLE ==========

  /**
   * NhГЎВәВӯn role hint tГЎВ»В« WelcomeController (vГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ: "BIDDER", "SELLER", "ADMIN"). CГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt subtitle
   * label Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ gГЎВ»ВЈi ГғВҪ ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng.
   */
  @Override
  public void onDataReceived(Object data) {
    if (data instanceof String role) {
      expectedRole = role;
      if (roleHintLabel != null) {
        String label =
            switch (role) {
              case "ADMIN" -> "Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp vГЎВ»вҖәi vai trГғВІ: QuГЎВәВЈn trГЎВ»вҖ№ viГғВӘn";
              case "SELLER" -> "Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp vГЎВ»вҖәi vai trГғВІ: NgГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi bГғВЎn";
              case "BIDDER" -> "Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp vГЎВ»вҖәi vai trГғВІ: NgГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t giГғВЎ";
              default -> "Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp vГЎВ»вҖәi vai trГғВІ: " + role;
            };
        roleHintLabel.setText(label);
      }
    }
  }

  @Override
  public void onNavigatedFrom() {
    expectedRole = null;
  }

  /** Reset form khi navigate trГЎВ»Её lГЎВәВЎi mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh nГғВ y. */
  @Override
  public void onNavigatedTo() {
    clearForm();
  }

  // ========== FXML ACTIONS ==========

  /**
   * XГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ sГЎВ»Вұ kiГЎВ»вҖЎn nhГЎВәВҘn nГғВәt "Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp".
   *
   * <p>LuГЎВ»вҖңng:
   *
   * <ol>
   *   <li>Validate input cГҶВЎ bГЎВәВЈn.
   *   <li>GГЎВ»ВҚi {@code POST /api/auth/login} trГғВӘn luГЎВ»вҖңng nГЎВ»ВҒn.
   *   <li>NГЎВәВҝu thГғВ nh cГғВҙng: lГҶВ°u JWT, username, role vГғВ o SceneManager ГўвҖ вҖҷ Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»ВҒu hГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәng.
   *   <li>NГЎВәВҝu thГЎВәВҘt bГЎВәВЎi: hiГЎВ»Ж’n thГЎВ»вҖ№ thГғВҙng bГғВЎo lГЎВ»вҖ”i.
   * </ol>
   */
  @FXML
  public void handleLogin() {
    String username = usernameField.getText().trim();
    String password = passwordField.getText();

    if (username.isEmpty() || password.isEmpty()) {
      showError("Vui lГғВІng nhГЎВәВӯp Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§y Г„вҖҳГЎВ»В§ tГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp vГғВ  mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u.");
      return;
    }

    loginButton.setDisable(true);
    hideError();

    // GГЎВ»ВҚi API trГғВӘn luГЎВ»вҖңng nГЎВ»ВҒn Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ khГғВҙng block JavaFX thread
    Thread.ofVirtual()
        .start(
            () -> {
              try {
                var body = new java.util.HashMap<String, String>();
                body.put("username", username);
                body.put("password", password);

                HttpResponse<String> response = RestClient.post("/api/auth/login", body);

                if (response.statusCode() == 200) {
                  JsonNode json = MAPPER.readTree(response.body());
                  String token = json.get("token").asText();
                  String role = json.get("role").asText();
                  String uname = json.get("username").asText();
                  long userId = json.get("userId").asLong();

                  Platform.runLater(() -> onLoginSuccess(token, role, uname, userId));
                } else {
                  JsonNode json = MAPPER.readTree(response.body());
                  String msg =
                      json.has("message")
                          ? json.get("message").asText()
                          : "Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp thГЎВәВҘt bГЎВәВЎi. Vui lГғВІng kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra lГЎВәВЎi.";
                  Platform.runLater(
                      () -> {
                        showError(msg);
                        loginButton.setDisable(false);
                      });
                }
              } catch (Exception e) {
                LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi server khi Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp", e);
                Platform.runLater(
                    () -> {
                      showError("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn server. Vui lГғВІng thГЎВ»Вӯ lГЎВәВЎi.");
                      loginButton.setDisable(false);
                    });
              }
            });
  }

  /** ChuyГЎВ»Ж’n sang mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ. */
  @FXML
  public void goToRegister() {
    SceneManager.getInstance().navigateTo("register.fxml");
  }

  /** ChuyГЎВ»Ж’n sang mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh quГғВӘn mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u. */
  @FXML
  public void goToForgotPassword() {
    SceneManager.getInstance().navigateTo("forgot-password.fxml");
  }

  /** Quay lГЎВәВЎi mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh chГғВ o mГЎВ»В«ng. */
  @FXML
  public void goBack() {
    SceneManager.getInstance().navigateBack("welcome.fxml");
  }

  // ========== PRIVATE HELPERS ==========

  /** LГҶВ°u session vГғВ  Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»ВҒu hГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәng Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh phГғВ№ hГЎВ»ВЈp theo role. */
  private void onLoginSuccess(String token, String role, String username, long userId) {
    // KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra role thГЎВ»Вұc tГЎВәВҝ cГғВі khГЎВ»вҖәp vГЎВ»вҖәi cГЎВ»вҖўng Г„вҖҳГғВЈ chГЎВ»ВҚn khГғВҙng
    if (expectedRole != null && !expectedRole.equals(role)) {
      String portalName =
          switch (expectedRole) {
            case "ADMIN" -> "QuГЎВәВЈn trГЎВ»вҖ№ viГғВӘn";
            case "SELLER" -> "NgГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi bГғВЎn";
            case "BIDDER" -> "NgГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t giГғВЎ";
            default -> expectedRole;
          };
      showError(
          "TГғВ i khoГЎВәВЈn nГғВ y khГғВҙng phГЎВәВЈi "
              + portalName
              + ". Vui lГғВІng chГЎВ»ВҚn Г„вҖҳГғВәng vai trГғВІ ГЎВ»Её mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh chГғВ o.");
      loginButton.setDisable(false);
      return;
    }

    SceneManager sm = SceneManager.getInstance();
    sm.setJwtToken(token);
    sm.setCurrentUsername(username);
    sm.setCurrentRole(role);
    sm.setCurrentUserId(userId);

    LOGGER.info("Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp thГғВ nh cГғВҙng: username={}, role={}", username, role);

    // MГЎВ»Её kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi WebSocket riГғВӘng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ nhГЎВәВӯn thГғВҙng bГғВЎo biГЎВәВҝn Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng sГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ°
    if (!"ADMIN".equals(role)) {
      UserBalanceWatcher.getInstance().connect((long) userId, token);
    }

    if ("ADMIN".equals(role)) {
      sm.navigateTo("admin-panel.fxml");
    } else {
      sm.navigateTo("auction-list.fxml");
    }
  }

  private void showError(String message) {
    errorLabel.setText(message);
    errorLabel.setVisible(true);
    errorLabel.setManaged(true);
  }

  private void hideError() {
    errorLabel.setVisible(false);
    errorLabel.setManaged(false);
  }

  private void clearForm() {
    if (usernameField != null) {
      usernameField.clear();
    }
    if (passwordField != null) {
      passwordField.clear();
    }
    // Only reset the hint label when there is no expected role ГўвӮ¬вҖқ onDataReceived may have set it
    if (roleHintLabel != null && expectedRole == null) {
      roleHintLabel.setText("Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp");
    }
    hideError();
    if (loginButton != null) {
      loginButton.setDisable(false);
    }
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\ui\controller\ProfileController.java ==========
package com.auction.ui.controller;

import com.auction.ui.util.Navigable;
import com.auction.ui.util.SceneManager;
import com.auction.util.BackgroundBidWatcher;
import com.auction.util.NotificationStore;
import com.auction.util.RestClient;
import com.auction.util.UserBalanceWatcher;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.net.http.HttpResponse;
import java.text.NumberFormat;
import java.util.Locale;
import javafx.application.Platform;
import javafx.fxml.FXML;
import javafx.scene.control.Button;
import javafx.scene.control.Label;
import javafx.scene.layout.VBox;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * Controller cho mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh hГЎВ»вҖң sГҶВЎ cГғВЎ nhГғВўn (profile.fxml).
 *
 * <p>HiГЎВ»Ж’n thГЎВ»вҖ№ thГғВҙng tin tГғВ i khoГЎВәВЈn: username, role, sГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ° (BIDDER/SELLER). Cung cГЎВәВҘp Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»ВҒu hГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәng Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn
 * Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖўi mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u, nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn (BIDDER), Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng xuГЎВәВҘt.
 */
public class ProfileController implements Navigable {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ProfileController.class);
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER = new ObjectMapper();
  private static final NumberFormat VND = NumberFormat.getCurrencyInstance(Locale.of("vi", "VN"));

  @FXML private Label usernameLabel;
  @FXML private Label roleLabel;
  @FXML private Button depositButton;
  @FXML private VBox balanceBox;
  @FXML private Label profileBalanceLabel;

  @Override
  public void onNavigatedTo() {
    // LГЎВәВҜng nghe thГғВҙng bГғВЎo biГЎВәВҝn Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng sГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ° tГЎВ»В« UserBalanceWatcher
    UserBalanceWatcher.getInstance().setOnBalanceUpdate(this::onBalanceUpdated);
    SceneManager sm = SceneManager.getInstance();

    if (usernameLabel != null) {
      usernameLabel.setText(sm.getCurrentUsername() != null ? sm.getCurrentUsername() : "ГўвӮ¬вҖқ");
    }

    String role = sm.getCurrentRole();
    if (roleLabel != null) {
      roleLabel.setText(role != null ? role : "ГўвӮ¬вҖқ");
    }

    boolean isBidder = "BIDDER".equals(role);
    if (depositButton != null) {
      depositButton.setVisible(isBidder);
      depositButton.setManaged(isBidder);
    }

    boolean hasBalance = "BIDDER".equals(role) || "SELLER".equals(role);
    if (balanceBox != null) {
      balanceBox.setVisible(hasBalance);
      balanceBox.setManaged(hasBalance);
      if (profileBalanceLabel != null) {
        profileBalanceLabel.setText("Г„Вҗang tГЎВәВЈi...");
      }
    }
    if (hasBalance) {
      loadBalance();
    }
  }

  @FXML
  public void goToChangePassword() {
    SceneManager.getInstance().navigateTo("change-password.fxml");
  }

  @FXML
  public void goToDeposit() {
    SceneManager.getInstance().navigateTo("deposit.fxml");
  }

  @FXML
  public void handleLogout() {
    // DГЎВ»В«ng kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi WebSocket user trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc khi logout
    UserBalanceWatcher.getInstance().disconnect();
    BackgroundBidWatcher.getInstance().stopAll();
    SceneManager.getInstance().logout();
  }

  @FXML
  public void goBack() {
    SceneManager.getInstance().navigateBack("auction-list.fxml");
  }

  @Override
  public void onNavigatedFrom() {
    // HГЎВ»В§y listener Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ trГғВЎnh cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt UI khi khГғВҙng cГғВІn ГЎВ»Её mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh nГғВ y
    UserBalanceWatcher.getInstance().setOnBalanceUpdate(null);
  }

  /** NhГЎВәВӯn thГғВҙng bГғВЎo biГЎВәВҝn Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng sГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ° tГЎВ»В« UserBalanceWatcher ГўвӮ¬вҖқ gГЎВ»ВҚi trГғВӘn FX thread. */
  private void onBalanceUpdated(java.math.BigDecimal newBalance, boolean approved) {
    if (approved && newBalance != null) {
      if (profileBalanceLabel != null) {
        profileBalanceLabel.setText(VND.format(newBalance));
      }
      NotificationStore.getInstance()
          .add("ГўЕ“вҖҰ YГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc duyГЎВ»вҖЎt. SГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ° mГЎВ»вҖәi: " + VND.format(newBalance));
    } else {
      NotificationStore.getInstance().add("ГўВқЕ’ YГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn bГЎВ»вҖ№ tГЎВ»В« chГЎВ»вҖҳi.");
    }
  }

  private void loadBalance() {
    Thread.ofVirtual()
        .start(
            () -> {
              try {
                HttpResponse<String> response = RestClient.get("/api/users/me");
                if (response.statusCode() == 200) {
                  var node = MAPPER.readTree(response.body());
                  BigDecimal balance =
                      node.has("balance") && !node.get("balance").isNull()
                          ? node.get("balance").decimalValue()
                          : BigDecimal.ZERO;
                  Platform.runLater(
                      () -> {
                        if (profileBalanceLabel != null) {
                          profileBalanceLabel.setText(VND.format(balance));
                        }
                      });
                }
              } catch (Exception e) {
                LOGGER.error("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ load sГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ° profile", e);
              }
            });
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\ui\controller\RegisterController.java ==========
package com.auction.ui.controller;

import com.auction.ui.util.Navigable;
import com.auction.ui.util.SceneManager;
import com.auction.util.RestClient;
import com.auction.util.UserBalanceWatcher;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.net.http.HttpResponse;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import javafx.application.Platform;
import javafx.fxml.FXML;
import javafx.scene.control.Button;
import javafx.scene.control.ComboBox;
import javafx.scene.control.Label;
import javafx.scene.control.PasswordField;
import javafx.scene.control.TextField;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * Controller cho mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ tГғВ i khoГЎВәВЈn (register.fxml).
 *
 * <p><b>MГЎВ»ВҘc Г„вҖҳГғВӯch:</b> XГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ luГЎВ»вҖңng tГЎВәВЎo tГғВ i khoГЎВәВЈn mГЎВ»вҖәi: validate dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu phГғВӯa client, gГЎВ»ВҚi REST API
 * {@code POST /api/auth/register}, lГҶВ°u JWT token vГғВ o {@link SceneManager}, vГғВ  Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»ВҒu hГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәng Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn danh
 * sГғВЎch phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ sau khi Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ thГғВ nh cГғВҙng.
 *
 * <p><b>CГғВЎc phГҶВ°ГҶВЎng thГЎВ»В©c chГғВӯnh:</b>
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>{@link #handleRegister()} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ Validate vГғВ  gГЎВ»Вӯi request Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn server.
 *   <li>{@link #goToLogin()} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ Quay lГЎВәВЎi mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp.
 * </ul>
 *
 * <p><b>VГЎВ»вҖ№ trГғВӯ trong kiГЎВәВҝn trГғВәc:</b> RegisterController lГғВ  Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»Ж’m Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§u vГғВ o cГЎВ»В§a ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng mГЎВ»вҖәi. Sau khi
 * Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ thГғВ nh cГғВҙng, server trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ JWT token vГғВ  ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc tГЎВ»Вұ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp vГғВ o hГЎВ»вҖЎ thГЎВ»вҖҳng.
 */
public class RegisterController implements Navigable {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(RegisterController.class);
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER = new ObjectMapper();

  @FXML private TextField usernameField;
  @FXML private TextField emailField;
  @FXML private PasswordField passwordField;
  @FXML private PasswordField confirmPasswordField;
  @FXML private ComboBox<String> roleCombo;
  @FXML private Label errorLabel;
  @FXML private Button registerButton;

  // ========== NAVIGABLE LIFECYCLE ==========

  /** Reset form khi navigate Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ. */
  @Override
  public void onNavigatedTo() {
    clearForm();
  }

  // ========== FXML ACTIONS ==========

  /**
   * XГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ sГЎВ»Вұ kiГЎВ»вҖЎn nhГЎВәВҘn nГғВәt "Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ".
   *
   * <p>Validate phГғВӯa client: username khГғВҙng trГЎВ»вҖҳng, email hГЎВ»ВЈp lГЎВ»вҖЎ, mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u ГўвҖ°ВҘ 6 kГғВҪ tГЎВ»Вұ, hai mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u
   * khГЎВ»вҖәp nhau, vГғВ  role Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc chГЎВ»ВҚn. Sau Г„вҖҳГғВі gГЎВ»Вӯi request trГғВӘn luГЎВ»вҖңng nГЎВ»ВҒn, lГҶВ°u session nГЎВәВҝu thГғВ nh cГғВҙng.
   */
  @FXML
  public void handleRegister() {
    String username = usernameField.getText().trim();
    String email = emailField.getText().trim();
    String password = passwordField.getText();
    String confirmPassword = confirmPasswordField.getText();
    String role = roleCombo.getValue();

    // Validate phГғВӯa client
    if (username.isEmpty()) {
      showError("TГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp khГғВҙng Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ trГЎВ»вҖҳng.");
      return;
    }
    if (!email.matches("^[A-Za-z0-9+_.-]+@(.+)$")) {
      showError("Г„ВҗГЎВ»вҖ№nh dГЎВәВЎng email khГғВҙng hГЎВ»ВЈp lГЎВ»вҖЎ.");
      return;
    }
    if (password.length() < 6) {
      showError("MГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u phГЎВәВЈi cГғВі ГғВӯt nhГЎВәВҘt 6 kГғВҪ tГЎВ»Вұ.");
      return;
    }
    if (!password.equals(confirmPassword)) {
      showError("Hai mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u khГғВҙng khГЎВ»вҖәp nhau.");
      return;
    }
    if (role == null) {
      showError("Vui lГғВІng chГЎВ»ВҚn vai trГғВІ.");
      return;
    }

    registerButton.setDisable(true);
    hideError();

    // GГЎВ»ВҚi API trГғВӘn luГЎВ»вҖңng nГЎВ»ВҒn
    Thread.ofVirtual()
        .start(
            () -> {
              try {
                Map<String, String> body = new HashMap<>();
                body.put("username", username);
                body.put("email", email);
                body.put("password", password);
                body.put("role", role);

                HttpResponse<String> response = RestClient.post("/api/auth/register", body);

                if (response.statusCode() == 201) {
                  JsonNode json = MAPPER.readTree(response.body());
                  String token = json.get("token").asText();
                  String returnedRole = json.get("role").asText();
                  String uname = json.get("username").asText();
                  long userId = json.get("userId").asLong();

                  Platform.runLater(() -> onRegisterSuccess(token, returnedRole, uname, userId));
                } else {
                  JsonNode json = MAPPER.readTree(response.body());
                  String msg =
                      json.has("message")
                          ? json.get("message").asText()
                          : "Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ thГЎВәВҘt bГЎВәВЎi. TГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ Г„вҖҳГғВЈ tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi.";
                  Platform.runLater(
                      () -> {
                        showError(msg);
                        registerButton.setDisable(false);
                      });
                }
              } catch (Exception e) {
                LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi server khi Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ", e);
                Platform.runLater(
                    () -> {
                      showError("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn server. Vui lГғВІng thГЎВ»Вӯ lГЎВәВЎi.");
                      registerButton.setDisable(false);
                    });
              }
            });
  }

  /** Quay lГЎВәВЎi mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp. */
  @FXML
  public void goToLogin() {
    SceneManager.getInstance().navigateTo("login.fxml");
  }

  // ========== PRIVATE HELPERS ==========

  /** LГҶВ°u session vГғВ  Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»ВҒu hГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәng sau khi Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ thГғВ nh cГғВҙng. */
  private void onRegisterSuccess(String token, String role, String username, long userId) {
    SceneManager sm = SceneManager.getInstance();
    sm.setJwtToken(token);
    sm.setCurrentUsername(username);
    sm.setCurrentRole(role);
    sm.setCurrentUserId(userId);

    LOGGER.info("Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ thГғВ nh cГғВҙng: username={}, role={}", username, role);

    // KГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi kГғВӘnh WebSocket Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ nhГЎВәВӯn thГғВҙng bГғВЎo biГЎВәВҝn Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng sГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ° (giГЎВ»вҖҳng LoginController)
    if (!"ADMIN".equals(role)) {
      UserBalanceWatcher.getInstance().connect(userId, token);
    }

    sm.navigateTo("auction-list.fxml");
  }

  private void showError(String message) {
    errorLabel.setText(message);
    errorLabel.setVisible(true);
    errorLabel.setManaged(true);
  }

  private void hideError() {
    errorLabel.setVisible(false);
    errorLabel.setManaged(false);
  }

  private void clearForm() {
    if (usernameField != null) {
      usernameField.clear();
    }
    if (emailField != null) {
      emailField.clear();
    }
    if (passwordField != null) {
      passwordField.clear();
    }
    if (confirmPasswordField != null) {
      confirmPasswordField.clear();
    }
    if (roleCombo != null) {
      roleCombo.setValue(null);
    }
    hideError();
    if (registerButton != null) {
      registerButton.setDisable(false);
    }
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\ui\controller\WelcomeController.java ==========
package com.auction.ui.controller;

import com.auction.ui.util.SceneManager;
import javafx.fxml.FXML;

/**
 * Controller cho mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh chГғВ o mГЎВ»В«ng (welcome.fxml).
 *
 * <p><b>MГЎВ»ВҘc Г„вҖҳГғВӯch:</b> LГғВ  mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§u tiГғВӘn khi ГЎВ»В©ng dГЎВ»ВҘng khГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng. Cho phГғВ©p ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng chГЎВ»ВҚn vai trГғВІ
 * (ADMIN, BIDDER, SELLER) Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»ВҒu hГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәng Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp.
 *
 * <p><b>CГғВЎc phГҶВ°ГҶВЎng thГЎВ»В©c chГғВӯnh:</b>
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>{@link #goToLoginAsAdmin()} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ ChuyГЎВ»Ж’n sang login.fxml vГЎВ»вҖәi hint role ADMIN.
 *   <li>{@link #goToLoginAsBidder()} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ ChuyГЎВ»Ж’n sang login.fxml vГЎВ»вҖәi hint role BIDDER.
 *   <li>{@link #goToLoginAsSeller()} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ ChuyГЎВ»Ж’n sang login.fxml vГЎВ»вҖәi hint role SELLER.
 * </ul>
 *
 * <p><b>VГЎВ»вҖ№ trГғВӯ trong kiГЎВәВҝn trГғВәc:</b> WelcomeController lГғВ  Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»Ж’m khГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§u cГЎВ»В§a luГЎВ»вҖңng Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»ВҒu hГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәng client.
 * Sau khi chГЎВ»ВҚn role, ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc chuyГЎВ»Ж’n sang LoginController Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp.
 */
public class WelcomeController {

  /** XГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ nГғВәt ADMIN ГўвӮ¬вҖқ chuyГЎВ»Ж’n sang mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp, truyГЎВ»ВҒn hint "ADMIN". */
  @FXML
  public void goToLoginAsAdmin() {
    SceneManager.getInstance().navigateTo("login.fxml", "ADMIN");
  }

  /** XГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ nГғВәt BIDDER ГўвӮ¬вҖқ chuyГЎВ»Ж’n sang mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp, truyГЎВ»ВҒn hint "BIDDER". */
  @FXML
  public void goToLoginAsBidder() {
    SceneManager.getInstance().navigateTo("login.fxml", "BIDDER");
  }

  /** XГЎВ»Вӯ lГғВҪ nГғВәt SELLER ГўвӮ¬вҖқ chuyГЎВ»Ж’n sang mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp, truyГЎВ»ВҒn hint "SELLER". */
  @FXML
  public void goToLoginAsSeller() {
    SceneManager.getInstance().navigateTo("login.fxml", "SELLER");
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\ui\util\Navigable.java ==========
package com.auction.ui.util;

/**
 * Interface lifecycle cho cГғВЎc FXML Controller. SceneManager gГЎВ»ВҚi tГЎВ»Вұ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng khi chuyГЎВ»Ж’n mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh.
 *
 * <p>DГғВ№ng default method ГўвҖ вҖҷ controller chГЎВ»вҖ° override method nГғВ o cГЎВәВ§n, khГғВҙng bГЎВәВҜt buГЎВ»в„ўc implement cГЎВәВЈ 3.
 */
public interface Navigable {

  /**
   * GГЎВ»ВҚi mГЎВ»вҖ”i khi navigate TГЎВ»ЕЎI mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh nГғВ y. DГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ refresh data, cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt UI. VГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ:
   * AuctionListController ГўвҖ вҖҷ gГЎВ»ВҚi lГЎВәВЎi API lГЎВәВҘy danh sГғВЎch mГЎВ»вҖәi.
   */
  default void onNavigatedTo() {}

  /**
   * NhГЎВәВӯn data tГЎВ»В« mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc truyГЎВ»ВҒn sang. VГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ: auction-list truyГЎВ»ВҒn auctionId ГўвҖ вҖҷ auction-detail.
   *
   * @param data dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu bГЎВәВҘt kГЎВ»Ві, controller tГЎВ»Вұ cast vГЎВ»ВҒ Г„вҖҳГғВәng kiГЎВ»Ж’u
   */
  default void onDataReceived(Object data) {}

  /**
   * GГЎВ»ВҚi khi RГЎВ»Е“I KHГЎВ»ЕҪI mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh (navigate Г„вҖҳi chГЎВ»вҖ” khГғВЎc). DГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ cleanup: Г„вҖҳГғВіng WebSocket, hГЎВ»В§y Timer,
   * dГЎВ»В«ng animation...
   */
  default void onNavigatedFrom() {}
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\ui\util\SceneManager.java ==========
package com.auction.ui.util;

import java.io.IOException;
import java.net.URL;
import java.util.ArrayDeque;
import java.util.Deque;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import javafx.beans.value.ChangeListener;
import javafx.fxml.FXMLLoader;
import javafx.geometry.Insets;
import javafx.geometry.Pos;
import javafx.scene.Parent;
import javafx.scene.Scene;
import javafx.scene.control.Label;
import javafx.scene.layout.StackPane;
import javafx.stage.Stage;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * Singleton quГЎВәВЈn lГғВҪ toГғВ n bГЎВ»в„ў navigation trong ГЎВ»В©ng dГЎВ»ВҘng JavaFX.
 *
 * <p>KiГЎВәВҝn trГғВәc: Single Scene + StackPane swap (giГЎВ»вҖҳng SPA trong web). - 1 Scene duy nhГЎВәВҘt, khГғВҙng bao
 * giГЎВ»Вқ tГЎВәВЎo/hГЎВ»В§y Scene - 1 StackPane root, chuyГЎВ»Ж’n mГғВ n = swap children - FXML lazy load lГЎВәВ§n Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§u, cache
 * vГ„В©nh viГЎВ»вҖҰn trong HashMap - Controller cГ…В©ng cache ГўвҖ вҖҷ giГЎВ»ВҜ state khi quay lГЎВәВЎi - CSS load 1 lГЎВәВ§n gГЎВәВҜn vГғВ o
 * Scene ГўвҖ вҖҷ tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ FXML Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҒu cГғВі theme
 *
 * <p>SГЎВ»Вӯ dГЎВ»ВҘng: SceneManager.getInstance().navigateTo("auction-list.fxml");
 * SceneManager.getInstance().navigateTo("auction-detail.fxml", auctionId);
 */
public class SceneManager {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(SceneManager.class);

  // ========== SINGLETON ==========
  private static SceneManager instance;

  public static SceneManager getInstance() {
    if (instance == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "SceneManager chГҶВ°a Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc khГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo! GГЎВ»ВҚi init() trong ClientApp.start() trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc.");
    }
    return instance;
  }

  /**
   * KhГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo SceneManager ГўвӮ¬вҖқ chГЎВ»вҖ° gГЎВ»ВҚi 1 lГЎВәВ§n duy nhГЎВәВҘt trong ClientApp.start().
   *
   * @param primaryStage Stage chГғВӯnh tГЎВ»В« JavaFX Application
   * @param width chiГЎВ»ВҒu rГЎВ»в„ўng cГЎВ»Вӯa sГЎВ»вҖў
   * @param height chiГЎВ»ВҒu cao cГЎВ»Вӯa sГЎВ»вҖў
   * @return instance Г„вҖҳГғВЈ khГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo
   */
  public static SceneManager init(Stage primaryStage, double width, double height) {
    if (instance != null) {
      LOGGER.warn("SceneManager Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc khГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc Г„вҖҳГғВі, trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ instance cГ…В©.");
      return instance;
    }
    instance = new SceneManager(primaryStage, width, height);
    LOGGER.info("SceneManager khГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo thГғВ nh cГғВҙng ГўвӮ¬вҖқ {}x{}", width, height);
    return instance;
  }

  // ========== CACHE ==========

  /** Cache view (Parent) Г„вҖҳГғВЈ load ГўвӮ¬вҖқ key lГғВ  tГғВӘn FXML, value lГғВ  root node */
  private final Map<String, Parent> viewCache = new HashMap<>();

  /** Cache controller tГҶВ°ГҶВЎng ГЎВ»В©ng ГўвӮ¬вҖқ key lГғВ  tГғВӘn FXML, value lГғВ  controller object */
  private final Map<String, Object> controllerCache = new HashMap<>();

  // ========== CORE COMPONENTS ==========

  private final Stage primaryStage;
  private final Scene scene;
  private final StackPane rootContainer;

  /** TГғВӘn FXML Г„вҖҳang hiГЎВ»Ж’n thГЎВ»вҖ№ hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi ГўвӮ¬вҖқ dГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ gГЎВ»ВҚi onNavigatedFrom() */
  private String currentFxml;

  /** Badge thГғВҙng bГғВЎo toГғВ n cГЎВ»ВҘc ГўвӮ¬вҖқ hiГЎВ»Ж’n thГЎВ»вҖ№ trГғВӘn mГЎВ»ВҚi mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh trГЎВ»В« auction-list (cГғВі bell riГғВӘng). */
  private Label globalBadgeLabel;

  /** Stack lГЎВ»вҖ№ch sГЎВ»Вӯ Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»ВҒu hГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәng ГўвӮ¬вҖқ dГғВ№ng cho navigateBack() */
  private final Deque<String> backStack = new ArrayDeque<>();

  // ========== SESSION STATE ==========

  private String jwtToken;
  private String currentUsername;
  private String currentRole;
  private Long currentUserId;

  // ========== CONSTRUCTOR (private ГўвӮ¬вҖқ Singleton) ==========

  private SceneManager(Stage primaryStage, double width, double height) {
    this.primaryStage = primaryStage;
    this.rootContainer = new StackPane();
    this.scene = new Scene(rootContainer, width, height);

    // Load CSS theme 1 lГЎВәВ§n duy nhГЎВәВҘt ГўвӮ¬вҖқ ГғВЎp dГЎВ»ВҘng cho tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ FXML
    URL cssUrl = getClass().getResource("/css/style.css");
    if (cssUrl != null) {
      scene.getStylesheets().add(cssUrl.toExternalForm());
    } else {
      // FIX: KhГғВҙng crash nГЎВәВҝu thiГЎВәВҝu CSS, chГЎВ»вҖ° log warning
      LOGGER.warn("KhГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy /css/style.css ГўвӮ¬вҖқ ГЎВ»В©ng dГЎВ»ВҘng chГЎВәВЎy khГғВҙng cГғВі theme.");
    }

    primaryStage.setScene(scene);
    setupGlobalNotificationBadge();
  }

  // ========== GLOBAL NOTIFICATION BADGE ==========

  /**
   * KhГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo badge thГғВҙng bГғВЎo toГғВ n cГЎВ»ВҘc, Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t gГғВіc trГғВӘn-phГЎВәВЈi cГЎВ»В§a rootContainer.
   *
   * <p>Badge nГғВ y luГғВҙn active ГЎВ»Её mГЎВ»ВҚi mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh. RiГғВӘng "auction-list.fxml" Г„вҖҳГғВЈ cГғВі bell button riГғВӘng nГғВӘn
   * badge toГғВ n cГЎВ»ВҘc sГЎВәВҪ tГЎВ»Вұ ГЎВәВ©n khi Г„вҖҳang ГЎВ»Её mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh Г„вҖҳГғВі.
   */
  private void setupGlobalNotificationBadge() {
    globalBadgeLabel = new Label();
    globalBadgeLabel.getStyleClass().add("notification-badge");
    StackPane.setAlignment(globalBadgeLabel, Pos.TOP_RIGHT);
    StackPane.setMargin(globalBadgeLabel, new Insets(10, 10, 0, 0));
    globalBadgeLabel.setVisible(false);
    globalBadgeLabel.setManaged(false);
    rootContainer.getChildren().add(globalBadgeLabel);

    ChangeListener<Number> listener = (obs, oldVal, newVal) -> updateGlobalBadge(newVal.intValue());
    com.auction.util.NotificationStore.getInstance().unreadCountProperty().addListener(listener);
  }

  /** CГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi badge toГғВ n cГЎВ»ВҘc. ГЎВәВЁn khi Г„вҖҳang ГЎВ»Её auction-list (mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh Г„вҖҳГғВі cГғВі bell riГғВӘng). */
  private void updateGlobalBadge(int count) {
    if ("auction-list.fxml".equals(currentFxml)) {
      globalBadgeLabel.setVisible(false);
      globalBadgeLabel.setManaged(false);
      return;
    }
    if (count > 0) {
      globalBadgeLabel.setText(count > 99 ? "99+" : String.valueOf(count));
      globalBadgeLabel.setVisible(true);
      globalBadgeLabel.setManaged(true);
    } else {
      globalBadgeLabel.setVisible(false);
      globalBadgeLabel.setManaged(false);
    }
  }

  // ========== NAVIGATION ГўвӮ¬вҖқ CORE ==========

  /**
   * ChuyГЎВ»Ж’n sang mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh mГЎВ»вҖәi ГўвӮ¬вҖқ ghi lГЎВәВЎi mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi vГғВ o backStack Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ quay lГЎВәВЎi.
   *
   * @param fxmlName tГғВӘn file FXML Г„вҖҳГғВӯch (vГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ: "auction-list.fxml")
   */
  public void navigateTo(String fxmlName) {
    if (currentFxml != null) {
      backStack.push(currentFxml);
    }
    performNavigate(fxmlName, null, false);
  }

  /**
   * ChuyГЎВ»Ж’n mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh + truyГЎВ»ВҒn data cho controller Г„вҖҳГғВӯch. onDataReceived() Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГЎВ»ВҚi TRГҶВҜГЎВ»ЕЎC
   * onNavigatedTo() Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ controller cГғВі Г„вҖҳГЎВ»В§ data.
   *
   * @param fxmlName tГғВӘn file FXML Г„вҖҳГғВӯch
   * @param data dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu truyГЎВ»ВҒn sang
   */
  public void navigateTo(String fxmlName, Object data) {
    if (currentFxml != null) {
      backStack.push(currentFxml);
    }
    performNavigate(fxmlName, data, true);
  }

  /**
   * Quay lГЎВәВЎi mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc trong backStack. NГЎВәВҝu stack rГЎВ»вҖ”ng, dГғВ№ng {@code defaultFxml}. KHГғвҖқNG ghi
   * mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi vГғВ o stack (khГғВҙng tГЎВәВЎo vГғВІng lГЎВәВ·p).
   */
  public void navigateBack(String defaultFxml) {
    String target = backStack.isEmpty() ? defaultFxml : backStack.pop();
    performNavigate(target, null, false);
  }

  /**
   * ThГЎВ»Вұc hiГЎВ»вҖЎn Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»ВҒu hГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәng ГўвӮ¬вҖқ dГғВ№ng chung cho navigateTo, navigateBack, vГғВ  logout. GГЎВ»ВҚi
   * onNavigatedFrom() cГЎВ»В§a controller cГ…В© vГғВ  onNavigatedTo() cГЎВ»В§a controller mГЎВ»вҖәi.
   */
  private void performNavigate(String fxmlName, Object data, boolean hasData) {
    notifyNavigatedFrom();

    Parent view;
    try {
      view = viewCache.get(fxmlName);
      if (view == null) {
        view = loadFxml(fxmlName);
      }
    } catch (Exception e) {
      LOGGER.error("performNavigate thГЎВәВҘt bГЎВәВЎi khi load '{}': {}", fxmlName, e.getMessage(), e);
      showErrorScreen("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ load mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh: " + fxmlName + "\n" + e.getMessage());
      return;
    }

    rootContainer.getChildren().setAll(view);
    currentFxml = fxmlName;

    Object controller = controllerCache.get(fxmlName);
    if (controller instanceof Navigable nav) {
      if (hasData) {
        try {
          nav.onDataReceived(data);
        } catch (Exception e) {
          LOGGER.error("onDataReceived() lГЎВ»вҖ”i ГЎВ»Её '{}': {}", fxmlName, e.getMessage(), e);
        }
      }
      try {
        nav.onNavigatedTo();
      } catch (Exception e) {
        LOGGER.error("onNavigatedTo() lГЎВ»вҖ”i ГЎВ»Её '{}': {}", fxmlName, e.getMessage(), e);
      }
    }

    LOGGER.debug("Navigated to: {}", fxmlName);

    // Г„ВҗГЎВ»вҖңng bГЎВ»в„ў global badge sau mГЎВ»вҖ”i lГЎВәВ§n chuyГЎВ»Ж’n mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh
    updateGlobalBadge(com.auction.util.NotificationStore.getInstance().getUnreadCount());
  }

  // ========== FXML LOADING ==========

  /**
   * Load FXML tГЎВ»В« resources, cache cГЎВәВЈ view lГЎВәВ«n controller. ChГЎВ»вҖ° gГЎВ»ВҚi 1 lГЎВәВ§n cho mГЎВ»вҖ”i FXML ГўвӮ¬вҖқ tГЎВ»В« lГЎВәВ§n thГЎВ»В© 2
   * trГЎВ»Её Г„вҖҳi lГЎВәВҘy tГЎВ»В« cache.
   *
   * <p>FIX: kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra URL null trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc khi load Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ bГғВЎo lГЎВ»вҖ”i rГғВө rГғВ ng thay vГғВ¬ NullPointerException khГғВі
   * debug.
   */
  private Parent loadFxml(String fxmlName) {
    // FIX: KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra URL tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc ГўвӮ¬вҖқ nГЎВәВҝu null thГғВ¬ path sai
    URL url = getClass().getResource("/ui/fxml/" + fxmlName);
    if (url == null) {
      String msg =
          "KhГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy FXML tГЎВәВЎi: /ui/fxml/"
              + fxmlName
              + " ГўвӮ¬вҖқ KiГЎВ»Ж’m tra file cГғВі nГЎВәВұm Г„вҖҳГғВәng trong src/main/resources/ui/fxml/ khГғВҙng.";
      LOGGER.error(msg);
      throw new RuntimeException(msg);
    }

    try {
      FXMLLoader loader = new FXMLLoader(url);
      Parent view = loader.load();

      viewCache.put(fxmlName, view);
      controllerCache.put(fxmlName, loader.getController());

      LOGGER.info("Lazy loaded FXML: {}", fxmlName);
      return view;
    } catch (IOException e) {
      LOGGER.error("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ load FXML '{}': {}", fxmlName, e.getMessage(), e);
      throw new RuntimeException("Load FXML thГЎВәВҘt bГЎВәВЎi: " + fxmlName, e);
    }
  }

  // ========== LIFECYCLE HELPERS ==========

  private void notifyNavigatedFrom() {
    if (currentFxml != null) {
      Object controller = controllerCache.get(currentFxml);
      if (controller instanceof Navigable nav) {
        try {
          nav.onNavigatedFrom();
        } catch (Exception e) {
          LOGGER.error("onNavigatedFrom() lГЎВ»вҖ”i ГЎВ»Её '{}': {}", currentFxml, e.getMessage(), e);
        }
      }
    }
  }

  /** HiГЎВ»Ж’n thГЎВ»вҖ№ mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh lГЎВ»вҖ”i tГЎВәВЎm thГЎВ»Вқi thay vГғВ¬ crash im lГЎВәВ·ng. GiГғВәp debug khi FXML khГғВҙng load Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc. */
  private void showErrorScreen(String message) {
    Label errorLabel = new Label("ГўЕЎВ  LГЎВ»вҖ”i Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»ВҒu hГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәng:\n" + message);
    errorLabel.setStyle("-fx-text-fill: red; -fx-font-size: 14px; -fx-padding: 20;");
    errorLabel.setWrapText(true);
    rootContainer.getChildren().setAll(errorLabel);
  }

  // ========== SESSION MANAGEMENT ==========

  public void logout() {
    jwtToken = null;
    currentUsername = null;
    currentRole = null;
    currentUserId = null;
    backStack.clear();
    com.auction.util.BackgroundBidWatcher.getInstance().stopAll();
    com.auction.util.NotificationStore.getInstance().clear();
    globalBadgeLabel.setVisible(false);
    globalBadgeLabel.setManaged(false);

    // XГғВіa cache cГғВЎc view cГЎВәВ§n auth, giГЎВ»ВҜ lГЎВәВЎi welcome + login + register
    viewCache
        .keySet()
        .removeIf(
            k ->
                !k.equals("welcome.fxml") && !k.equals("login.fxml") && !k.equals("register.fxml"));
    controllerCache
        .keySet()
        .removeIf(
            k ->
                !k.equals("welcome.fxml") && !k.equals("login.fxml") && !k.equals("register.fxml"));

    // DГғВ№ng performNavigate trГЎВ»Вұc tiГЎВәВҝp ГўвӮ¬вҖқ khГғВҙng push vГғВ o backStack sau khi Г„вҖҳГғВЈ clear
    performNavigate("welcome.fxml", null, false);
  }

  /**
   * XГғВіa cache cГЎВ»В§a 1 mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh cГЎВ»ВҘ thГЎВ»Ж’. DГғВ№ng khi cГЎВәВ§n force reload FXML (vГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ: sau khi tГЎВәВЎo item mГЎВ»вҖәi
   * cГЎВәВ§n reload create-auction).
   */
  public void invalidateCache(String fxmlName) {
    viewCache.remove(fxmlName);
    controllerCache.remove(fxmlName);
    LOGGER.debug("Г„ВҗГғВЈ xГғВіa cache: {}", fxmlName);
  }

  // ========== GETTERS / SETTERS ГўвӮ¬вҖқ SESSION STATE ==========

  public String getJwtToken() {
    return jwtToken;
  }

  public void setJwtToken(String jwtToken) {
    this.jwtToken = jwtToken;
  }

  public String getCurrentUsername() {
    return currentUsername;
  }

  public void setCurrentUsername(String currentUsername) {
    this.currentUsername = currentUsername;
  }

  public String getCurrentRole() {
    return currentRole;
  }

  public void setCurrentRole(String currentRole) {
    this.currentRole = currentRole;
  }

  public Long getCurrentUserId() {
    return currentUserId;
  }

  public void setCurrentUserId(Long currentUserId) {
    this.currentUserId = currentUserId;
  }

  public Stage getPrimaryStage() {
    return primaryStage;
  }

  @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
