  public <T> T getController(String fxmlName) {
    return (T) controllerCache.get(fxmlName);
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\util\BackgroundBidWatcher.java ==========
package com.auction.util;

import com.auction.dto.BidUpdateMessage;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.JavaTimeModule;
import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
import javafx.application.Platform;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * Singleton theo dГғВөi bid trong nГЎВ»ВҒn cho cГғВЎc phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ mГғВ  user Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t giГғВЎ nhГҶВ°ng Г„вҖҳГғВЈ rГЎВ»Вқi mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh
 * chi tiГЎВәВҝt.
 *
 * <p>Khi user rГЎВ»Вқi {@code AuctionDetailController} mГғВ  vГЎВәВ«n cГғВІn bid, controller gГЎВ»ВҚi {@link
 * #watch(Long, String, String, Long)} Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ. BackgroundBidWatcher mГЎВ»Её kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi WebSocket riГғВӘng
 * cho phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГғВі vГғВ  Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ©y thГғВҙng bГғВЎo qua {@link NotificationStore} khi cГғВі cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt.
 *
 * <p>Khi user quay lГЎВәВЎi mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh chi tiГЎВәВҝt cГЎВ»В§a phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГғВі, {@link #stopWatching(Long)} Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГЎВ»ВҚi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’
 * trГғВЎnh nhГЎВәВӯn event trГғВ№ng vГЎВ»вҖәi kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi WebSocket cГЎВ»В§a controller. {@link #stopAll()} Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГЎВ»ВҚi khi Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng
 * xuГЎВәВҘt.
 */
public class BackgroundBidWatcher {

  private static final BackgroundBidWatcher INSTANCE = new BackgroundBidWatcher();
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(BackgroundBidWatcher.class);
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER =
      new ObjectMapper().registerModule(new JavaTimeModule());

  /** Map auctionId ГўвҖ вҖҷ WebSocketClient Г„вҖҳang watch. */
  private final Map<Long, WebSocketClient> watchers = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();

  private BackgroundBidWatcher() {}

  public static BackgroundBidWatcher getInstance() {
    return INSTANCE;
  }

  /**
   * BГЎВәВҜt Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§u theo dГғВөi mГЎВ»в„ўt phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ trong nГЎВ»ВҒn.
   *
   * <p>NГЎВәВҝu Г„вҖҳГғВЈ cГғВі watcher cho {@code auctionId}, phГҶВ°ГҶВЎng thГЎВ»В©c nГғВ y khГғВҙng-op (trГғВЎnh kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi Г„вҖҳГғВҙi).
   *
   * @param auctionId ID phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ cГЎВәВ§n theo dГғВөi
   * @param token JWT token cГЎВ»В§a user
   * @param itemName TГғВӘn sГЎВәВЈn phГЎВәВ©m (dГғВ№ng cho nГЎВ»в„ўi dung thГғВҙng bГғВЎo)
   * @param userId ID user hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi
   */
  public void watch(Long auctionId, String token, String itemName, Long userId) {
    if (watchers.containsKey(auctionId)) {
      LOGGER.debug("BackgroundBidWatcher: Г„вҖҳГғВЈ watch auctionId={}, bГЎВ»ВҸ qua.", auctionId);
      return;
    }

    WebSocketClient client = new WebSocketClient();
    watchers.put(auctionId, client);

    String name = itemName != null ? itemName : "PhiГғВӘn #" + auctionId;

    client.connect(
        auctionId,
        token,
        json -> {
          try {
            BidUpdateMessage msg = MAPPER.readValue(json, BidUpdateMessage.class);
            String type = msg.getType();
            if (type == null) {
              return;
            }

            switch (type) {
              case BidUpdateMessage.TYPE_BID_UPDATE -> {
                Long leaderId = msg.getLeadingBidderId();
                BigDecimal price = msg.getCurrentPrice();
                if (leaderId != null && !leaderId.equals(userId)) {
                  // NgГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi khГғВЎc vГЎВ»В«a vГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈt giГғВЎ cГЎВ»В§a user
                  String notification = "ГўЕЎВ ГҜВёВҸ BГЎВәВЎn bГЎВ»вҖ№ vГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈt giГғВЎ tГЎВәВЎi " + name + ": " + price;
                  Platform.runLater(() -> NotificationStore.getInstance().add(notification));
                }
              }
              case BidUpdateMessage.TYPE_AUTO_BID_TRIGGERED -> {
                Long leaderId = msg.getLeadingBidderId();
                BigDecimal price = msg.getCurrentPrice();
                if (leaderId != null && leaderId.equals(userId)) {
                  // Auto-bid Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t thГғВ nh cГғВҙng cho chГғВӯnh user nГғВ y
                  String notification = "Г°ЕёВӨвҖ“ Auto-bid Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t " + price + " cho bГЎВәВЎn tГЎВәВЎi " + name;
                  Platform.runLater(() -> NotificationStore.getInstance().add(notification));
                }
              }
              case BidUpdateMessage.TYPE_AUCTION_ENDED -> {
                String winner = msg.getLeadingBidderUsername();
                String notification =
                    "Г°ЕёВҸВҒ PhiГғВӘn kГЎВәВҝt thГғВәc: "
                        + name
                        + (winner != null ? " ГўвӮ¬вҖқ NgГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi thГЎВәВҜng: " + winner : "");
                Platform.runLater(
                    () -> {
                      NotificationStore.getInstance().add(notification);
                      stopWatching(auctionId);
                    });
              }
              default -> {
                // TYPE_TIME_EXTENDED vГғВ  cГғВЎc type khГғВЎc: bГЎВ»ВҸ qua
              }
            }
          } catch (Exception e) {
            LOGGER.debug(
                "BackgroundBidWatcher parse error (auction={}): {}", auctionId, e.getMessage());
          }
        });

    LOGGER.info("BackgroundBidWatcher: bГЎВәВҜt Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§u watch auctionId={}", auctionId);
  }

  /**
   * DГЎВ»В«ng theo dГғВөi mГЎВ»в„ўt phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ cГЎВ»ВҘ thГЎВ»Ж’.
   *
   * <p>ThГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc gГЎВ»ВҚi khi user quay lГЎВәВЎi mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh chi tiГЎВәВҝt cГЎВ»В§a phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГғВі.
   *
   * @param auctionId ID phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ cГЎВәВ§n dГЎВ»В«ng
   */
  public void stopWatching(Long auctionId) {
    WebSocketClient client = watchers.remove(auctionId);
    if (client != null) {
      client.disconnect();
      LOGGER.info("BackgroundBidWatcher: dГЎВ»В«ng watch auctionId={}", auctionId);
    }
  }

  /** DГЎВ»В«ng tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ watcher ГўвӮ¬вҖқ gГЎВ»ВҚi khi ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng xuГЎВәВҘt. */
  public void stopAll() {
    watchers.forEach(
        (id, client) -> {
          client.disconnect();
          LOGGER.info("BackgroundBidWatcher: dГЎВ»В«ng watch auctionId={} (stopAll)", id);
        });
    watchers.clear();
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\util\NotificationStore.java ==========
package com.auction.util;

import javafx.beans.property.ReadOnlyIntegerProperty;
import javafx.beans.property.SimpleIntegerProperty;
import javafx.collections.FXCollections;
import javafx.collections.ObservableList;

/**
 * Singleton lГҶВ°u trГЎВ»ВҜ thГғВҙng bГғВЎo bid trong phiГғВӘn ГўвӮ¬вҖқ chГЎВ»вҖ° thГғВӘm tГЎВ»В« FX thread. SГЎВ»вҖҳ lГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈng thГғВҙng bГғВЎo chГҶВ°a Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҚc
 * Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc reset khi ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng mГЎВ»Её panel.
 */
public class NotificationStore {

  private static final NotificationStore INSTANCE = new NotificationStore();

  private final ObservableList<String> notifications = FXCollections.observableArrayList();
  private final SimpleIntegerProperty unreadCount = new SimpleIntegerProperty(0);

  private NotificationStore() {}

  public static NotificationStore getInstance() {
    return INSTANCE;
  }

  public void add(String notification) {
    notifications.add(0, notification);
    unreadCount.set(unreadCount.get() + 1);
  }

  public int getUnreadCount() {
    return unreadCount.get();
  }

  public ReadOnlyIntegerProperty unreadCountProperty() {
    return unreadCount;
  }

  public void markAllRead() {
    unreadCount.set(0);
  }

  public ObservableList<String> getNotifications() {
    return notifications;
  }

  public void clear() {
    notifications.clear();
    unreadCount.set(0);
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\util\RestClient.java ==========
package com.auction.util;

import com.auction.ui.util.SceneManager;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.SerializationFeature;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.JavaTimeModule;
import java.net.URI;
import java.net.http.HttpClient;
import java.net.http.HttpRequest;
import java.net.http.HttpResponse;
import java.time.Duration;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * Utility client HTTP dГғВ№ng cho client JavaFX giao tiГЎВәВҝp vГЎВ»вҖәi server Javalin.
 *
 * <p><b>MГЎВ»ВҘc Г„вҖҳГғВӯch:</b> Cung cГЎВәВҘp cГғВЎc phГҶВ°ГҶВЎng thГЎВ»В©c gГЎВ»Вӯi HTTP request (GET, POST, PUT, DELETE) Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn REST
 * API cГЎВ»В§a server, tГЎВ»Вұ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng gГЎВәВҜn JWT token vГғВ o header {@code Authorization: Bearer <token>} nГЎВәВҝu ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi
 * dГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp (lГЎВәВҘy tГЎВ»В« {@link SceneManager}).
 *
 * <p><b>CГғВЎc phГҶВ°ГҶВЎng thГЎВ»В©c chГғВӯnh:</b>
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>{@link #get(String)} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ GГЎВ»Вӯi GET request, trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ JSON string.
 *   <li>{@link #post(String, Object)} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ GГЎВ»Вӯi POST request vГЎВ»вҖәi body JSON.
 *   <li>{@link #put(String, Object)} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ GГЎВ»Вӯi PUT request vГЎВ»вҖәi body JSON.
 *   <li>{@link #delete(String)} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ GГЎВ»Вӯi DELETE request.
 * </ul>
 *
 * <p><b>VГЎВ»вҖ№ trГғВӯ trong kiГЎВәВҝn trГғВәc:</b> TГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ UI Controller Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҒu gГЎВ»ВҚi RestClient Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ tГҶВ°ГҶВЎng tГғВЎc vГЎВ»вҖәi
 * server. RestClient lГғВ  cГЎВәВ§u nГЎВ»вҖҳi giГЎВ»ВҜa tГЎВәВ§ng UI (JavaFX) vГғВ  tГЎВәВ§ng API (Javalin REST).
 *
 * <p><b>VГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ sГЎВ»Вӯ dГЎВ»ВҘng:</b>
 *
 * <pre>
 *   HttpResponse&lt;String&gt; resp = RestClient.get("/api/auctions");
 *   if (resp.statusCode() == 200) {
 *     List&lt;AuctionResponse&gt; list = RestClient.parseList(resp.body(), AuctionResponse.class);
 *   }
 * </pre>
 */
public class RestClient {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(RestClient.class);

  /** URL gГЎВ»вҖҳc cГЎВ»В§a server ГўвӮ¬вҖқ khГЎВ»вҖәp vГЎВ»вҖәi SERVER_PORT trong App.java */
  private static final String BASE_URL = "http://localhost:8080";

  private static final HttpClient HTTP_CLIENT =
      HttpClient.newBuilder().connectTimeout(Duration.ofSeconds(5)).build();

  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER =
      new ObjectMapper()
          .registerModule(new JavaTimeModule())
          .disable(SerializationFeature.WRITE_DATES_AS_TIMESTAMPS);

  private RestClient() {}

  // ========== PUBLIC API ==========

  /**
   * GГЎВ»Вӯi GET request Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn {@code BASE_URL + path}.
   *
   * @param path Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng dГЎВәВ«n API (vГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ: "/api/auctions")
   * @return HttpResponse chГЎВ»В©a body JSON dГЎВәВЎng String
   * @throws RuntimeException nГЎВәВҝu gГЎВ»Вӯi request thГЎВәВҘt bГЎВәВЎi
   */
  public static HttpResponse<String> get(String path) {
    HttpRequest request = buildRequest(path).GET().build();
    return send(request);
  }

  /**
   * GГЎВ»Вӯi POST request vГЎВ»вҖәi body JSON serialize tГЎВ»В« {@code body}.
   *
   * @param path Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng dГЎВәВ«n API
   * @param body object sГЎВәВҪ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc serialize thГғВ nh JSON
   * @return HttpResponse chГЎВ»В©a body JSON
   */
  public static HttpResponse<String> post(String path, Object body) {
    HttpRequest request = buildRequest(path).POST(toBody(body)).build();
    return send(request);
  }

  /**
   * GГЎВ»Вӯi PUT request vГЎВ»вҖәi body JSON serialize tГЎВ»В« {@code body}.
   *
   * @param path Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng dГЎВәВ«n API
   * @param body object sГЎВәВҪ Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc serialize thГғВ nh JSON
   * @return HttpResponse chГЎВ»В©a body JSON
   */
  public static HttpResponse<String> put(String path, Object body) {
    HttpRequest request = buildRequest(path).PUT(toBody(body)).build();
    return send(request);
  }

  /**
   * GГЎВ»Вӯi DELETE request.
   *
   * @param path Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng dГЎВәВ«n API
   * @return HttpResponse chГЎВ»В©a body JSON
   */
  public static HttpResponse<String> delete(String path) {
    HttpRequest request = buildRequest(path).DELETE().build();
    return send(request);
  }

  /**
   * Parse JSON string thГғВ nh object cГЎВ»В§a kiГЎВ»Ж’u {@code clazz}.
   *
   * @param json JSON string cГЎВәВ§n parse
   * @param clazz kiГЎВ»Ж’u Г„вҖҳГғВӯch
   * @return object Г„вҖҳГғВЈ parse
   */
  public static <T> T parse(String json, Class<T> clazz) {
    try {
      return MAPPER.readValue(json, clazz);
    } catch (Exception e) {
      throw new RuntimeException("LГЎВ»вҖ”i parse JSON: " + e.getMessage(), e);
    }
  }

  /**
   * Parse JSON string thГғВ nh List cГЎВ»В§a kiГЎВ»Ж’u {@code clazz}.
   *
   * @param json JSON array string
   * @param clazz kiГЎВ»Ж’u phГЎВәВ§n tГЎВ»Вӯ trong list
   * @return List Г„вҖҳГғВЈ parse
   */
  public static <T> java.util.List<T> parseList(String json, Class<T> clazz) {
    try {
      var type = MAPPER.getTypeFactory().constructCollectionType(java.util.List.class, clazz);
      return MAPPER.readValue(json, type);
    } catch (Exception e) {
      throw new RuntimeException("LГЎВ»вҖ”i parse JSON list: " + e.getMessage(), e);
    }
  }

  // ========== PRIVATE HELPERS ==========

  /**
   * TГЎВәВЎo HttpRequest.Builder vГЎВ»вҖәi URI Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§y Г„вҖҳГЎВ»В§, Content-Type JSON, vГғВ  Authorization header nГЎВәВҝu Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng
   * nhГЎВәВӯp.
   */
  private static HttpRequest.Builder buildRequest(String path) {
    HttpRequest.Builder builder =
        HttpRequest.newBuilder()
            .uri(URI.create(BASE_URL + path))
            .header("Content-Type", "application/json")
            .timeout(Duration.ofSeconds(10));

    // TГЎВ»Вұ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng gГЎВәВҜn JWT token nГЎВәВҝu Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp
    try {
      String token = SceneManager.getInstance().getJwtToken();
      if (token != null && !token.isEmpty()) {
        builder.header("Authorization", "Bearer " + token);
      }
    } catch (IllegalStateException e) {
      // SceneManager chГҶВ°a khГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo (vГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ: trong test) ГўвӮ¬вҖқ bГЎВ»ВҸ qua
    }

    return builder;
  }

  /** Serialize object thГғВ nh HttpRequest.BodyPublisher JSON. NГЎВәВҝu body null ГўвҖ вҖҷ body rГЎВ»вҖ”ng. */
  private static HttpRequest.BodyPublisher toBody(Object body) {
    if (body == null) {
      return HttpRequest.BodyPublishers.noBody();
    }
    try {
      String json = MAPPER.writeValueAsString(body);
      return HttpRequest.BodyPublishers.ofString(json);
    } catch (Exception e) {
      throw new RuntimeException("LГЎВ»вҖ”i serialize request body: " + e.getMessage(), e);
    }
  }

  /** GГЎВ»Вӯi request vГғВ  trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ response, throw RuntimeException nГЎВәВҝu thГЎВәВҘt bГЎВәВЎi. */
  private static HttpResponse<String> send(HttpRequest request) {
    try {
      LOGGER.debug("ГўвҖ вҖҷ {} {}", request.method(), request.uri());
      HttpResponse<String> response =
          HTTP_CLIENT.send(request, HttpResponse.BodyHandlers.ofString());
      LOGGER.debug("ГўвҖ Вҗ {} {}", response.statusCode(), request.uri());
      return response;
    } catch (Exception e) {
      LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i gГЎВ»Вӯi HTTP request: {}", e.getMessage());
      throw new RuntimeException("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn server: " + e.getMessage(), e);
    }
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\util\UserBalanceWatcher.java ==========
package com.auction.util;

import com.auction.dto.BidUpdateMessage;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.JavaTimeModule;
import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.util.function.BiConsumer;
import javafx.application.Platform;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * Singleton quГЎВәВЈn lГғВҪ kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi WebSocket kГғВӘnh riГғВӘng cГЎВ»В§a user ({@code /ws/user/{id}}).
 *
 * <p>MГЎВ»Её kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi sau khi Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp thГғВ nh cГғВҙng vГғВ  giГЎВ»ВҜ trong suГЎВ»вҖҳt phiГғВӘn lГғВ m viГЎВ»вҖЎc. Khi Admin duyГЎВ»вҖЎt hoГЎВәВ·c
 * tГЎВ»В« chГЎВ»вҖҳi yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn, server gГЎВ»Вӯi message {@code BALANCE_UPDATED} qua kГғВӘnh nГғВ y.
 *
 * <p>CГғВЎc mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh muГЎВ»вҖҳn nhГЎВәВӯn thГғВҙng bГғВЎo Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ callback qua {@link #setOnBalanceUpdate(BiConsumer)}.
 * ChГЎВ»вҖ° cГғВі mГЎВ»в„ўt listener tГЎВәВЎi mГЎВ»в„ўt thГЎВ»Вқi Г„вҖҳiГЎВ»Ж’m ГўвӮ¬вҖқ mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh nГғВ o Г„вҖҳang hiГЎВ»Ж’n thГЎВ»вҖ№ thГғВ¬ Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ, khi rГЎВ»Вқi Г„вҖҳi thГғВ¬
 * hГЎВ»В§y bГЎВәВұng cГғВЎch truyГЎВ»ВҒn {@code null}.
 */
public class UserBalanceWatcher {

  private static final UserBalanceWatcher INSTANCE = new UserBalanceWatcher();
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(UserBalanceWatcher.class);
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER =
      new ObjectMapper().registerModule(new JavaTimeModule());

  private final WebSocketClient wsClient = new WebSocketClient();

  /** Callback nhГЎВәВӯn (newBalance, approved) ГўвӮ¬вҖқ chГЎВәВЎy trГғВӘn FX thread. */
  private volatile BiConsumer<BigDecimal, Boolean> onBalanceUpdate;

  private UserBalanceWatcher() {}

  public static UserBalanceWatcher getInstance() {
    return INSTANCE;
  }

  /**
   * MГЎВ»Её kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi WebSocket user ГўвӮ¬вҖқ gГЎВ»ВҚi ngay sau khi Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp thГғВ nh cГғВҙng.
   *
   * @param userId ID user hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi
   * @param token JWT token
   */
  public void connect(Long userId, String token) {
    wsClient.connectUser(
        userId,
        token,
        json -> {
          try {
            BidUpdateMessage msg = MAPPER.readValue(json, BidUpdateMessage.class);
            if (BidUpdateMessage.TYPE_BALANCE_UPDATED.equals(msg.getType())) {
              boolean approved = msg.isAutoBid(); // field autoBid tГғВЎi dГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ chГЎВ»В©a approved
              BigDecimal newBalance = msg.getNewBalance();
              LOGGER.info("NhГЎВәВӯn BALANCE_UPDATED: approved={}, newBalance={}", approved, newBalance);

              // LuГғВҙn thГғВӘm vГғВ o NotificationStore dГғВ№ mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh nГғВ o Г„вҖҳang hiГЎВ»Ж’n thГЎВ»вҖ№
              Platform.runLater(
                  () -> {
                    String text =
                        approved
                            ? "ГўЕ“вҖҰ YГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc duyГЎВ»вҖЎt"
                            : "ГўВқЕ’ YГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn bГЎВ»вҖ№ tГЎВ»В« chГЎВ»вҖҳi";
                    NotificationStore.getInstance().add(text);

                    // Notify listener nГЎВәВҝu cГғВі (vГғВӯ dГЎВ»ВҘ ProfileController Г„вҖҳang mГЎВ»Её)
                    BiConsumer<BigDecimal, Boolean> cb = onBalanceUpdate;
                    if (cb != null) {
                      cb.accept(newBalance, approved);
                    }
                  });
            }
          } catch (Exception e) {
            LOGGER.debug("UserBalanceWatcher parse error: {}", e.getMessage());
          }
        });
    LOGGER.info("UserBalanceWatcher: kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi kГғВӘnh user #{}", userId);
  }

  /**
   * Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ callback nhГЎВәВӯn thГғВҙng bГғВЎo biГЎВәВҝn Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng sГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ°.
   *
   * @param callback hГғВ m nhГЎВәВӯn (newBalance, approved), chГЎВәВЎy trГғВӘn FX thread. TruyГЎВ»ВҒn {@code null} Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’
   *     hГЎВ»В§y Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ.
   */
  public void setOnBalanceUpdate(BiConsumer<BigDecimal, Boolean> callback) {
    this.onBalanceUpdate = callback;
  }

  /** Г„ВҗГғВіng kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi ГўвӮ¬вҖқ gГЎВ»ВҚi khi ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng xuГЎВәВҘt. */
  public void disconnect() {
    onBalanceUpdate = null;
    wsClient.disconnect();
    LOGGER.info("UserBalanceWatcher: Г„вҖҳГғВЈ ngГЎВәВҜt kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi.");
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\util\WebSocketClient.java ==========
package com.auction.util;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.JavaTimeModule;
import java.net.URI;
import java.net.http.HttpClient;
import java.net.http.WebSocket;
import java.util.concurrent.CompletionStage;
import java.util.concurrent.Executors;
import java.util.concurrent.ScheduledExecutorService;
import java.util.concurrent.ScheduledFuture;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * Client WebSocket cho ГЎВ»В©ng dГЎВ»ВҘng JavaFX ГўвӮ¬вҖқ nhГЎВәВӯn realtime updates tГЎВ»В« server Javalin.
 *
 * <p>HГЎВ»вҖ” trГЎВ»ВЈ tГЎВ»Вұ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng reconnect vГЎВ»вҖәi exponential backoff khi mГЎВәВҘt kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi (tГЎВ»вҖҳi Г„вҖҳa {@value #MAX_RETRIES}
 * lГЎВәВ§n thГЎВ»Вӯ lГЎВәВЎi).
 */
public class WebSocketClient {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(WebSocketClient.class);
  private static final String WS_BASE_URL = "ws://localhost:8080/ws/auction/";
  private static final String WS_USER_BASE_URL = "ws://localhost:8080/ws/user/";
  private static final int MAX_RETRIES = 5;

  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER =
      new ObjectMapper().registerModule(new JavaTimeModule());

  private WebSocket webSocket;
  private Long currentAuctionId;
  private String currentToken;
  private Consumer<String> currentOnMessage;
  private int retryCount;
  private boolean intentionalClose;
  private ScheduledFuture<?> pendingReconnect;

  private final ScheduledExecutorService scheduler =
      Executors.newSingleThreadScheduledExecutor(
          r -> {
            Thread t = new Thread(r, "ws-reconnect");
            t.setDaemon(true);
            return t;
          });

  /**
   * MГЎВ»Её kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi WebSocket Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn server vГғВ  Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ callback.
   *
   * @param auctionId ID phiГғВӘn Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҘu giГғВЎ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ subscribe
   * @param jwtToken JWT token cho xГғВЎc thГЎВ»Вұc (gГЎВ»Вӯi qua query param)
   * @param onMessage callback nhГЎВәВӯn JSON string khi cГғВі message tГЎВ»В« server
   */
  public void connect(Long auctionId, String jwtToken, Consumer<String> onMessage) {
    cancelPendingReconnect();
    this.currentAuctionId = auctionId;
    this.currentToken = jwtToken;
    this.currentOnMessage = onMessage;
    this.retryCount = 0;
    this.intentionalClose = false;
    doConnect();
  }

  private void doConnect() {
    String uri = WS_BASE_URL + currentAuctionId + "?token=" + currentToken;

    HttpClient.newHttpClient()
        .newWebSocketBuilder()
        .buildAsync(
            URI.create(uri),
            new WebSocket.Listener() {

              @Override
              public void onOpen(WebSocket ws) {
                webSocket = ws;
                retryCount = 0;
                LOGGER.info("WebSocket kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi thГғВ nh cГғВҙng: phiГғВӘn #{}", currentAuctionId);
                ws.request(1);
              }

              @Override
              public CompletionStage<?> onText(WebSocket ws, CharSequence data, boolean last) {
                // Discard messages that arrive after an intentional disconnect to prevent
                // duplicates when a BackgroundBidWatcher connection is starting up in parallel.
                if (!intentionalClose) {
                  String json = data.toString();
                  LOGGER.debug("WS nhГЎВәВӯn message: {}", json);
                  currentOnMessage.accept(json);
                }
                ws.request(1);
                return null;
              }

              @Override
              public CompletionStage<?> onClose(WebSocket ws, int statusCode, String reason) {
                LOGGER.info("WebSocket Г„вҖҳГғВіng kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi: status={}, reason={}", statusCode, reason);
                webSocket = null;
                if (!intentionalClose) {
                  scheduleReconnect();
                }
                return null;
              }

              @Override
              public void onError(WebSocket ws, Throwable error) {
                LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i WebSocket: {}", error.getMessage());
                webSocket = null;
                if (!intentionalClose) {
                  scheduleReconnect();
                }
              }
            })
        .exceptionally(
            e -> {
              LOGGER.error("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi WebSocket: {}", e.getMessage());
              if (!intentionalClose) {
                scheduleReconnect();
              }
              return null;
            });
  }

  private void scheduleReconnect() {
    if (retryCount >= MAX_RETRIES) {
      LOGGER.warn("WebSocket: Г„вҖҳГғВЈ thГЎВ»Вӯ {} lГЎВәВ§n, dГЎВ»В«ng kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi lГЎВәВЎi.", MAX_RETRIES);
      return;
    }
    long delaySec = Math.min(30L, 1L << (retryCount + 1));
    retryCount++;
    LOGGER.info("WebSocket: thГЎВ»Вӯ kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi lГЎВәВЎi lГЎВәВ§n {} sau {}s...", retryCount, delaySec);
    pendingReconnect = scheduler.schedule(this::doConnect, delaySec, TimeUnit.SECONDS);
  }

  private void cancelPendingReconnect() {
    if (pendingReconnect != null && !pendingReconnect.isDone()) {
      pendingReconnect.cancel(false);
      pendingReconnect = null;
    }
  }

  /**
   * MГЎВ»Её kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi WebSocket Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn kГғВӘnh riГғВӘng cГЎВ»В§a user ({@code /ws/user/{id}}) Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ nhГЎВәВӯn thГғВҙng bГғВЎo biГЎВәВҝn
   * Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng sГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ° khi Admin duyГЎВ»вҖЎt hoГЎВәВ·c tГЎВ»В« chГЎВ»вҖҳi yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn.
   *
   * @param userId ID cГЎВ»В§a user hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi (tГЎВ»В« SceneManager)
   * @param jwtToken JWT token Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ xГғВЎc thГЎВ»Вұc
   * @param onMessage callback nhГЎВәВӯn JSON string khi cГғВі message tГЎВ»В« server
   */
  public void connectUser(Long userId, String jwtToken, Consumer<String> onMessage) {
    cancelPendingReconnect();
    this.currentAuctionId = userId; // tГғВЎi dГғВ№ng field Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ lГҶВ°u userId
    this.currentToken = jwtToken;
    this.currentOnMessage = onMessage;
    this.retryCount = 0;
    this.intentionalClose = false;
    doConnectUser();
  }

  private void doConnectUser() {
    String uri = WS_USER_BASE_URL + currentAuctionId + "?token=" + currentToken;

    HttpClient.newHttpClient()
        .newWebSocketBuilder()
        .buildAsync(
            URI.create(uri),
            new WebSocket.Listener() {

              @Override
              public void onOpen(WebSocket ws) {
                webSocket = ws;
                retryCount = 0;
                LOGGER.info("User WebSocket kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi thГғВ nh cГғВҙng: userId=#{}", currentAuctionId);
                ws.request(1);
              }

              @Override
              public CompletionStage<?> onText(WebSocket ws, CharSequence data, boolean last) {
                if (!intentionalClose) {
                  currentOnMessage.accept(data.toString());
                }
                ws.request(1);
                return null;
              }

              @Override
              public CompletionStage<?> onClose(WebSocket ws, int statusCode, String reason) {
                LOGGER.info("User WebSocket Г„вҖҳГғВіng: status={}", statusCode);
                webSocket = null;
                if (!intentionalClose) {
                  scheduleReconnectUser();
                }
                return null;
              }

              @Override
              public void onError(WebSocket ws, Throwable error) {
                LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i User WebSocket: {}", error.getMessage());
                webSocket = null;
                if (!intentionalClose) {
                  scheduleReconnectUser();
                }
              }
            })
        .exceptionally(
            e -> {
              LOGGER.error("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi User WebSocket: {}", e.getMessage());
              if (!intentionalClose) {
                scheduleReconnectUser();
              }
              return null;
            });
  }

  private void scheduleReconnectUser() {
    if (retryCount >= MAX_RETRIES) {
      LOGGER.warn("User WebSocket: Г„вҖҳГғВЈ thГЎВ»Вӯ {} lГЎВәВ§n, dГЎВ»В«ng.", MAX_RETRIES);
      return;
    }
    long delaySec = Math.min(30L, 1L << (retryCount + 1));
    retryCount++;
    pendingReconnect = scheduler.schedule(this::doConnectUser, delaySec, TimeUnit.SECONDS);
  }

  /** Г„ВҗГғВіng kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi WebSocket nГЎВәВҝu Г„вҖҳang mГЎВ»Её. NГғВӘn gГЎВ»ВҚi trong {@code Navigable.onNavigatedFrom()}. */
  public void disconnect() {
    intentionalClose = true;
    cancelPendingReconnect();
    if (webSocket != null && !webSocket.isInputClosed()) {
      webSocket.sendClose(WebSocket.NORMAL_CLOSURE, "Client rГЎВ»Вқi mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh");
      webSocket = null;
      LOGGER.info("WebSocket Г„вҖҳГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГғВіng kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi.");
    }
  }

  /**
   * @return true nГЎВәВҝu Г„вҖҳang kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi vГЎВ»вҖәi server
   */
  public boolean isConnected() {
    return webSocket != null && !webSocket.isInputClosed();
  }
}

package com.auction;

/**
 * Г„ВҗiГЎВ»Ж’m khГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng chГғВӯnh cГЎВ»В§a server Javalin ГўвӮ¬вҖқ Online Auction System.
 *
 * <p>ThГЎВ»В© tГЎВ»Вұ khГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo:
 *
 * <ol>
 *   <li>Jackson ObjectMapper (hГЎВ»вҖ” trГЎВ»ВЈ LocalDateTime, BigDecimal).
 *   <li>Database connection (HikariCP + JDBI).
 *   <li>DAOs ГўвҖ вҖҷ Services ГўвҖ вҖҷ Controllers.
 *   <li>Observer pattern: AuctionEventManager + WebSocketObserver.
 *   <li>AuctionScheduler (OPENГўвҖ вҖҷRUNNINGГўвҖ вҖҷFINISHED transition).
 *   <li>Javalin: Middleware ГўвҖ вҖҷ Exception handlers ГўвҖ вҖҷ Routes ГўвҖ вҖҷ Start.
 * </ol>
 *
 * <p>BiГЎВәВҝn mГғВҙi trГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u (Г„вҖҳГЎВ»ВҚc tГЎВ»В« .env):
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>DB_URL, DB_USER, DB_PASSWORD ГўвӮ¬вҖқ kГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi PostgreSQL.
 *   <li>JWT_SECRET ГўвӮ¬вҖқ khГғВіa kГғВҪ JWT (default: "auction-secret-key-dev").
 * </ul>
 */
public class App {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(App.class);
  private static final int SERVER_PORT = 8080;

  public static void main(String[] args) {
    // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ 1. CГЎВәВҘu hГғВ¬nh Jackson ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГҜВҝВҪГҜВҝВҪГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
    ObjectMapper mapper = new ObjectMapper();
    mapper.registerModule(new JavaTimeModule());
    mapper.disable(SerializationFeature.WRITE_DATES_AS_TIMESTAMPS);

    // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ 2. KhГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo Database ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
    Jdbi jdbi = DatabaseConfig.create();
    LOGGER.info("KГЎВәВҝt nГЎВ»вҖҳi database thГғВ nh cГғВҙng");
    ensureSchemaExists(jdbi);

    // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ 3. KhГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo DAOs ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
    var userDao = new UserDao(jdbi);
    var itemDao = new ItemDao(jdbi);
    var auctionDao = new AuctionDao(jdbi);
    var bidTransactionDao = new BidTransactionDao(jdbi);
    var autoBidConfigDao = new AutoBidConfigDao(jdbi);
    var depositRequestDao = new DepositRequestDao(jdbi);
    var passwordResetRequestDao = new PasswordResetRequestDao(jdbi);

    // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ 3b. Seed tГғВ i khoГЎВәВЈn admin mГЎВәВ·c Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖ№nh ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
    seedAdminIfNeeded(userDao);

    // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ 4. KhГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo Observer (EventManager) ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
    var eventManager = new AuctionEventManager();

    // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ 5. KhГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo WebSocket Handler + Observer integration ГўвҖқвӮ¬
    var wsHandler = new AuctionWebSocketHandler(eventManager);

    // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ 6. KhГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo Services ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
    var userService = new UserService(userDao, depositRequestDao);
    var passwordResetService = new PasswordResetService(userDao, passwordResetRequestDao);
    var itemService = new ItemService(itemDao);
    var auctionService = new AuctionService(auctionDao, itemDao, userDao);
    var bidService =
        new BidService(
            auctionDao,
            bidTransactionDao,
            autoBidConfigDao,
            eventManager,
            jdbi,
            auctionService,
            userDao);

    // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ 7. KhГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo Scheduler (tГЎВ»Вұ chuyГЎВ»Ж’n trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi phiГғВӘn) ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
    var scheduler = new AuctionScheduler(auctionDao, userDao, itemDao, eventManager);
    scheduler.start();

    // Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ shutdown hook Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ dГЎВ»В«ng scheduler khi server tГЎВәВҜt
    Runtime.getRuntime()
        .addShutdownHook(
            new Thread(
                () -> {
                  scheduler.stop();
                  LOGGER.info("Server Г„вҖҳang tГЎВәВҜt...");
                }));

    // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ 8. TГЎВәВЎo Javalin instance ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
    Javalin app =
        Javalin.create(
            config -> {
              config.jsonMapper(new JavalinJackson(mapper, false));
              config.http.defaultContentType = "application/json";
              config.bundledPlugins.enableCors(cors -> cors.addRule(it -> it.anyHost()));
            });

    // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ 9. Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ JWT Middleware ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
    app.before("/api/*", JwtMiddleware::handle);

    // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ 10. Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ Exception Handlers ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
    registerExceptionHandlers(app);

    // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ 11. Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ Routes ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
    app.get("/api/health", ctx -> ctx.json(Map.of("status", "ok")));

    AuthController.register(app, userService);
    AuthController.registerPasswordReset(app, passwordResetService);
    ItemController.register(app, itemService);
    AuctionController.register(app, auctionService);

    // Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ BidController vГЎВ»вҖәi BidService mГЎВ»вҖәi
    var bidController = new BidController(bidService);
    bidController.register(app);

    // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ User profile endpoints ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
    app.get(
        "/api/users/me",
        ctx -> {
          Long userId = ctx.attribute("userId");
          ctx.json(userService.findById(userId));
        });

    app.put(
        "/api/users/me/password",
        ctx -> {
          Long userId = ctx.attribute("userId");
          ChangePasswordRequest req = ctx.bodyAsClass(ChangePasswordRequest.class);
          userService.changePassword(userId, req);
          ctx.status(204);
        });

    // LГЎВ»вҖ№ch sГЎВ»Вӯ yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn cГЎВ»В§a chГғВӯnh user
    app.get(
        "/api/users/me/deposit-requests",
        ctx -> {
          Long userId = ctx.attribute("userId");
          ctx.json(depositRequestDao.findByUserId(userId));
        });

    // Bidder gГЎВ»Вӯi yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u nГЎВәВЎp tiГЎВ»ВҒn ГўвӮ¬вҖқ tГЎВәВЎo PENDING record, chГЎВ»Вқ Admin duyГЎВ»вҖЎt
    app.post(
        "/api/users/me/deposit",
        ctx -> {
          Long userId = ctx.attribute("userId");
          DepositRequest req = ctx.bodyAsClass(DepositRequest.class);
          DepositRecord record = userService.requestDeposit(userId, req.getAmount());
          ctx.status(202).json(record);
        });

    // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ Admin deposit management endpoints ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
    app.get(
        "/api/admin/deposit-requests",
        ctx -> {
          requireAdmin(ctx);
          ctx.json(userService.getPendingDeposits());
        });

    app.post(
        "/api/admin/deposit-requests/{id}/approve",
        ctx -> {
          requireAdmin(ctx);
          Long requestId = Long.parseLong(ctx.pathParam("id"));
          com.auction.dto.UserResponse result = userService.approveDeposit(requestId);
          // Notify user qua WebSocket vГЎВ»ВҒ biГЎВәВҝn Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng sГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ°
          wsHandler.notifyBalanceUpdate(result.getId(), result.getBalance(), true);
          ctx.json(result);
        });

    app.post(
        "/api/admin/deposit-requests/{id}/reject",
        ctx -> {
          requireAdmin(ctx);
          Long requestId = Long.parseLong(ctx.pathParam("id"));
          Long userId = userService.rejectDeposit(requestId);
          // Notify user qua WebSocket rГЎВәВұng yГғВӘu cГЎВәВ§u bГЎВ»вҖ№ tГЎВ»В« chГЎВ»вҖҳi
          wsHandler.notifyBalanceUpdate(userId, null, false);
          ctx.status(204);
        });

    // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ Admin password reset endpoints ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
    app.get(
        "/api/admin/password-reset-requests",
        ctx -> {
          requireAdmin(ctx);
          ctx.json(passwordResetService.getPendingRequests());
        });

    app.post(
        "/api/admin/password-reset-requests/{id}/approve",
        ctx -> {
          requireAdmin(ctx);
          Long requestId = Long.parseLong(ctx.pathParam("id"));
          passwordResetService.approveReset(requestId);
          ctx.status(200).json(Map.of("message", "Г„ВҗГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t lГЎВәВЎi mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u vГЎВ»ВҒ 123456."));
        });

    app.post(
        "/api/admin/password-reset-requests/{id}/reject",
        ctx -> {
          requireAdmin(ctx);
          Long requestId = Long.parseLong(ctx.pathParam("id"));
          passwordResetService.rejectReset(requestId);
          ctx.status(204);
        });

    // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ Admin hard-delete auction endpoint ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
    app.delete(
        "/api/admin/auctions/{id}",
        ctx -> {
          requireAdmin(ctx);
          Long auctionId = Long.parseLong(ctx.pathParam("id"));
          auctionService.hardDelete(auctionId);
          ctx.status(204);
        });

    // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ Admin user management endpoints ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
    app.get(
        "/api/admin/users",
        ctx -> {
          requireAdmin(ctx);
          ctx.json(userService.getAll());
        });

    app.delete(
        "/api/admin/users/{id}",
        ctx -> {
          requireAdmin(ctx);
          Long userId = Long.parseLong(ctx.pathParam("id"));
          userService.delete(userId);
          ctx.status(204);
        });

    // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ Auto-bid endpoints ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
    app.post(
        "/api/auctions/{id}/auto-bid",
        ctx -> {
          String role = ctx.attribute("role");
          if (!"BIDDER".equals(role)) {
            throw new UnauthorizedException("ChГЎВ»вҖ° BIDDER mГЎВ»вҖәi Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc bГЎВәВӯt auto-bid");
          }
          Long auctionId = Long.parseLong(ctx.pathParam("id"));
          Long bidderId = ctx.attribute("userId");
          AutoBidRequest req = ctx.bodyAsClass(AutoBidRequest.class);
          if (req.getMaxBid() == null || req.getIncrement() == null) {
            throw new InvalidBidException("maxBid vГғВ  increment lГғВ  bГЎВәВҜt buГЎВ»в„ўc");
          }
          BigDecimal maxBid = req.getMaxBid();
          BigDecimal increment = req.getIncrement();

          var existing = autoBidConfigDao.findByAuctionAndBidder(auctionId, bidderId);
          if (existing.isPresent()) {
            AutoBidConfig config = existing.get();
            config.setMaxBid(maxBid);
            config.setIncrement(increment);
            config.setActive(true);
            autoBidConfigDao.update(config);
            ctx.status(200).json(config);
          } else {
            AutoBidConfig config = new AutoBidConfig(auctionId, bidderId, maxBid, increment);
            autoBidConfigDao.insert(config);
            ctx.status(201).json(config);
          }
        });

    app.delete(
        "/api/auctions/{id}/auto-bid",
        ctx -> {
          String role = ctx.attribute("role");
          if (!"BIDDER".equals(role)) {
            throw new UnauthorizedException("ChГЎВ»вҖ° BIDDER mГЎВ»вҖәi Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc tГЎВәВҜt auto-bid");
          }
          Long auctionId = Long.parseLong(ctx.pathParam("id"));
          Long bidderId = ctx.attribute("userId");
          autoBidConfigDao
              .findByAuctionAndBidder(auctionId, bidderId)
              .ifPresent(
                  config -> {
                    config.setActive(false);
                    autoBidConfigDao.update(config);
                  });
          ctx.status(204);
        });

    // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ 12. Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ WebSocket ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
    app.ws(
        "/ws/auction/{id}",
        ws -> {
          ws.onConnect(wsHandler::onConnect);
          ws.onClose(wsHandler::onClose);
          ws.onError(wsHandler::onError);
        });

    // KГғВӘnh WebSocket riГғВӘng cho tГЎВ»В«ng user ГўвӮ¬вҖқ nhГЎВәВӯn thГғВҙng bГғВЎo biГЎВәВҝn Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng sГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ°
    app.ws(
        "/ws/user/{id}",
        ws -> {
          ws.onConnect(wsHandler::onUserConnect);
          ws.onClose(wsHandler::onUserClose);
          ws.onError(wsHandler::onUserError);
        });

    // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ 13. KhГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng server ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
    app.start(SERVER_PORT);
    LOGGER.info("Server Г„вҖҳang chГЎВәВЎy tГЎВәВЎi http://localhost:{}", SERVER_PORT);
  }

  /** NГғВ©m UnauthorizedException nГЎВәВҝu request khГғВҙng Г„вҖҳГЎВәВҝn tГЎВ»В« ADMIN. */
  private static void requireAdmin(io.javalin.http.Context ctx) {
    if (!"ADMIN".equals(ctx.attribute("role"))) {
      throw new UnauthorizedException("ChГЎВ»вҖ° ADMIN mГЎВ»вҖәi cГғВі quyГЎВ»ВҒn thГЎВ»Вұc hiГЎВ»вҖЎn thao tГғВЎc nГғВ y");
    }
  }

  /**
   * TГЎВәВЎo hoГЎВәВ·c cГЎВәВӯp nhГЎВәВӯt tГғВ i khoГЎВәВЈn admin mГЎВәВ·c Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖ№nh (admin / 123456) khi server khГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng. Г„ВҗГЎВәВЈm bГЎВәВЈo admin
   * luГғВҙn cГғВі thГЎВ»Ж’ Г„вҖҳГ„Ж’ng nhГЎВәВӯp trong mГғВҙi trГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng dev/test.
   */
  private static void seedAdminIfNeeded(UserDao userDao) {
    try {
      String hash = BCrypt.withDefaults().hashToString(12, "123456".toCharArray());
      var existing = userDao.findByUsername("admin");
      if (existing.isEmpty()) {
        Admin admin = new Admin("admin", hash, "admin@auction.com");
        userDao.insert(admin);
        LOGGER.info("Г„ВҗГғВЈ tГЎВәВЎo tГғВ i khoГЎВәВЈn admin mГЎВәВ·c Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖ№nh: username=admin, password=123456");
      } else {
        existing.get().setPasswordHash(hash);
        userDao.update(existing.get());
        LOGGER.info("Г„ВҗГғВЈ Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖңng bГЎВ»в„ў mГЎВәВӯt khГЎВәВ©u admin: username=admin, password=123456");
      }
    } catch (Exception e) {
      LOGGER.warn("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ seed admin: {}", e.getMessage());
    }
  }

  /**
   * ГғВҒp dГЎВ»ВҘng cГғВЎc migration cГғВІn thiГЎВәВҝu theo kiГЎВ»Ж’u idempotent (IF NOT EXISTS). Thay thГЎВәВҝ cho Flyway vГғВ¬
   * project khГғВҙng cГЎВәВҘu hГғВ¬nh auto-migration. An toГғВ n Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ gГЎВ»ВҚi nhiГЎВ»ВҒu lГЎВәВ§n ГўвӮ¬вҖқ khГғВҙng ГЎВәВЈnh hГҶВ°ГЎВ»Еёng schema Г„вҖҳГғВЈ tГЎВ»вҖңn
   * tГЎВәВЎi.
   */
  private static void ensureSchemaExists(Jdbi jdbi) {
    try {
      jdbi.useHandle(
          handle -> {
            // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ V1: BГЎВәВЈng users (core) ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
            handle.execute(
                """
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                    id            BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
                    username      VARCHAR(50)  UNIQUE NOT NULL,
                    password_hash VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
                    email         VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
                    role          VARCHAR(20)  NOT NULL DEFAULT 'BIDDER'
                                  CHECK (role IN ('BIDDER', 'SELLER', 'ADMIN')),
                    created_at    TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
                    balance       DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0
                )
                """);

            // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ V2: BГЎВәВЈng items ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
            handle.execute(
                """
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS items (
                    id          BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
                    name        VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
                    description TEXT,
                    seller_id   BIGINT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
                    category    VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'ELECTRONICS'
                                CHECK (category IN ('ELECTRONICS', 'ART', 'VEHICLE')),
                    brand       VARCHAR(100),
                    artist      VARCHAR(100),
                    year        INTEGER,
                    created_at  TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
                    updated_at  TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
                )
                """);

            // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ V3: BГЎВәВЈng auctions ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
            handle.execute(
                """
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS auctions (
                    id                BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
                    item_id           BIGINT NOT NULL REFERENCES items(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
                    starting_price    DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,
                    current_price     DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,
                    leading_bidder_id BIGINT REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
                    start_time        TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
                    end_time          TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
                    status            VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'OPEN'
                                      CHECK (status IN ('OPEN', 'RUNNING', 'FINISHED', 'PAID', 'CANCELED')),
                    created_at        TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
                    updated_at        TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
                )
                """);
            handle.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_auctions_status ON auctions(status)");

            // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ V4: BГЎВәВЈng bid_transactions ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
            handle.execute(
                """
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bid_transactions (
                    id          BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
                    auction_id  BIGINT NOT NULL REFERENCES auctions(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
                    bidder_id   BIGINT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
                    amount      DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,
                    auto_bid    BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,
                    created_at  TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
                )
                """);
            handle.execute(
                "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_bid_transactions_auction ON bid_transactions(auction_id)");

            // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ V5: BГЎВәВЈng auto_bid_configs ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
            handle.execute(
                """
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS auto_bid_configs (
                    id          BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
                    auction_id  BIGINT NOT NULL REFERENCES auctions(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
                    bidder_id   BIGINT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
                    max_bid     DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,
                    increment   DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,
                    is_active   BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE,
                    UNIQUE (auction_id, bidder_id)
                )
                """);

            // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ V6: CГЎВ»в„ўt balance (idempotent nГЎВәВҝu bГЎВәВЈng Г„вҖҳГғВЈ tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc) ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
            handle.execute(
                "ALTER TABLE users ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS balance DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0");

            // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ V7: BГЎВәВЈng deposit_requests ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
            handle.execute(
                """
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS deposit_requests (
                    id          BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
                    user_id     BIGINT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
                    amount      DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,
                    status      VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'PENDING'
                                CHECK (status IN ('PENDING', 'APPROVED', 'REJECTED')),
                    created_at  TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
                    reviewed_at TIMESTAMP
                )
                """);
            handle.execute(
                "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_deposit_requests_status ON deposit_requests(status)");

            // ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ V8: BГЎВәВЈng password_reset_requests ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬ГўвҖқвӮ¬
            handle.execute(
                """
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS password_reset_requests (
                    id          BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
                    user_id     BIGINT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
                    status      VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'PENDING'
                                CHECK (status IN ('PENDING', 'APPROVED', 'REJECTED')),
                    created_at  TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
                    reviewed_at TIMESTAMP
                )
                """);
          });
      LOGGER.info("Schema kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra xong ГўвӮ¬вҖқ tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ bГЎВәВЈng tГЎВ»вҖңn tГЎВәВЎi.");
    } catch (Exception e) {
      LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i khi Г„вҖҳГЎВәВЈm bГЎВәВЈo schema: {}", e.getMessage(), e);
    }
  }

  /**
   * Г„ВҗГ„Ж’ng kГғВҪ exception handlers ГўвӮ¬вҖқ ГғВЎnh xГЎВәВЎ custom exception ГўвҖ вҖҷ HTTP status code.
   *
   * <p>BГЎВәВЈng ГғВЎnh xГЎВәВЎ:
   *
   * <pre>
   *   InvalidBidException      ГўвҖ вҖҷ 400 Bad Request
   *   AuctionClosedException   ГўвҖ вҖҷ 400 Bad Request
   *   UnauthorizedException    ГўвҖ вҖҷ 401 Unauthorized
   *   NotFoundException        ГўвҖ вҖҷ 404 Not Found
   *   DuplicateException       ГўвҖ вҖҷ 409 Conflict
   *   Exception (catch-all)    ГўвҖ вҖҷ 500 Internal Server Error
   * </pre>
   */
  private static void registerExceptionHandlers(Javalin app) {
    app.exception(
        IllegalArgumentException.class,
        (e, ctx) -> {
          LOGGER.warn("DГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu khГғВҙng hГЎВ»ВЈp lГЎВ»вҖЎ: {}", e.getMessage());
          ctx.status(400).json(ErrorResponse.of("BAD_REQUEST", e.getMessage()));
        });

    app.exception(
        IllegalStateException.class,
        (e, ctx) -> {
          LOGGER.warn("TrГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi khГғВҙng hГЎВ»ВЈp lГЎВ»вҖЎ: {}", e.getMessage());
          ctx.status(409).json(ErrorResponse.of("INVALID_STATE", e.getMessage()));
        });

    app.exception(
        InvalidBidException.class,
        (e, ctx) -> {
          LOGGER.warn("LГЎВ»вҖ”i Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t giГғВЎ: {}", e.getMessage());
          ctx.status(400).json(ErrorResponse.of("INVALID_BID", e.getMessage()));
        });

    app.exception(
        AuctionClosedException.class,
        (e, ctx) -> {
          LOGGER.warn("LГЎВ»вҖ”i trГЎВәВЎng thГғВЎi phiГғВӘn: {}", e.getMessage());
          ctx.status(400).json(ErrorResponse.of("AUCTION_CLOSED", e.getMessage()));
        });

    app.exception(
        UnauthorizedException.class,
        (e, ctx) -> {
          LOGGER.warn("LГЎВ»вҖ”i xГғВЎc thГЎВ»Вұc: {}", e.getMessage());
          ctx.status(401).json(ErrorResponse.of("UNAUTHORIZED", e.getMessage()));
        });

    app.exception(
        NotFoundException.class,
        (e, ctx) -> {
          LOGGER.warn("KhГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy tГғВ i nguyГғВӘn: {}", e.getMessage());
          ctx.status(404).json(ErrorResponse.of("NOT_FOUND", e.getMessage()));
        });

    app.exception(
        DuplicateException.class,
        (e, ctx) -> {
          LOGGER.warn("Xung Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўt dГЎВ»ВҜ liГЎВ»вҖЎu: {}", e.getMessage());
          ctx.status(409).json(ErrorResponse.of("DUPLICATE", e.getMessage()));
        });

    app.exception(
        Exception.class,
        (e, ctx) -> {
          LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i server khГғВҙng xГғВЎc Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖ№nh", e);
          ctx.status(500)
              .json(ErrorResponse.of("INTERNAL_ERROR", "LГЎВ»вҖ”i hГЎВ»вҖЎ thГЎВ»вҖҳng, vui lГғВІng thГЎВ»Вӯ lГЎВәВЎi sau."));
        });
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\ClientApp.java ==========
package com.auction;

import com.auction.ui.util.SceneManager;
import javafx.application.Application;
import javafx.scene.text.Font;
import javafx.stage.Stage;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * Г„ВҗiГЎВ»Ж’m khГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng ГЎВ»В©ng dГЎВ»ВҘng JavaFX (Client) ГўвӮ¬вҖқ Online Auction System.
 *
 * <p><b>KiГЎВәВҝn trГғВәc Client:</b>
 *
 * <pre>
 *   ClientApp (entry point)
 *     ГўвҖ вҖҷ SceneManager (singleton, quГЎВәВЈn lГғВҪ navigation + session)
 *     ГўвҖ вҖҷ welcome.fxml ГўвҖ вҖҷ login.fxml / register.fxml
 *     ГўвҖ вҖҷ auction-list.fxml (danh sГғВЎch phiГғВӘn)
 *     ГўвҖ вҖҷ auction-detail.fxml (Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t giГғВЎ realtime + chart)
 *     ГўвҖ вҖҷ create-item.fxml, create-auction.fxml (Seller)
 *     ГўвҖ вҖҷ admin-panel.fxml (Admin)
 * </pre>
 *
 * <p><b>CГғВЎch chГЎВәВЎy client:</b>
 *
 * <pre>
 *   ./gradlew runClient
 * </pre>
 *
 * <p><b>LГҶВ°u ГғВҪ:</b> Server phГЎВәВЈi Г„вҖҳang chГЎВәВЎy ({@code ./gradlew run}) trГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc khi khГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng client. Server
 * mГЎВәВ·c Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖ№nh trГғВӘn {@code http://localhost:8080}.
 *
 * <p><b>LiГғВӘn kГЎВәВҝt vГЎВ»вҖәi cГғВЎc file khГғВЎc:</b>
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>{@link SceneManager} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ singleton quГЎВәВЈn lГғВҪ toГғВ n bГЎВ»в„ў mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh vГғВ  session JWT
 *   <li>{@code /resources/fxml/} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ tГЎВәВҘt cГЎВәВЈ file FXML (View trong MVC)
 *   <li>{@code /resources/css/style.css} ГўвӮ¬вҖқ dark theme ГғВЎp dГЎВ»ВҘng cho toГғВ n bГЎВ»в„ў ГЎВ»В©ng dГЎВ»ВҘng
 * </ul>
 */
public class ClientApp extends Application {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ClientApp.class);

  /** ChiГЎВ»ВҒu rГЎВ»в„ўng cГЎВ»Вӯa sГЎВ»вҖў tГЎВ»вҖҳi thiГЎВ»Ж’u */
  private static final double MIN_WIDTH = 1000;

  /** ChiГЎВ»ВҒu cao cГЎВ»Вӯa sГЎВ»вҖў tГЎВ»вҖҳi thiГЎВ»Ж’u */
  private static final double MIN_HEIGHT = 700;

  /**
   * KhГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng giao diГЎВ»вҖЎn JavaFX.
   *
   * <p>ThГЎВ»В© tГЎВ»Вұ khГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo:
   *
   * <ol>
   *   <li>KhГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo SceneManager vГЎВ»вҖәi Stage chГғВӯnh.
   *   <li>CГғВ i Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ·t kГғВӯch thГҶВ°ГЎВ»вҖәc tГЎВ»вҖҳi thiГЎВ»Ж’u cho cГЎВ»Вӯa sГЎВ»вҖў.
   *   <li>HiГЎВ»Ж’n thГЎВ»вҖ№ mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh chГғВ o mГЎВ»В«ng.
   *   <li>Show Stage.
   * </ol>
   *
   * @param primaryStage Stage chГғВӯnh do JavaFX cung cГЎВәВҘp
   */
  @Override
  public void start(Stage primaryStage) {
    try {
      loadFonts();

      // KhГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo SceneManager singleton
      SceneManager sceneManager = SceneManager.init(primaryStage, MIN_WIDTH, MIN_HEIGHT);

      // CГЎВәВҘu hГғВ¬nh Stage
      primaryStage.setTitle("Online Auction System");
      primaryStage.setMinWidth(MIN_WIDTH);
      primaryStage.setMinHeight(MIN_HEIGHT);

      // Load mГғВ n hГғВ¬nh chГғВ o mГЎВ»В«ng Г„вҖҳГЎВәВ§u tiГғВӘn
      sceneManager.navigateTo("welcome.fxml");

      primaryStage.show();
      LOGGER.info("ГЎВ»ВЁng dГЎВ»ВҘng Г„вҖҳГғВЈ khГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng ГўвӮ¬вҖқ {}x{}", MIN_WIDTH, MIN_HEIGHT);

    } catch (Exception e) {
      LOGGER.error("LГЎВ»вҖ”i khГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng ГЎВ»В©ng dГЎВ»ВҘng JavaFX", e);
      throw new RuntimeException("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ khГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng ГЎВ»В©ng dГЎВ»ВҘng", e);
    }
  }

  private static void loadFonts() {
    String[] variants = {
      "Lexend-Thin", "Lexend-ExtraLight", "Lexend-Light",
      "Lexend-Regular", "Lexend-Medium", "Lexend-SemiBold",
      "Lexend-Bold", "Lexend-ExtraBold", "Lexend-Black"
    };
    int loaded = 0;
    for (String variant : variants) {
      String path = "/fonts/" + variant + ".ttf";
      try (var stream = ClientApp.class.getResourceAsStream(path)) {
        if (stream == null) {
          LOGGER.warn("KhГғВҙng tГғВ¬m thГЎВәВҘy font file: {}", path);
          continue;
        }
        Font font = Font.loadFont(stream, 12);
        if (font != null) {
          LOGGER.info("Font loaded: {} ГўвҖ вҖҷ family=\"{}\"", variant, font.getFamily());
          loaded++;
        } else {
          LOGGER.warn("Font.loadFont trГЎВәВЈ vГЎВ»ВҒ null cho: {}", path);
        }
      } catch (Exception e) {
        LOGGER.warn("KhГғВҙng thГЎВ»Ж’ load font {}: {}", path, e.getMessage());
      }
    }
    LOGGER.info("Г„ВҗГғВЈ load {}/{} biГЎВәВҝn thГЎВ»Ж’ font Lexend", loaded, variants.length);

    // Diagnostic: verify which font families JavaFX CSS can actually see
    java.util.List<String> lexendFamilies =
        Font.getFamilies().stream()
            .filter(f -> f.toLowerCase().startsWith("lexend"))
            .collect(java.util.stream.Collectors.toList());
    LOGGER.info("=== Lexend families visible to CSS: {} ===", lexendFamilies);
    for (String fam : lexendFamilies) {
      LOGGER.info("  '{}' ГўвҖ вҖҷ names: {}", fam, Font.getFontNames(fam));
    }
  }

  /**
   * Main method ГўвӮ¬вҖқ entry point cho JVM.
   *
   * <p>JavaFX Application cГЎВәВ§n gГЎВ»ВҚi {@code Application.launch()} Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ khГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng Application Thread
   * (JavaFX Thread). KhГғВҙng gГЎВ»ВҚi {@code new ClientApp().start()} trГЎВ»Вұc tiГЎВәВҝp.
   *
   * @param args tham sГЎВ»вҖҳ dГғВІng lГЎВ»вҖЎnh (khГғВҙng sГЎВ»Вӯ dГЎВ»ВҘng)
   */
  public static void main(String[] args) {
    launch(args);
  }
}


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\java\com\auction\Launcher.java ==========
package com.auction;

/**
 * Launcher ГўвӮ¬вҖқ wrapper bГЎВәВҜt buГЎВ»в„ўc Г„вҖҳГЎВ»Ж’ chГЎВәВЎy JavaFX tГЎВ»В« fat JAR.
 *
 * <p><b>TГЎВәВЎi sao cГЎВәВ§n class nГғВ y?</b>
 *
 * <p>Khi Г„вҖҳГғВіng gГғВіi fat JAR, JVM kiГЎВ»Ж’m tra xem {@code Main-Class} trong {@code MANIFEST.MF} cГғВі extends
 * {@code javafx.application.Application} khГғВҙng. NГЎВәВҝu cГғВі ГўвҖ вҖҷ JVM nГғВ©m lГЎВ»вҖ”i vГғВ¬ JavaFX chГҶВ°a Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc khГЎВ»Еёi tГЎВәВЎo
 * Г„вҖҳГғВәng cГғВЎch trong mГғВҙi trГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng module.
 *
 * <p>GiГЎВәВЈi phГғВЎp chuГЎВәВ©n: dГғВ№ng mГЎВ»в„ўt class trung gian <b>khГғВҙng</b> extends {@code Application} lГғВ m {@code
 * Main-Class}, class nГғВ y gГЎВ»ВҚi {@code ClientApp.main()} ГўвҖ вҖҷ JavaFX khГЎВ»Еёi Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўng bГғВ¬nh thГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқng.
 *
 * <p><b>DГғВ№ng khi:</b> chГЎВәВЎy client Г„вҖҳГЎВ»в„ўc lГЎВәВӯp bГЎВәВұng {@code java -jar auction-client.jar}
 *
 * @see ClientApp
 * @see Main
 */
public class Launcher {

  /**
   * Entry point cho fat JAR client.
   *
   * @param args tham sГЎВ»вҖҳ dГғВІng lГЎВ»вҖЎnh (Г„вҖҳГҶВ°ГЎВ»ВЈc truyГЎВ»ВҒn thГЎВәВіng vГғВ o ClientApp)
   */
  public static void main(String[] args) {
    ClientApp.main(args);
  }
}

/* ================================================================
   FONTS
   Two @font-face rules ГўвӮ¬вҖқ one per actual CSS weight used in this file
   (normal and bold). Numeric weights 100-900 are NOT used here because
   JavaFX CSS does not implement the full @font-face font-weight matching
   algorithm: when multiple @font-face rules share the same font-family,
   only the LAST one is retained, so declaring 9 numeric-weight variants
   would silently replace all of them with the final entry (Lexend-Black).
   Using keyword values lets JavaFX correctly select the right file via
   the standard "normal vs bold" style matching it does support.
   ================================================================ */

@font-face {
    font-family: 'Lexend';
    src: url('../fonts/Lexend-Regular.ttf');
    font-weight: normal;
}

@font-face {
    font-family: 'Lexend';
    src: url('../fonts/Lexend-Bold.ttf');
    font-weight: bold;
}

// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\resources\db\migration\V1__initial_schema.sql ==========
-- V1: Initial schema for auction system (UPDATED - khГЎВ»вҖәp vГЎВ»вҖәi DAO hiГЎВ»вҖЎn tГЎВәВЎi)

CREATE TABLE users (
    id              BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    username        VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    password_hash   VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    email           VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    role            VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL CHECK (role IN ('BIDDER', 'SELLER', 'ADMIN')),
    created_at      TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE TABLE items (
    id              BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    seller_id       BIGINT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),
    name            VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    description     TEXT,
    category        VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL CHECK (category IN ('ELECTRONICS', 'ART', 'VEHICLE')),
    brand           VARCHAR(100),
    artist          VARCHAR(100),
    year            INTEGER,
    created_at      TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at      TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE TABLE auctions (
    id                  BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    item_id             BIGINT NOT NULL REFERENCES items(id),
    starting_price      DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,
    current_price       DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,
    leading_bidder_id   BIGINT REFERENCES users(id),
    start_time          TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    end_time            TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    status              VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'OPEN'
                        CHECK (status IN ('OPEN', 'RUNNING', 'FINISHED', 'PAID', 'CANCELED')),
    created_at          TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at          TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE TABLE bid_transactions (
    id              BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    auction_id      BIGINT NOT NULL REFERENCES auctions(id),
    bidder_id       BIGINT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),
    amount          DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,
    auto_bid        BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,
    created_at      TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE TABLE auto_bid_configs (
    id                  BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    auction_id          BIGINT NOT NULL REFERENCES auctions(id),
    bidder_id           BIGINT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),
    max_bid             DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,
    increment_amount    DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,
    active              BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE,
    registered_at       TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    UNIQUE (auction_id, bidder_id)
);

-- Indexes for common queries
CREATE INDEX idx_auctions_status ON auctions(status);
CREATE INDEX idx_bid_transactions_auction ON bid_transactions(auction_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_items_seller ON items(seller_id);

// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\resources\db\migration\V2__seed_admin.sql ==========
-- V2: Seed tГғВ i khoГЎВәВЈn admin mГЎВәВ·c Г„вҖҳГЎВ»вҖ№nh
-- Username: admin | Password: 123456

INSERT INTO users (username, password_hash, email, role, created_at)

// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\resources\db\migration\V3__add_balance.sql ==========
-- V3: ThГғВӘm cГЎВ»в„ўt balance (sГЎВ»вҖҳ dГҶВ° tГғВ i khoГЎВәВЈn) cho ngГҶВ°ГЎВ»Вқi dГғВ№ng
ALTER TABLE users ADD COLUMN balance DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0;


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\resources\db\migration\V4__deposit_requests.sql ==========
CREATE TABLE deposit_requests (
    id          BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id     BIGINT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    amount      DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,
    status      VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'PENDING'
                CHECK (status IN ('PENDING', 'APPROVED', 'REJECTED')),
    created_at  TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    reviewed_at TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE INDEX idx_deposit_requests_status ON deposit_requests(status);


// ========== D:\Programming\Java\oop-course-project-uet\src\main\resources\db\migration\V5__password_reset_requests.sql ==========
CREATE TABLE password_reset_requests (
    id          BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id     BIGINT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    status      VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'PENDING'
                CHECK (status IN ('PENDING', 'APPROVED', 'REJECTED')),
    created_at  TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    reviewed_at TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE INDEX idx_password_reset_requests_status ON password_reset_requests(status);
CREATE INDEX idx_password_reset_requests_user   ON password_reset_requests(user_id);
